- Auto-deploy internals: `lib/media/cloudflare-deploy.ts` (Cloudflare API client: `resolveAccountId` via `GET /accounts`, `uploadWorker` PUT multipart `main_module` + `secret_text` bindings, `enableWorkerUrl` claims/enables the `workers.dev` subdomain; auth = Bearer token OR `X-Auth-Email`/`X-Auth-Key`). Worker script uploaded is `cactus-media-worker`, compat date `2024-01-01`. Worker source is transpiled from `workers/media-worker/index.ts` to `lib/media/worker-source.generated.ts` (string export `MEDIA_WORKER_SOURCE`) by `scripts/generate-media-worker.mjs` (uses the `typescript` devDep; single-file type-strip, zero imports), run in `dev`/`build`, git-ignored via `.git/info/exclude`. Route `app/api/admin/media/deploy-worker/route.ts` (isAdmin, `maxDuration 60`) sources each `WORKER_SECRET_KEYS[provider]` value **and** the CF credential/account id from the request body (freshly-typed), then `getVercelEnvValues` (the project's saved values), then `process.env`; derives `ALLOWED_ORIGIN` from `SITE_URL`, deploys, then persists the CF creds (two sensitive) + URL via `upsertVercelEnvVars` + `recordDeploymentNeeded`. `CLOUDFLARE_API_TOKEN`/`CLOUDFLARE_GLOBAL_API_KEY` added to `SENSITIVE_KEYS` (`lib/vercel/env.ts`); all four CF keys added to `ALLOWED_KEYS` (`app/api/admin/env/route.ts`).
- `getVercelEnvValues(token, projectId, keys, target='production')` (`lib/vercel/env.ts`) reads values back off the project via `GET /v10/projects/{id}/env?decrypt=true`, for code that needs a value saved *after* the running deployment was built. **Vercel only decrypts `plain` vars: anything in `SENSITIVE_KEYS` comes back as an empty string** and maps to `null` ("set, but unreadable - only a redeploy can supply it"); keys absent from the result aren't set at all. The deploy-worker route uses that distinction to split its 400 into "never entered → enter and save it above" vs "saved write-only + site not redeployed since → redeploy from the Status tab".
- `uploadWorker` special-cases Cloudflare error **10000** ("Authentication error"): listing accounts needs far less permission than writing a script, so a credential that clears `resolveAccountId` can still be refused here. The thrown message names `CLOUDFLARE_WORKERS_EDIT_PERMISSION` (`lib/media/providers.ts`, also first entry of `CLOUDFLARE_TOKEN_PERMISSIONS`) and the account id rather than parroting Cloudflare's two words.

Upload path (`lib/media/upload.ts`): 10 MB cap; JPEG/PNG/WebP/GIF only; sharp decodes the bytes and rejects content/type mismatches. S3-compatible providers use `@aws-sdk/client-s3` with per-provider endpoints; Vercel Blob via `@vercel/blob`; Supabase via `@supabase/storage-js`; Cloudinary/ImageKit via their SDKs (key = public_id / fileId). Object keys: `media/<PROVIDER>/<folderPath>/<nanoid>-<filename>.<ext>` (legacy B2 keys have no provider segment). `uploadMedia`/`relocateMediaBlob`/`buildKey` take an opt-in `exactName` flag: when set, the sanitised filename becomes the key basename verbatim with **no nanoid** (`…/<folderPath>/<name>.<ext>`) - the caller owns uniqueness within the folder. Used by the Shop's product-image filing (see Shop module) so image urls read `shop/<category>/<product>/<slug><n>.<ext>`; `moveOrRenameMedia` forwards the same flag. **Basename clipping lives in the pure, unit-tested `lib/media/keys.ts` (`exactBaseName`, `nanoidLabel`, `MAX_EXACT_BASENAME=120`) - the two key forms carry uniqueness differently and must NOT share a clip rule.** A nanoid-form label is decoration and is clipped to 40 chars; an exact name is the only unique thing in the key, so it is kept whole to 120 chars and, past that, becomes `<prefix>-<sha256[0:10]>` (deterministic, so re-filing stays a no-op). Both forms previously shared one 40-char clip, which silently truncated `<product-slug><n>` to a common stub: every image of a long-named product **and every variant image filed beside it collapsed onto ONE key**, so storage overwrote blob with blob while each `Media` row kept its own id/url - surfacing as media-library previews that didn't match the image served, and images replacing each other (live case: a 51-char product slug, 2026-07-16). `moveOrRenameMedia` additionally refuses to delete a blob whose key equals the one it just wrote (both for the replaced `victim` and for the original), so a key clash can never delete the image that is now live. `organise.ts` also exports `getOrCreateFolderByPath(names[])` - walks/creates a folder chain by display name and returns the leaf folder id (idempotent), for auto-filing items into a known tree.

Cloudflare Worker (`workers/media-worker/index.ts`, excluded from tsconfig, deployed separately via wrangler): GET-only; validates `media/…` keys; infers the provider from the key path (unknown segment = legacy B2); fetches from the matching backend (SigV4-signs S3-compatible requests itself; Vercel Blob via BLOB_BASE_URL; Supabase via service-role REST); passes `?w=&q=` through Cloudflare Image Resizing options; responds with 1-year immutable cache headers and `Access-Control-Allow-Origin: ALLOWED_ORIGIN`.

URL construction/resolution: proxied rows store `<CLOUDFLARE_WORKER_URL>/<key>` as the canonical URL; direct rows store the provider CDN URL. The custom Next image loader (`lib/media/loader.ts`, wired via `next.config.ts images.loaderFile`) branches on hostname: Cloudinary gets `/upload/w_<w>,q_<q>/` inserted, ImageKit gets `?tr=w-…,q-…`, everything else gets `?w=&q=` appended for the Worker.

Migration (`lib/media/migration.ts`): one `MediaMigrationJob` at a time; 15-item batches; per item download original bytes → upload to destination → single-row provider/key/url update → best-effort delete of the original; failed items recorded and skipped by later batches; retry clears the failed list. Batches run only while an admin keeps the Settings → Media screen open (client loop), never via cron.

In-use computation (`lib/media/references.ts`): `loadMediaUsageIndex()` gathers, in one pass, every `Media.id` held in a FK column (`SiteConfig.logo/logoDark/favicon/faviconDark`, `InfoPage.ogImageId`, `Member.avatarMediaId`, `MemberDataExportRequest.mediaId`) plus a lowercased `haystack` of all Puck builder JSON (`InfoPage.builderData` + `publishedData`, `Layout.builderData`). `isMediaInUse(media, index)` returns true if the id is in the FK set OR the item's `url`/`key`/`id` appears in the haystack (Puck blocks embed media by url via bgImage/imageUrl/mediaUrl, or by id via ImageBlock/Card mediaId - stored in content, not as a relation). `getInUseMediaIds(rows)` classifies a batch. Consumed by the media library tabs and by `getMediaReferences` (`lib/media/upload.ts`) for delete warnings.

`saveMediaRecord`'s `uploadedById` is now optional (was required) - Member-uploaded avatars (MEMBERS_SPEC.md) have no valid value for it, since that column is a FK to the core `User` table and a `Member` is an entirely separate one.

Member avatars (Phase 4 of MEMBERS_SPEC.md, `Member.avatarChoice`): UPLOAD goes through the ordinary media pipeline above; GRAVATAR is served by `GET /api/members/avatar-proxy/[id]` - the server computes `sha256(email)` and streams the Gravatar bytes through this origin (24h cache) rather than redirecting to gravatar.com, so no CSP `img-src` addition is needed and the email/hash never reaches the client; GENERATED renders `components/members/GeneratedAvatar.tsx`, an inline SVG of the member's initials using `--color-bg-subtle`/`--color-border`/`--color-primary` (a single tone, not a per-user hue palette, to stay hardcoded-hex-free without inventing an avatar-specific colour list). `components/members/MemberAvatar.tsx` is the single dispatcher between the three, falling back to the generated avatar client-side if the Gravatar proxy 404s. Phase 9: `lib/members/avatar.ts`'s `resolveEffectiveAvatarChoice` downgrades a member's stored choice to whatever `avatarUploadsEnabled`/`gravatarEnabled` still permit, applied at every read (profile page, directory, account API, `MembersProfile` Puck block) and re-checked server-side in the avatar-proxy route itself.

Provider selection control: `SiteConfig.mediaProvider` (admin Settings → Media, persisted immediately); `isMediaProviderConfigured` requires every env var in `envKeysForProvider(provider)` (proxied providers include CLOUDFLARE_WORKER_URL). Uploads are refused until both hold.

### Email

- Provider chain (`lib/email/index.ts`): Brevo HTTP API when `BREVO_API_KEY` is set, else nodemailer SMTP (`SMTP_HOST/PORT/USER/PASS`); throws when neither is configured. From name/address come from `SiteConfig.emailFromName/emailFromAddress` (fallbacks: siteName / `noreply@example.com`). `SiteConfig.emailProvider` exists as a column but the chain is decided purely by env-var presence. `sendTestEmailWithCredentials(to, siteName, creds)` sends the standard test email through caller-supplied Brevo/SMTP credentials (unsaved form values; blank fields fall back to env) - used by the settings-page per-card "Send test email" button that appears next to "Save credentials" once new values are typed.
- Notification types sent by core (admin/User side): login OTP (password login), email verification code (registration), recovery link (recovery request), recovery-requested notice (same trigger), recovery-completed notice (recovery completion), password-changed notice (password add/change) - all plain `sendEmail` calls, no template override system.
- Module emails (contact-form): submission notification to the configured/admin address ("full" content or "notify"-only modes, optional CCs, reply-to submitter), auto-reply to the submitter (markdown with `{{name}}`/`{{email}}` placeholders), admin reply email (markdown + signature, reply-to the site address).
- In-app admin notifications (not email) live in the Notification table: "Changes awaiting deployment" (rolling, reasons deduped by label), `core-update`, `module-update:{id}`, `contact-form:messages` (rolling unread count); Members system re-uses the generic `message` type for pending-approval/deletion admin alerts (`lib/members/admin-notify.ts`, `upsertAlert` dedupe) - see below, it has no dedicated type of its own.

Members system emails (`lib/email/templates.ts`, admin-editable - see Phase 6 of MEMBERS_SPEC.md): 11 `member.*` templates, each with a code default and an optional `EmailTemplate` DB override (absence = default; reset = delete the row). Transactional ones (verify-email, magic-link, deletion-requested, deletion-cancelled, deletion-admin-notify, security-alert) always send; the rest (welcome, suspended, approved, digest-daily, digest-weekly) would check `MemberNotificationPreference` if the caller supplied a matching category, but core has no non-transactional categories of its own yet. `renderEmailTemplate(key, vars)` does `{{tag}}` interpolation (HTML-escaped in the body, plain in the subject); `sendMemberEmail(member, key, vars, opts?)` renders + sends via the ordinary `sendEmail`. Digests: `lib/members/digest.ts`'s `runDigest('DAILY'|'WEEKLY')` batches each member's subscribed-category `MemberActivityEvent` rows (by `type`) from the last 24h/7d into one email, cron-driven (`GET /api/cron/members/digest?mode=daily|weekly`, `CRON_SECRET`-gated).

### Scripts

- `scripts/migrate-sitelogo-cell-height.mjs` - one-off data migration + read-only audit for the SiteLogo "Element height" rename (`logoHeight`/`logoHeightShrunk` → `cellHeight`/`cellHeightShrunk`). Recursively walks `Layout` (type='header') `builderData`/`publishedData` and `SavedBlock` (componentType SiteLogo/Grid/Group) Puck blobs, remapping SiteLogo keys 1:1; also reports header true-centering coverage (centre-aligned Grid columns, 3-item space-distributed Groups). DRY RUN by default (reads, reports, writes nothing); `--apply` persists. Reads `DATABASE_URL` from `.env`. Not part of any build step; the render fallback makes it non-load-bearing.
- `scripts/migrate-grid-columns-split.mjs` - one-off data migration for the Grid component split (the single dynamic "Grid" Columns-select block replaced by fixed-column variants). Rewrites the affected Puck blocks across `Layout`/`InfoPage`/`SavedBlock` blobs. Reads `DATABASE_URL`; not part of any build step. Same non-load-bearing one-off shape as `migrate-sitelogo-cell-height.mjs`.
- `scripts/prebuild.mjs` - the single prebuild entry point for `npm run build` (`node scripts/prebuild.mjs && next build`). Replaces the old serial `&&` chain, whose real dependency graph is a fan-out rather than a line: `checkout-modules` must land module code on disk first (a barrier - everything downstream reads `/modules`), after which three branches run **concurrently** because none reads another's inputs or outputs - (a) `prisma generate`, (b) the database chain `build-migrate` → `sync-module-manifests`, (c) `generate-all`. `prisma generate` does not need the database, the migration chain does not need a generated client, and the generators need neither, so the prebuild costs the slowest branch rather than the sum. Each branch's output is buffered and flushed as one labelled block on completion (concurrent logs cannot interleave); any non-zero exit aborts the build with that branch's status, exactly as `&&` did. Also sets `CHECKPOINT_DISABLE=1` and `PRISMA_HIDE_UPDATE_MESSAGE=true` for every child, killing the Prisma CLI's version-check network round trip and its unactionable "update available" banner.
- `scripts/build-migrate.mjs` - conditional migration runner for Vercel builds. Skips entirely without DATABASE_URL; swaps Neon pooler URL for the direct endpoint (or DIRECT_URL); sets `PRISMA_SCHEMA_DISABLE_ADVISORY_LOCK=1` (plus `CHECKPOINT_DISABLE`/`PRISMA_HIDE_UPDATE_MESSAGE`, set here as well as in `prebuild.mjs` so a direct invocation behaves the same); runs `prisma migrate deploy`, then `reconcile-core-schema.mjs`, then `run-module-migrations.mjs`, each with 3 retries and backoff. Invokes the Prisma CLI through `node_modules/.bin/prisma` (falling back to `npx` only if that binary is absent) - `npx` re-runs npm's package resolution on every call for no gain. `migrate resolve --rolled-back` (which clears a failed-migration record left by an interrupted earlier apply, e.g. a Neon cold-start disconnect, that would otherwise block every later attempt with P3009) runs only **before a retry**, not before the first attempt: a stale failed record makes attempt 1 fail fast with P3009, the resolve then runs and attempt 2 applies cleanly, so recovery is unchanged while the happy path no longer pays a full Prisma CLI boot plus a DB round trip on every single build.
- `scripts/reconcile-core-schema.mjs` - build-step-only runner that closes core-schema drift on existing installs. The single core migration is edited in place and `prisma migrate deploy` never re-applies it, so additive changes made after an install was provisioned never reach its database. This runner applies every **unapplied** `.sql` in `prisma/core-reconcile/` (lexicographic) via a direct `pg` client (same SSL/direct-endpoint handling as `run-module-migrations.mjs`/`build-migrate.mjs`). Applied files are recorded, with their sha256, in the existing `ModuleMigration` ledger under the reserved module name `__core__` - deliberately not a new runner-owned table, which would show up in backups taken from one install and not another. Previously every file re-ran on **every** deploy for a guaranteed no-op; that list only grows, and each entry cost a statement batch and a database round trip per build. A file whose contents change is re-applied (checksum mismatch), so the self-heal guarantee is intact; an install predating the ledger simply applies each file once (a no-op on an up-to-date database) and records it. Each file is additive and idempotent (`IF NOT EXISTS` / `pg_constraint`-guarded FKs / `ADD VALUE IF NOT EXISTS`), so it is a no-op on fresh or up-to-date installs and adds only the missing objects on a drifted one. Skips without DATABASE_URL; 3 retries with backoff. Files: `001_media_folders_tags.sql` (Folder/Tag/MediaTag tables + `Media.originalName`/`folderId`/`optimised` columns and their indexes/FKs - the `/hq/media` crash on the deskwell install, 2026-07-11), `002_member_twofactor_phone.sql` (`MemberTwoFactor.phoneEncrypted`), `003_twofactor_sms_enum.sql` (adds `SMS` to the `TwoFactorMethod` enum - kept as the only statement in its own file because `ALTER TYPE ... ADD VALUE` cannot share a multi-statement transaction batch on older Postgres), `004_perf_indexes.sql` (the `Layout`/`Module.status` indexes, and drops three plain indexes duplicating a `@unique`), `005_retire_starter_layouts.sql` (deletes the legacy starter rows, *then* drops `Layout.isStarter` and its index - in that order), `006_module_layouts_seeded.sql` (`Module.layoutsSeededAt`, backfilled to `installedAt` for `active`/`inactive`/`update_available` modules only - one still mid-install or `failed` has never had its code in a build, so it stays NULL and is seeded when its deploy lands), `007_admin_menu_config.sql` (adds the nullable `SiteConfig.adminMenuConfig` jsonb for the admin-sidebar customisation; null = built-in defaults, so existing installs need no backfill), `008_menu_item_visibility.sql` (guarded `CREATE TYPE "MenuItemVisibility"` + `ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS "MenuItem"."visibility"` defaulting PUBLIC, so every existing menu item keeps rendering to everyone with no backfill), `009_reseed_unseeded_module_layouts.sql` (clears `Module.layoutsSeededAt` on rows that provably never seeded, so `seedPendingModuleLayouts()` re-seeds them on the next request - see the Layout system section; the proof is `layoutsSeededAt < MIN(ModuleMigration.appliedAt)` for that module, i.e. the stamp predates the first moment the module's code was ever in a build, since the ledger rows are written by the build step with the code present. Nothing is cleared for a module seeded after its code landed - those either have their layouts or the owner deleted them, and re-minting deleted layouts is what the stamp exists to prevent. A module with no migration rows at all is left alone: nothing to prove it against, and none of them declare layout types).
- `scripts/checkout-modules.mjs` - clones every `modules.json` entry into `/modules`, pinned to the recorded `version` tag (`git clone --depth=1 --branch`). On Vercel always a fresh clone; locally tries `git checkout HEAD -- .` in the existing clone first (this reverts uncommitted local edits to tracked module files). Modules are handled **in parallel** (each writes only its own directory and reads no other's, so the clones were never actually dependent - just serialised by the loop); each module's log lines are buffered and flushed as one block on completion so concurrent git output cannot interleave.
- `scripts/generate-all.mjs` - the single entry point `npm run dev` and `npm run build` use to run all eight generators below (router, puck, cron, settings-tabs, sms-providers, extension-points, layout-types, media-worker), in that order, in **one** Node process via sequential `await import()`. They were previously eight `&&`-chained `node scripts/generate-module-*.mjs` invocations, i.e. eight Node boots (one of them loading the whole TypeScript compiler for `generate-media-worker`) for a few hundred milliseconds of real work. Semantics are identical: same generators, same order, and a generator that calls `process.exit(1)` on a bad manifest (the duplicate-`publicBasePath` check in `generate-module-router.mjs`) still aborts the build. Add new generators to the END of the list, not the middle.
- `scripts/generate-module-router.mjs` - scans `modules/*/app/api/**/route.ts` and `modules/*/app/cactus-admin/<name>/**/page.tsx`; writes the gitignored `lib/modules/router.ts` (API dispatch table + lazy page loaders). For any module declaring `publicBasePath` in its manifest, also scans `modules/<name>/app/public/<base>/**/{page.tsx,route.ts}` and emits `resolveModulePublicPage`, `dispatchModulePublicRoute`, `getModulePublicBases`, and (if `modules/<name>/lib/sitemap.ts` exists, exporting `getPublicSitemapEntries(siteUrl)`) wires it into `collectModuleSitemapEntries`; fails the build if two modules declare the same `publicBasePath`. Same pattern for robots: if `modules/<name>/lib/robots.ts` exists, exporting `getPublicRobotsDisallow(): Promise<string[]>`, it's wired into `collectModuleRobotsDisallow()` (called from `app/robots.ts`, merged into the `disallow` list alongside the fixed `/cactus-admin/`, `/setup/`, `/cactus-status/`, `/api/` entries). Shop's `modules/shop/lib/robots.ts` returns `['/shop']` when `shopStatus === 'CLOSED'`; `modules/shop/lib/sitemap.ts`'s `getPublicSitemapEntries` returns `[]` for the same state, so a closed shop drops out of both the sitemap and gets disallowed in robots.txt. Runs on every dev start and build. **Route ordering:** every emitted route table (`API_ROUTES`, `PUBLIC_ROUTE_HANDLERS`) and page-loader key set (`PAGE_LOADERS`, `PUBLIC_PAGE_LOADERS`) is sorted **literal-first per segment** by `comparePatternSegments`/`sortRoutesBySpecificity`/`sortPatternKeys` - at the first differing segment a literal beats a dynamic `[param]`. This matters because dispatch (`dispatchModuleApi`) is first-match-wins and `matchPattern` treats `[param]` as a wildcard, so without the sort a raw file-order `[id]` would shadow a sibling literal like `reorder`/`check-slug` (they start with `[` = 0x5B, which sorts ahead of letters), routing `…/categories/reorder` to the `[id]` handler with id="reorder" (405, no POST). Add new route tables through these sorters.
- `scripts/generate-module-puck.mjs` - collects `puckBlocks` from every module manifest; writes two gitignored files: `lib/puck/module-components.ts` (client-safe maps only) and `lib/puck/module-rsc-components.ts` (RSC maps only, server-only). Split into separate files (previously one) because a single shared file gave `lib/puck/config.tsx` a static import edge to any block's RSC half - if even one module block's RSC render used `next/headers` (e.g. Boards' cookie-based session checks), Next.js rejected the whole file the moment `lib/puck/config.tsx` was reached from the client Puck editor (`PuckEditor.tsx`/`LayoutPuckEditor.tsx`), regardless of which named export was actually used. Blocks whose RSC render needs server-only APIs must also split their own file in two (editor-safe placeholder + `.rsc.tsx` with the real render), and declare `rscImport` in the manifest pointing at the `.rsc` file (see `modules/boards/cactus.module.json`, `modules/gazette/cactus.module.json` for examples). RSC-only Puck config exports (`*RscConfig`, `getModuleLayoutPuckRscConfig`, `puckRscConfig`) live in `lib/puck/config.rsc.tsx`, not `config.tsx`, for the same reason.
- `scripts/generate-module-cron.mjs` - collects `cronJobs` from every module manifest; writes the gitignored `vercel.json` (`{crons: [...]}`); also prepends a hardcoded `CORE_CRONS` array (Members system: `/api/cron/members/purge`, `/api/cron/members/exports`) - core cron jobs are declared here rather than committed to `vercel.json` directly since that file is rebuilt from scratch on every build.
- `scripts/generate-module-settings-tabs.mjs` - collects `settingsTabs` from every module manifest (`{id, label, permission, import, component}`); writes the gitignored `lib/modules/settings-tabs.ts` (`moduleSettingsTabComponents: Record<id, Component>`). Consumed by `app/cactus-admin/config/ConfigPageClient.tsx` to render module-registered settings tabs generically (id/label/permission list comes from `app/cactus-admin/config/page.tsx`, which permission-filters live from `Module.manifest`, same pattern as `navEntries` in `layout.tsx`).
- `scripts/generate-module-sms-providers.mjs` - collects `smsProviders` from every module manifest (`{id, label, import, export}`); writes the gitignored `lib/modules/sms-providers.ts` (`moduleSmsProviders: Array<{module, id, label, provider}>`). Consumed by `lib/auth/sms.ts` (`getActiveSmsProvider()` - first configured provider from an active module, else null) to deliver login OTPs by text (admin password login + member SMS 2FA), always falling back to email.
- `scripts/generate-module-extension-points.mjs` - collects `extensionPoints` from every module manifest (`{point, id, permission, import, component}`); writes the gitignored `lib/modules/extension-points.ts` (`moduleExtensionPointComponents: Record<point, Record<id, Component>>`), grouped by the arbitrary `point` string. Core has no knowledge of any specific point name - a *publishing* module (e.g. `contact-form`) defines its own point names in its own page code and permission-filters live from `Module.manifest` (same pattern as `navEntries`/`settingsTabs`); a *contributing* module (e.g. `contact-form-reply-catcher`) declares entries against that point name in its manifest. See the "Module extension points" section in wiki/Authoring-a-module.md. First core (not module) publisher: `app/cactus-admin/config/page.tsx` (the Settings → Users → Roles subtab) reads `core.roles-page` the same way.
- `scripts/generate-module-layout-types.mjs` - collects `layoutTypes` from every module manifest; writes the gitignored `lib/layout/module-layout-types.ts` (pure data: groups + flat type→group lookup, each type optionally carrying `editorPreview: {className?, maxWidth?}`) and `lib/setup/module-starter-layouts.ts` (starter-template loader functions, imported per module). See "Module-declared layout types" under Puck Integration above.
- `scripts/generate-media-worker.mjs` - build-step: transpiles the Cloudflare media Worker (`workers/media-worker/index.ts`) to a plain ES module via `typescript` and embeds it as a string constant the app reads at runtime, so the admin > Settings > Media "Deploy Worker automatically" flow (`POST /api/admin/media/deploy-worker`) can upload runnable JavaScript to the user's Cloudflare account without a runtime transpile (`typescript` is a devDependency, pruned from the production runtime).
- `scripts/run-module-migrations.mjs` - build-step-only runner: for modules with status active/deploying/update_available, applies unapplied `modules/<name>/migrations/*.sql` files in lexicographic order, each in a transaction, recording name+checksum in `ModuleMigration`. The applied-migration ledger is read **once** into a Set up front, not one SELECT per (module, migration file) pair - with seven modules and several migrations each that was dozens of Neon round trips on every deploy purely to establish that there was nothing to do, which is the outcome on every build except the one that introduces a migration. The skip decision itself is unchanged. **Stale-ledger self-heal (2026-07-15):** before the per-module skip loop, if a module has recorded migrations in the ledger yet **no** table with its `tablePrefix` exists, the ledger is treated as stale (a restored/branched DB that carried the `ModuleMigration` rows but not the module's actual tables - which are not in a backup's schema section), its ledger rows are purged and its migrations re-applied from scratch. Restricted to the zero-prefixed-tables case so a healthy install is untouched and a non-idempotent `CREATE TABLE` can't collide. This is what recovered the live dwoffice.furniture contact-form/twilio tables after a restore left the ledger lying.
- `scripts/sync-module-manifests.mjs` - build-step-only: rewrites `Module.manifest` from each deployed module's `cactus.module.json` so nav entries/teardown stay in step with shipped code. Skips without DATABASE_URL.
- `scripts/sync-wiki.mjs` - `npm run sync-wiki`: pulls all `.md` files from the GitHub wiki repo (`WIKI_SOURCE_REPO` or GITHUB_REPO + `.wiki`) into `/wiki` via the API.
- `scripts/fetch-google-fonts.mjs` - standalone maintenance script (own npm script, not in the build): fetches the Google Fonts metadata catalogue and writes `lib/design/google-fonts.json`, the source for the admin font pickers. Run manually to refresh the available-fonts list.
- `scripts/dev-warm.sh` - `npm run dev:warm`: kills anything on the port, clears `.next`, starts `next dev --webpack` (webpack chosen over Turbopack to avoid an HMR chunk-hash reload cascade), and pre-warms `/`, `/home`, `/logged-out`, `/setup`, `/style-guide`, `/privacy-policy` in the background.

Build-time order (from `package.json` `build`, which is now just `prebuild.mjs && next build`): checkout-modules, then three concurrent branches - (a) prisma generate, (b) build-migrate (migrate deploy → reconcile-core-schema → run-module-migrations) → sync-module-manifests, (c) generate-all (generate-module-router → generate-module-puck → generate-module-cron → generate-module-settings-tabs → generate-module-sms-providers → generate-module-extension-points → generate-module-layout-types → generate-media-worker) - then `next build`. Dev (`npm run dev`) runs the generators then `next dev --webpack`.

### Build and Deploy

- Build steps in order: see Scripts above. `npm run build` is the single entry; Vercel runs it on every push. It is `node scripts/prebuild.mjs && next build`, where the prebuild is `checkout-modules` (barrier) followed by `prisma generate`, the `build-migrate` → `sync-module-manifests` database chain, and `generate-all` running concurrently.
- **Turbopack's build filesystem cache is on** (`next.config.ts` → `experimental.turbopackFileSystemCacheForBuild: true`). It persists the compilation cache in `.next/cache`, which Vercel already restores from the previous deployment (the "Restored build cache from previous deployment" line in the build log). Without it the full Turbopack compile - 41s of a measured 103s deploy - was paid on every push regardless of how small the diff was. It is still flagged experimental in Next 16, so if a deploy ever produces stale or impossible output, this is the first thing to switch off.
- **`next build` does NOT type-check.** `next.config.ts` sets `typescript.ignoreBuildErrors: true`. Measured on a real Vercel build, the `tsc` pass inside `next build` was 26s of a 123s deploy, and it duplicated the `tsc --noEmit` gate that CLAUDE.md's work loop already requires on every change. The check moved, it was not dropped: **`npm run typecheck` is now the only thing standing between a type error and production**, so it is not optional before a commit. There is deliberately no CI workflow enforcing it - `lib/updates/core-plan.ts` excludes only `modules/`, `modules.json` and `.gitmodules` from the core-update push, so a `.github/workflows/*` file would propagate into every customer's repo and run CI on their GitHub account. Adding one means excluding `.github/` from the core sync first.
- Prisma migrations run only inside the Vercel build step (`build-migrate.mjs` → `prisma migrate deploy`), never at runtime; the advisory lock is disabled because Vercel serialises builds and Neon cold starts exceed the lock timeout. One migration file exists, edited in place for schema changes (fresh-install platform). Because migrate deploy never re-applies an edited-in-place migration, additive core changes reach already-provisioned installs via idempotent `prisma/core-reconcile/*.sql` run by `reconcile-core-schema.mjs` immediately after migrate deploy.
- `prisma db push` is blocked (`npm run db:push` exits 1 with a message).
- Vercel-specific: `vercel.json` is generated (cron entries only) and gitignored; deployments are auto-triggered by pushes to `main`; env-var-only changes use the redeploy API (`POST /v13/deployments?forceNew=1` based on the latest production deployment); module/core changes deploy via Git Data API commits (registry sync / core sync) whose push triggers the build; the redeploy gate (`pendingRedeployId` sentinel → real id → cleared on READY / webhook / dismiss / 4-minute server timeout) drives the admin shell's deploy status bar and the notification bell's live section meanwhile. Deployment status arrives via webhook (Pro) or lazy polling (`getLatestDeploymentStatus`, Hobby).
- jsdom is pinned to `^26` (jsdom 29 breaks the Vercel serverless update check with ERR_REQUIRE_ESM).
- Tester repo relationship: `usersaynoso/Cactus-Foundation-Tester` is a downstream install of this platform used for live testing; local `.env.local` points at the same Neon database as the live Tester site. Pushes to the Tester repo use the identity `Chris Taylor-Guest <airings.snug-0m@icloud.com>` and version-prefixed commit titles; core code reaches it via the in-app core-update sync (blob-level tree diff of core files vs the matching upstream tag, skipping `modules/`, `.gitmodules`, `modules.json`).
- Release flow (per CLAUDE.md): patch-only version bumps, tag format `vX.Y.Z`, GitHub release created immediately after every push.

### Slash Commands

None. `.claude/commands/` does not exist. `.claude/` contains only `settings.json` (permission allowlist + `caveman@caveman` plugin enablement) and runtime state files. Available slash commands come from installed plugins, not this repo.

### Utilities and Lib

`lib/` root:

- `admin/search-index.ts` - `ADMIN_SEARCH_ENTRIES`: static, framework-agnostic registry the command palette adds on top of the nav (Settings tabs, their sections, and individual settings). Each entry: `{ id, label, section (breadcrumb), path (admin-relative, incl. `?tab=`/`?sub=`/`#hash`), keywords?, requires? (nav base path gate) }`. `search-index.test.ts` statically asserts unique ids, admin-relative paths, known `requires` values, and that **every `#hash` resolves to a real `id="…"` anchor** in `ConfigPageClient.tsx` (the one invariant tsc/eslint can't see). Adding a searchable setting = one entry here + a matching `id`/`admin-anchor` on the page.
- `deploy-log-translator.ts` - `translateLogLine(raw)`: maps Vercel build-log lines to friendly British-humour status messages (null = drop the line). Final line marker: "Bish bash bosh. You're live."
- `deploy-log-translator.test.ts` - vitest unit tests for the translator (run via `npm test`; no vitest config file exists).
- `markdown-client.ts` - browser-only markdown → sanitised HTML (marked + DOMPurify on `window`); identical allow-list to the server renderer.
- `sanitize.ts` - server/browser markdown → sanitised HTML; lazy-requires jsdom on the server; strips raw angle brackets pre-parse; also `markdownToPlainText`, `sanitizeRichText` (Puck RichText allow-list) and `sanitizeAndObfuscateRichText` (published RichText: sanitise first, obfuscate after - DOMPurify's re-serialisation decodes the obfuscator's entities, so the reverse order leaks the plain address; test: `lib/sanitize-obfuscate.test.ts`).
- `sanitize-config.ts` - shared `ALLOWED_TAGS`/`ALLOWED_ATTR` constants for both renderers.
- `email-obfuscate.tsx` - email spam-protection server half. `encodeEmail` = base64 of reversed address (the `data-eml` payload). For text: `linkifyEmails(text)` → React nodes (`<ObfuscatedEmail>` per match, entity-encoded visible text + `data-eml`); `obfuscateEmailsInHtml(html)` → same anchor markup spliced into text runs, entity-masking (not wrapping) inside `<a>`, rewriting a hand-written `href="mailto:…"` to `data-eml`, leaving `<code>/<pre>` verbatim. For owner-typed links: `emailSafeHref(href, obfuscate)` → `{href}` for ordinary links, `{'data-eml'}` and **no href** for a `mailto:` (query string preserved); `maskEmailText(label, obfuscate)` → entity-encoded `<span>` for label text inside an anchor, which can't be linkified without nesting an `<a>`. Consumed by every block in `config.tsx` (free text via the local `protectText` gate, hrefs via `emailSafeHref`) when `!puck.isEditing`, plus `MenuBlockClient.tsx`; client half is `components/EmailDeobfuscator.tsx`. Tests: `lib/email-obfuscate.test.ts`.
- `utils.ts` - `generateSlug`, `generateId` (nanoid), `parsePaginationParams` (page/perPage/skip, perPage ≤ 100), `errorResponse`, `successResponse`, `truncate`, `formatInTimezone`.

`lib/auth/`:

- `session.ts` - session + trusted-device create/validate/delete, cookie helpers, `listUserSessions`, `revokeSessionById`, `safeCompare` (timing-safe).
- `passkey.ts` - WebAuthn registration/authentication challenge creation and verification, `savePasskey`, `labelFromUserAgent`.
- `password.ts` - bcrypt hash/verify, strength check, Pwned Passwords check, `validateNewPassword`.
- `email-challenge.ts` - 6-digit OTP create/verify (10-min TTL, 5 attempts, hash compare).
- `rate-limit.ts` - action limits table (incl. Members system's `member_register`), `getClientIp`, `checkRateLimit`/`recordAttempt`, atomic `checkAndRecord` (raw INSERT … ON CONFLICT).
- `recovery.ts` - recovery token create/validate/consume (30-min TTL, single-use).
- `totp.ts` - secret generation, otpauth URI, QR data URL, `verifyTotpCode` with replay step guard.
- `turnstile.ts` - `verifyTurnstile` (fail-open unconfigured, fail-closed on error when configured).

`lib/config/`:

- `env.ts` - `isLocalMode`, `getEnvStatus` (single source of truth for the setup env-check and dashboard), `requiredEnvMissing`, `isEmailConfigured`, `isMediaProviderConfigured`, `getActiveMediaProvider`, `isMediaConfigured`, `configuredProxiedProviders`, `isGitHubConfigured`, `getGitHubConfigStatus`, `isVercelConfigured`, `isNeonConfigured`, `isEdgeConfigWritable`, `isTurnstileConfigured`, `getSiteUrl(+OrNull)`, `getWebAuthnRpId/Origin`, `getSessionSecret`.
- `site.ts` - 5-second in-memory caches for adminPath/status/pendingRedeployId (with the 4-minute redeploy auto-release), `invalidateSiteConfigCache`, `isSetupComplete`, the path/username BLOCKLIST, `isBlocklisted`, `generateSuggestedAdminPath`.
- `edge-config.ts` - Edge Config reads (`adminPath`, `siteStatus`) via `@vercel/edge-config`; `syncToEdgeConfig` writes via the Vercel REST API.
- `neon-regions.ts` - the 8 selectable Neon regions.

`lib/consent/`: `types.ts` (ConsentCategory/BannerConfig/Decision/CookiePayload + `DEFAULT_CONSENT_BANNER_CONFIG`), `gate.ts` (client: `hasConsent`, `onConsentChange`, `loadIfConsented`, `notifyConsentChange`; backs `window.cactusConsent`).

`lib/crypto/secrets.ts` - AES-256-GCM `encryptSecret`/`decryptSecret` using ENCRYPTION_KEY; format `iv:authTag:ciphertext` (hex).

`lib/members/`:

- `config.ts` - `MembersConfigSchema` (Zod, all Members settings with defaults: enabled false, registrationMode OPEN, emailVerificationRequired true, allowedAuthMethods [PASSKEY, MAGIC_LINK], passwordsEnabled false, trustedBrowserDays 30, sessionDays 30, avatar/gravatar toggles true, siteWideMembersOnly false + exceptions [], guestPreviewEnabled false, username changes off with 90/30-day cooldown/redirect, deletionGracePeriodDays 14, domain allow/blocklists [], profileVisibility PUBLIC, accountSectionsEnabled all true, directoryEnabled false, smsTwoFactorPolicy OPTIONAL - OPTIONAL|REQUIRED, whether members with a password must enrol a mobile number for SMS sign-in codes; REQUIRED only bites while an SMS provider module is active, see `sms-policy.ts` below), `parseMembersConfig` (corrupt column falls back to defaults), `getMembersConfig`, `getMembersConfigCached` (5s TTL for proxy reads), `invalidateMembersConfigCache`.
- `paths.ts` - `MEMBER_INTERNAL = '/cactus-account'`, `DEFAULT_MEMBER_AREA_PATH = 'account'`, `getMemberAreaPath()` (sanitised MEMBER_AREA_PATH env var; invalid or blocklisted values fall back to the default, `account` itself exempt from the blocklist check).
- `sms-policy.ts` - `memberNeedsSmsEnrolment(config, twoFactorConfigs)`: true only when `smsTwoFactorPolicy` is REQUIRED, the member has no verified SMS `MemberTwoFactor` row, AND an SMS provider module is active/configured (`getActiveSmsProvider`) - no provider means the policy silently behaves as OPTIONAL. Consumed by the password login + 2fa verify routes (`smsEnrolmentRequired` response flag → `LoginForm.tsx` `finishLogin` redirects to the account overview instead of `redirectTo`) and by the member account layout (warning banner, shown only to members who actually have a password).
- `tokens.ts` - hashed single-use tokens for member verification links (mirrors `lib/auth/recovery.ts`): `generateMemberToken`/`hashMemberToken`, `createVerificationToken`/`consumeVerificationToken` (`MemberVerificationToken`, 24h TTL), `canResendVerification` (60s per-member throttle, keyed off the latest token row regardless of used/unused).
- `registration.ts` - `isUsernameFormatValid`/`isUsernameAvailable` (format regex + blocklist + `Member.username` uniqueness), `isEmailDomainAllowed` (allow/blocklist against `membersConfig`), `deriveInitialStatus`/`deriveActivatedStatus` (status a `Member` is created with vs. the status it moves to once verified, per `registrationMode`; verification is only "required" when both `emailVerificationRequired` is true AND email is actually configured, otherwise there'd be no way to ever satisfy it), `validateInviteToken`/`consumeInviteToken` (`MemberInvite`, single-use), `sendVerificationEmail` (shared by the register route and the resend route), `loginRejectionForStatus` (single source of truth for every login method: null when a status may sign in (ACTIVE only), else `{error, redirectToVerify?}`).
- `session.ts` - member session/cookie layer, fully separate from `lib/auth/session.ts`: `createMemberSession`/`validateMemberSession` (ACTIVE-only, sliding expiry) /`deleteMemberSession`/`deleteAllMemberSessions`/`listMemberSessions`/`revokeMemberSessionById`, cookie helpers (`cactus_member_session`), `getMemberFromCookie`; trusted-browser twin `createMemberTrustedBrowser`/`isMemberBrowserTrusted`/`revokeAllMemberTrustedBrowsers` (cookie `cactus_member_trusted`). Durations read from `membersConfig.sessionDays`/`trustedBrowserDays` via `getMembersConfigCached`.
- `passkey.ts` - WebAuthn registration/authentication for members, mirrors `lib/auth/passkey.ts` against `Member`/`MemberPasskey`; reuses `WebAuthnChallenge` with `memberId` set and `member_registration`/`member_authentication` purposes instead of a second challenge table.
- `magic-link.ts` - `sendMagicLink`/`consumeMagicLink`, hashed single-use `MemberMagicLink` tokens (15-min TTL, plain sha256 like `tokens.ts` - status gating happens at the route, not here).
- `email-challenge.ts` - mirrors `lib/auth/email-challenge.ts` against `MemberEmailChallenge`; `createMemberEmailChallenge`/`verifyMemberEmailChallenge`, purposes `login_2fa`/`setup_2fa`, 10-min TTL, 5 attempts, hash compare.
- `recovery-codes.ts` - `generateMemberRecoveryCodes` (10 codes, shown once, replaces any unused set), `consumeMemberRecoveryCode`, `countRemainingRecoveryCodes`.
- `activity.ts` - `recordMemberActivity` (`source: null` = core, else the contributing module name), `listMemberActivity`.
- `deletion.ts` - `requestMemberDeletion`/`cancelMemberDeletion` (grace period from `membersConfig.deletionGracePeriodDays`), `purgeScheduledDeletions` (cron target, hard-delete past the grace period).
- `export.ts` - `assembleMemberExport` (core tables + each active module's `memberExtensions.dataExportPath`, called over self-origin HTTP with an internal bearer derived from `SESSION_SECRET` - `verifyInternalExportBearer` is exported for a module's own handler to check it), `createDataExportRequest` (assemble→upload→ready, synchronously within the request; refuses a second request while one is in flight; deletes the stuck row on failure rather than leaving it stuck, since the schema has no FAILED status), `expireDataExports` (cron target, 48h).
- `admin-log.ts` - `logMemberAdminAction(actor, memberId, action, detail?)`, writes a `MemberAdminActionLog` row (actor snapshot, not a live relation - survives the admin user being deleted later).
- `admin-notify.ts` - `notifyAdminMemberPendingApproval`/`notifyAdminMemberDeletionRequested`: in-app alert (reuses the generic `message` `NotificationType` + `upsertAlert` dedupe - members have no dedicated notification type of their own) + an email to every protected-role admin when email is configured (the deletion one renders through `lib/email/templates.ts`, `member.deletion-admin-notify`; the pending-approval one has no matching template in the 11-key registry, so it stays a plain inline send). Gating on `notifyAdminOnPendingApproval`/`adminNotifyOnDeletion` happens at the call site, not in here.
- `digest.ts` - `runDigest('DAILY'|'WEEKLY')`, see the Email section.
- `access.ts` - pure matching logic for `proxy.ts`'s Phase 8 site-access gate: `isPathExcepted`, `resolveRouteTier` (no I/O, unit-testable in isolation from the session/DB lookups that surround them in proxy.ts).
- `avatar.ts` - `resolveEffectiveAvatarChoice`, see Media Layer section.

`lib/db/prisma.ts` - global-singleton PrismaClient (query logging in development).

`lib/deploy/`: `reconcile.ts` (`markModulesDeploySucceeded` - promotes pendingVersion, clears alerts; `markModulesDeployFailed` - reverts to update_available or failed), `redeploy.ts` (`startDeferredRedeploy` - arms the redeploy gate synchronously, then in `after()` syncs modules.json or falls back to an env-var redeploy, and polls Vercel for the new deployment id). Both git-push paths (a modules.json commit, and `committedSince` mode where the caller already pushed) go through `captureOrTrigger`: poll first so the push's own build is adopted rather than double-deployed, then, only if no build ever appears, start one via `ensureVercelRedeploy`. Without that fallback a push that produces no build (missed webhook) is never retried by anything - the commit sits unbuilt while module rows are promoted to versions whose code never deployed.

`lib/design/tokens.ts` - `DesignTokens` v2 type, `DEFAULT_DESIGN_TOKENS`, `COLOUR_PRESETS`, `buildTokenStyles` (tokens → CSS custom properties for the public site), `buildAdminThemeStyles` (primary-colour family + `--font-sans` only, for admin white-labelling), `buildFontHref` (Google Fonts URL for non-system fonts). Every `themeStyle` colour has an optional `*Dark` sibling (`colourDark`, `hoverColourDark`, `textColourDark`, `bgColourDark`, `borderColourDark`, `labelColourDark`); `buildTokenStyles` emits each as a CSS var (`--color-link`, `--body-color`, `--btn-bg`, `--field-text`, `--h1-color`, …), redefines only the overridden ones in the `[data-theme="dark"]` + `@media(prefers-color-scheme:dark)` blocks, and its scoped `main …` rules reference those vars so a dark override cascades on the frontend (unset → inherits the light value). `ColourPreset` carries `linkColourDark`/`linkHoverColourDark` alongside the light pair, so applying a preset seeds dark-mode link colours too. `buttons.secondary`/`.outline` (`ButtonVariantStyle`) and `themeStyle.badges` (`Partial<Record<BadgeColourKey, BadgeStyle>>`, `BADGE_COLOUR_KEYS` export) follow the same optional-field/`*Dark`-sibling pattern; `themeStyle.pillRadius` is a plain string (no dark variant - a radius, not a colour), emitted as `--radius-pill` alongside the fixed `--radius-sm`/`-md`/`-lg` in the same `fixed` CSS-var string.

`lib/email/index.ts` - see Email section. `lib/email/templates.ts` - Members system admin-editable email templates, see Email section.

`lib/github/client.ts` - see GitHub API Integration. `lib/github/retry.ts` - shared Git Data API resilience: `isTransientGitError` (BadObjectState / 5xx / "not a fast forward" / "Reference does not exist" / secondary rate limit), `retryTransient` (8-attempt equal-jitter backoff, cap 60s), `createReplicatedBlob` (createBlob + read-back confirm before referencing in a tree). Used by `lib/updates/core.ts` (`syncCoreFromUpstream`) and `lib/modules/github.ts` (`commitModulesJson`) - both now wrap the whole createTree→createCommit→updateRef write in `retryTransient`, re-reading HEAD each attempt so replication lag and HEAD races self-heal.

`lib/layout/`: `displayConditions.ts` (rule types, match + specificity scoring), `resolveThemeLayout.ts` (best published layout for a type/context), `starter-templates.ts` (**the single source of truth for starter templates** - `CORE_STARTER_TEMPLATES: Record<layoutType, StarterTemplate[]>` = header ×14 / footer ×5 / infoPage ×4 / notFound ×4 / statusPage ×4, plus block-prop helpers; `getStarterTemplates(type)` merges core with the module-declared ones from the generated `lib/setup/module-starter-layouts.ts`, `allStarterTemplates()` flattens the lot for the seeder. **Must stay free of server-only imports** - the new-layout picker imports it straight into the browser. A `StarterTemplate` is `{id, name, description, data, publishByDefault?, defaultConditions?}`. Replaces both the old DB-seeded starter rows *and* the separate hardcoded `STARTERS_BY_TYPE` map that used to live inside `layouts/new/page.tsx` - the two had already drifted, 13 header variants vs 9), `layout-type-tabs.ts` (`CORE_LAYOUT_TYPES`, `TYPE_LABELS`, `CORE_TYPE_TABS`, `MODULE_GROUP_TABS` - shared by the Layouts list and the picker so their tab sets cannot disagree, which they previously did).

`lib/media/`: `providers.ts`, `loader.ts`, `upload.ts` (also `downloadMedia`, `deleteMedia`, `saveMediaRecord`, `getMediaReferences`), `migration.ts` - see Media Layer.

`lib/menu/resolve.ts` - `resolveMenu` (published-page filtering, nested tree build), `resolveMainMenu`.

`lib/modules/`: `manifest.ts` (zod schemas for `cactus.module.json` and `cactus.theme.json`, `parseGitHubRepo` strict URL validation, `fetchManifestFromRepo`, `validateTablePrefixUnique`; gained an optional `memberExtensions` field - `activityTypes[]`, `notificationCategories[]`, `dataExportPath?`, `routeTiers[]` - for modules to declare Members-system contributions, see MEMBERS_SPEC.md amendment 5), `member-extensions.ts` (live reads of every active module's `memberExtensions`: `getModuleActivityTypes`, `getModuleNotificationCategories`, `getModuleDataExportPaths`, `getModuleRouteTiers` (+ `getModuleRouteTiersCached`, 5s TTL, for `proxy.ts`); pure data, no codegen step needed since none of it is a component import, unlike `extensionPoints`/`settingsTabs`), `github.ts` (`getLatestRelease` by channel, `syncModulesJson`, `getLatestDeploymentStatus`), `updates.ts` (`findModuleUpdates` - pure detection), `router.ts` (AUTO-GENERATED, gitignored - API dispatch + page loaders for installed modules).

`lib/notifications/`: `alerts.ts` (`upsertAlert` keyed by dedupeKey - re-surfaces on title change; `clearAlert`; `recordCoreUpdate`; `recordModuleUpdate`), `deployment.ts` (`recordDeploymentNeeded` rolling reasons list, `getUnreadCount`, `labelForEnvKeys`).

`lib/permissions/check.ts` - see Permissions System.

`lib/privacy/template.ts` - privacy-policy generator: `WizardAnswers` type, `DATA_COLLECTED_OPTIONS`, `PURPOSE_OPTIONS`, `DISCLAIMER_TEXT`, `assemblePolicyMarkdown` (jurisdiction-aware GDPR/CCPA sections).

`lib/puck/`: `config.tsx` (all block definitions + per-context configs; TipTap HTML conversion for RSC richtext), `siteLogoAlign.ts` (`LOGO_ALIGN_OPTIONS` + `siteLogoAlign()`, shared by SiteLogo's two render halves so the editor and live markup cannot drift), `module-components.ts` (AUTO-GENERATED, gitignored), `editor-routes.ts` (`isPuckEditorRoute(pathname)` - the single definition of "this route is a full-viewport Puck editor", consumed only by `AdminShell`; matches `/pages/<id>`, `/layouts/<id>` and the legacy `/appearance/header|footer`, and deliberately NOT `/pages/new` or `/layouts/new`, which are an ordinary form and the starter-template picker. Unit-tested in `editor-routes.test.ts` because getting it wrong strips a normal admin page's padding and scrollbar, which typechecks fine), `resolveTemplateData.ts`, `renderInfoPage.tsx` (`resolveContentData`, `renderInfoPageContent`), `renderLayoutWithContent.tsx` (injects page content into a layout's ContentSlot), `MediaPickerField.tsx` (`OgImagePickerField`, `ImageUrlPickerField`, `withImagePickerFields` - media-library modal fields + the helper that swaps a config's image URL text fields for the picker in both editors; the shared `MediaPickerModal` now has a "+ Upload" button in its header that POSTs the chosen file to `/api/admin/media` and auto-selects the returned item, so the Image / Image+Floating Chips / Card / OG-image pickers can add a brand-new image without leaving the block, not just pick an existing one; the modal also browses the media folder tree - breadcrumb + subfolder tiles from `/api/admin/media/folders`, media scoped per-folder, search spans all folders), `MenuCheckboxField.tsx`, `MenuSelectField.tsx`, `MinMaxPairField.tsx` (two plain text inputs side-by-side in one custom field slot - min/max pair, used by MenuBlock's fluid spacing/letter-spacing/font-size fields), `UnitValueField.tsx` (`UnitValueField` + `ResponsiveUnitValueField` - number box + unit dropdown for CSS lengths, per-field `units:` list, stores the plain CSS string so saved data/render paths are untouched; responsive variant rides `ResponsiveFieldShell`; used by every length field that was previously free text - grid column widths, sticky offsets, image max-width, embed height, header shrunk height, underline thickness/offset, Section/Spacer custom sizes), `MenuBlockEditorPreview.tsx` (editor-side MenuBlock preview with live menu fetch), `SiteColourField.tsx` (palette swatch picker, dual light/dark preview per swatch, + custom native-picker swatch; optional `allowManual` prop adds a free-text CSS-colour box under the swatches - used by the border/icon/text-colour fields that were previously bare text inputs), `SiteFontField.tsx` (font-family picker for block fields - site fonts first, then Google Fonts catalogue search, free text allowed) + `useSiteFonts.ts` (cached `/api/admin/appearance` fonts fetch, mirrors `useSiteColours`), `BorderField.tsx` (show/hide + colour-swatch field, one box - colour swatches hide entirely when `show: 'hide'`), `useSiteColours.ts` (shared cached `/api/admin/appearance` fetch behind both of the above, avoids remount flicker), `SiteLogoEditorPreview.tsx` + `useSiteBranding.ts` (cached `/api/admin/config` fetch, injects real branding logo into the `SiteLogo` block's editor preview), `BgColorField.tsx` (`SectionBgColorField`/`HeroBgColorField`/`HeaderBgColorField`/`PageBgColorField` - background mode select + a mode-aware second input, one box: colour swatches only for the solid-colour modes (`color`, `transparent-scroll` - the SWATCH_MODES set), a CSS-gradient text box for `gradient`, and nothing at all for none/transparent/image/decorative modes, whose `color` value never paints. Shared body takes `allowOpacity` + `allowDark` flags (both on for Section + Hero only). `allowOpacity` adds a "Colour opacity" 0-100 slider for `mode: color`; a translucent colour is stored as `color-mix(in srgb, <base> N%, transparent)` - via `splitBgColour`/`composeBgColour` round-trip - so it still rides a `var(--color-N)` (rgba() can't). `allowDark` adds a "Dark mode colour" swatch row; when set, the whole value is encoded as CSS `light-dark(<light>, <dark>)` (round-tripped by `splitLightDark`/`composeLightDark`, paren-aware split since each arm may be a color-mix). The site sets `color-scheme: light|dark` with its theme (globals.css), so the browser resolves the right arm with NO render-side change - Section/Hero already paint `backgroundColor: color`. Lets a section/hero background colour be made see-through (translucent card over a hero photo) AND carry a separate colour per light/dark mode. One opacity applies to both arms), `ColourSwatchButton.tsx` (shared swatch button w/ hover tooltip, used by `SiteColourField`/`BorderField`/`BgColorField`; also exports `CustomColourSwatch` - a rainbow swatch wrapping a hidden native colour picker, appended to all three swatch rows so any colour can be set, not just the palette, storing a raw hex - and `isCustomColour` helper), `components/AosInit.tsx` (AOS init client component), `components/MenuBlockClient.tsx` (public interactive menu: dropdowns, mobile hamburger, and a per-breakpoint "Nav behaviour" of show/collapse-to-hamburger/dropdown-current-page - the `navToggle` responsive field; dropdown mode shows a current-page trigger via `NavDropdown`, revealed by `cactus-nav-dd-*` breakpoint classes from `buildTokenStyles`), `components/SiteLogoClient.tsx` (logo/site-name link with hover state), `components/ScaleToFit.tsx` (client wrapper that shrinks any content to fit its grid column via `transform:scale`, opt-in per column via Grid `col*Scale`; also see `getGridTemplateColumns` now using `minmax(0, W)` not `minmax(min-content, W)` so a set column width is honoured instead of propped open by content), `components/MembersBlocksRsc.tsx` (Members system Puck blocks' live async RSC render functions - see Puck Integration section).
- `lib/puck/tabs/`: `createPanelPlugin.tsx` (shared sidebar-tab factory + hand-rolled lucide-style tab icons), `rootFieldsOverride.tsx` (`hideRootFieldsOverride`), `headerBackLinkOverride.tsx` (`createBackLinkOverride(href, label)` - `overrides.header` factory that overlays a back-arrow link into Puck's own header, in the blank gutter it already reserves left of its title on desktop; see Puck Integration), `sidebarOverrides.css` (global CSS matched by class-name-prefix substring since `@puckeditor/core` hashes its CSS Modules class names - see Puck Integration), `LayoutSettingsTab.tsx`, `PageSettingsTab.tsx`, `SeoTab.tsx`, `PageHistoryTab.tsx`, `SavedBlocksTab.tsx`.
- `lib/puck/outline/`: `OutlineTree.tsx` (default export, wired as `overrides.outline` in both editors - draggable replacement for Puck's select-only Outline tab; pointer-event drag, drop indicator, auto-expand on hover, panel autoscroll, Alt+arrow keyboard moves), `tree.ts` (pure tree logic, no React: `buildOutline` walks root content + slot props + legacy `data.zones`, `indexOutline`/`ancestorIds`/`zoneIsInsideItem` for parent lookup and the drop-into-own-subtree guard, `flattenOutline` for visible rows, `computeMove` for Puck's remove-then-insert index shift), `tree.test.ts` (unit tests - the index shift and the subtree guard are the two things that silently corrupt a page if wrong).
- `lib/layout/layout-type-labels.ts` - `getLayoutTypeLabel(type)`: human label for a layout type (`Header`/`Footer`/`Page Layout`/`404`/`Status Page`, or the generated module-type label via `moduleLayoutTypeToGroup`). Used for Puck's `headerTitle` prop in `LayoutPuckEditor.tsx`.

`lib/setup/`: `starterLayouts.ts` - **no longer seeds starter rows**; starter templates are in-code data (`lib/layout/starter-templates.ts`). Jobs, deliberately kept apart:
  - `seedDefaultLayouts(db)` (**install only** - `/api/setup/complete`, `reset-database`): for each template flagged `publishByDefault` (core's default header/footer/full-width page/404 hero/coming-soon/maintenance, plus module templates whose pages have no hardcoded fallback, i.e. Shop's), seeds **one ordinary published Layout** at id `<template-id>-live` with the template's `defaultConditions`. Create-only upsert. The `-live` suffix is load-bearing: existing installs' live layouts already sit there, and renaming it would seed them a second header.
  - `seedPendingModuleLayouts(db)` (**request time**, from `ensureLayoutsCurrent()`): seeds any `active`/`inactive`/`update_available` module still carrying a **NULL** `layoutsSeededAt` whose code is in this build, then stamps it. Covers both the reconcile that ran on a build without the module's code (skipped unstamped) and the stamps `core-reconcile/009` cleared. It lives on a request path because reconcile only runs when a *module* deploy finishes - a site whose Shop was already mis-stamped would otherwise stay 404ing until the owner happened to install or update another module. **NULL-only**, so it can never re-mint a layout an owner deleted: a seeded module keeps its stamp regardless of what happens to the rows afterwards. Runs *after* the prune, so a module's fresh layouts are never binned by the same pass that made them, and outside the version gate (recovery must not wait for the next core update). `planPendingModuleSeeds(pending, inBuild)` is the **pure, unit-tested** half (5 cases in `starterLayouts.test.ts`).
  - `ensureLayoutsCurrent()` (**request time** - `app/(public)/layout.tsx`, `GET /api/admin/layouts`): runs `pruneLegacyStarterCopies` once per core version, gated on `SiteConfig.starterTemplatesVersion` vs `package.json` (module-level flag = one `SiteConfig` query per warm instance; a failed run leaves the stamp unwritten so a later request retries), then `seedPendingModuleLayouts` on every warm instance. **Never re-creates a layout a seeded module once had** - an existing site has its layouts already, and seeding a second `entire_site` header into it would silently change its design (Tester's live header is `starter-header-tall-live`, not `starter-header-live`, so a naive re-seed would have done exactly that).
  - `pruneLegacyStarterCopies(db)`: deletes the `<id>-live`/`<id>-edited` copies the old scheme spawned - its migration branch keyed off `status === 'published'`, which every starter row also was, so it minted a `<id>-live` copy of **every** starter on **every** core update (Tester had accumulated 54 published-but-condition-less rows + 21 `-edited` "(Copy)" drafts on top of 68 starters = 158 Layout rows). Deciding these is a **content** comparison against the in-code templates, which SQL cannot do, so it stays at runtime. **The starter rows themselves are NOT deleted here** - `prisma/core-reconcile/005_retire_starter_layouts.sql` does that at build time. That split is load-bearing, not cosmetic: the reconcile drops the `isStarter` column during the build, so a runtime `where: { isStarter: true }` would run *after* the column was gone, throw, get swallowed by `ensureLayoutsCurrent`'s catch, leave the stamp unwritten, and strand the rows forever. Delete-then-drop, in one SQL file, in that order. Everything this function keys on (row id, display conditions, `builderData`) survives the drop.
  - `planStarterCleanup(rows, templates)` - **pure, unit-tested** (`starterLayouts.test.ts`). Deletes a row only when all three hold: id is `<known-template-id>-live` or `-edited`; `displayConditions.include` is empty (renders nowhere); and `builderData` still `stableStringify`-equals the canonical template (nobody edited it). Anything the owner touched, published, or built fails one of the three and survives. `stableStringify` sorts object keys at every depth so a jsonb round-trip (Postgres does not preserve key order) still compares equal.

  `stylesInfoPage.ts` (`upsertStylesInfoPage` - seeds the draft `style-guide` page; `STYLES_PAGE_SLUG`/`TITLE`).

`lib/updates/core.ts` - `compareVersions`, `getCoreUpdateStatus` (channel-aware, cached 10 min / errors 30 s, aggregates release notes for all newer releases), `syncCoreFromUpstream` (reconcile-toward-target push, see GitHub API Integration), `invalidateCoreUpdateCache`; re-exports `planCoreSync`/`isSkippedCorePath`. `lib/updates/core-plan.ts` - pure dependency-free reconciliation planner `planCoreSync` (writes = target blob sha ≠ base blob sha; deletes = core-managed + removed upstream + present in base; none if base tree truncated) + `isSkippedCorePath`; unit-tested by `lib/updates/core.plan.test.ts`.

`lib/vercel/`: `deploy.ts` (`triggerVercelRedeploy` - redeploy latest production deployment; `ensureVercelRedeploy` - same but adopts an already-in-flight production deploy instead of stacking another. Both build via `createRedeploy`, which passes `withLatestCommit: true` alongside `deploymentId`: without it Vercel inherits the source deployment's gitSource *including its commit sha*, so a "redeploy" replays the last-deployed commit rather than the branch's current HEAD - correct-looking whenever the two coincide, and a silent rollback when they don't), `env.ts` (list/upsert/delete project env vars; sensitive-key typing - sensitive vars skip the `development` target; `SENSITIVE_KEYS` set).

### Components

Admin (`components/admin/`):

- `AdminShell.tsx` - sidebar shell: mobile drawer, collapsible rail (persisted in localStorage, auto-collapse inside Puck editors - "inside a Puck editor" is `isPuckEditorRoute` from `lib/puck/editor-routes.ts`, which also decides the `admin-content--puck` chrome class), toolbar (collapse toggle, command-palette search button, ThemeToggle, NotificationBell), wraps children in `AdminPathProvider`; renders `DeployStatusBar` as a full-width strip above the whole shell (sidebar included) on every admin page; mounts `CommandPalette` once for the whole admin. Props: adminPath, siteName, version, sections (server-resolved `ResolvedNavSection[]`), moduleSettingsTabs (permission-filtered `{id,label}[]` of module Settings tabs, forwarded to `CommandPalette` for search), unreadCount, faviconUrl, faviconDarkUrl, children. Sidebar logo swaps `/cactus.svg` for the admin's uploaded favicon (via `resolveBranding()` in `app/cactus-admin/layout.tsx`, `faviconUrl`/`faviconDarkUrl` - light/dark pair shown/hidden by the existing `data-logo-variant` + `data-theme` CSS toggle) once one's set, falling back to the Cactus mark otherwise; `.admin-sidebar-logo-text` wraps the site name onto up to 2 lines (`-webkit-line-clamp: 2`) before ellipsis-truncating, instead of clipping to one line.
- `DeployStatusBar.tsx` - always-mounted, self-hiding slim strip pinned (sticky) to the very top of the admin shell, above sidebar and content. Reads the shared client deploy-status store (`lib/deploy-status-client.ts`); shows spinner + state badge + latest translated log line, or a Dismiss button on failure. The store does the polling: `/api/admin/redeploy-status` until the `'pending'` sentinel resolves to a real deployment id (2s), then `/api/setup/deployment-logs` (4s); on READY tail-done it clears the gate (`DELETE /api/admin/redeploy-status`), drops the update-check sessionStorage cache and `window.location.reload()`s. `announceRedeployStarted()` (same store) is called by every redeploy-triggering client action - it flips the store active immediately and fires the `cactus:redeploy-started` window event, which pops the notification bell open.
- `AdminNav.tsx` - renders the server-resolved `sections` prop (`ResolvedNavSection[]` from `resolveAdminMenu`); no hardcoded nav array any more. Each item row is a link + hover pin (favourite) star + optional restricted badge (lock/eye-off, admins only) + route-change loading spinner; module icons are still manifest-supplied SVG innerHTML (sanitised server-side) or a fallback icon. Above the sections: a filter box (live-filters items to a flat result list), a Quick "New…" menu (deep-links collected from visible items' `createAction`), and an expand/collapse-all button. Optional Favourites and Recently-visited groups (both `localStorage`: `cactus-sidebar-favourites`, `cactus-sidebar-recents`) render above the real sections. Up/Down arrow keys rove focus between items; navigating auto-expands the active item's section and scrolls it into view. Section labels still toggle+persist per-label (`cactus-sidebar-sections-collapsed`); collapsed-rail tooltips (portal `.admin-nav-tip`) + account/sign-out/version(→`AboutModal`) footer unchanged. Props: adminPath, version, sections, collapsed, onNavClick.
- `CommandPalette.tsx` - Cmd/Ctrl+K command palette. Subsequence match (`scoreCommand`) over: every sidebar destination + `createAction` shortcut, **plus the static deep-settings index** `lib/admin/search-index.ts` (every Settings tab, the sections inside them, and individual settings - backup, SMTP, roles, cookie banner, colours, etc.). Each index entry matches on label **and** keyword synonyms (label hits rank above keyword hits above breadcrumb hits) and carries a breadcrumb hint + a deep-link `path` (query `?tab=`/`?sub=` and/or a `#section` hash). Deep entries are gated by `requires` (a nav base path): only offered when that page is visible in the user's resolved sidebar, so search never links to a screen the role hides. Also indexes **module-provided Settings tabs** (Shop, Gazette, …) as `${label} settings` → `/config?tab=<id>`, from the `moduleSettingsTabs` prop the admin layout resolves (permission-filtered server-side from each active module's `manifest.settingsTabs`, gated by the tab's own permission in the layout's existing batch query). Up/Down + Enter to jump (`router.push`); when the target `href` has a `#`, also fires a `cactus:scroll-hash` window event so a same-tab hash-only jump still scrolls. Esc to close; `?` (when not typing) opens the shortcuts overlay. Portals to `document.body`; also opened by `AdminShell`'s toolbar search button via `cactus:open-command-palette`. Props: adminPath, sections, moduleSettingsTabs?.
- `useScrollToHash.ts` - hook: scrolls the element named by the current URL hash into view (retries ~2s so it lands after tab-gated content mounts), then flashes it (`.admin-search-target-flash`). Listens to `hashchange` + the palette's `cactus:scroll-hash` event; re-attempts when caller-passed `deps` change (e.g. active tab). Powers the command-palette "jump straight to this setting" deep links. Used by `ConfigPageClient` (Settings). Anchors are plain `id="…"` + `className="admin-anchor"` (`scroll-margin-top` in globals.css) on the page's section wrappers.
- `AboutModal.tsx` - About Cactus Foundation dialog opened from the sidebar version number. Cactus mark (`/cactus.svg`) + name + slogan + blurb + grouped credits roll (from `lib/about/credits.ts` `ABOUT`/`CREDITS`, includes a Claude Code credit), footer with a "Release notes" button. That button opens a second stacked overlay `ReleaseNotesModal` (same file) which infinite-scrolls the full release history from `GET /api/admin/release-notes?page=N` (15/page), newest-first, rendering each release's sanitized notes HTML. **Portals to `document.body`** via `createPortal` (gated on a `useSyncExternalStore` mounted check) - required because `AdminNav` mounts it inside `.admin-sidebar` (`position: sticky`, which always creates its own stacking context), so a non-portaled `position: fixed` overlay nested there paints within that context and gets covered by `<main>` regardless of z-index. `ReleaseNotesModal` doesn't need its own portal call, it renders inside the already-portaled tree. Both layers are token-styled overlays (backdrop-click + Escape close; release notes on top; each `Overlay` sets `isolation: isolate`). Colours/radii via CSS vars only; header/body/footer rows each set their own `background: var(--color-bg)` and the card clips with `overflow: hidden`.
- `AdminPathContext.tsx` - React context (default `cactus-admin`); `useAdminPath()`.
- `LayoutPreview.tsx` - a small structural drawing of a layout, **derived from that layout's own Puck `data`** (`{type, data, height?}`). Containers (`Grid` cols/`columnSizes`, `Split` `ratio` + `zones`, `Section` `maxWidth`, `Group` `direction`/`justify`) give the shape; leaf blocks become boxes and bars (`SiteLogo`, `MenuBlock`, `LoginButton`, `ThemeToggle`, `SocialLinks`, `Copyright`, `Heading`, `TextBlock`, `Callout`, `Hero` (height from `minHeight`), `ContentSlot` (the dashed primary well - the one thing a page layout must show)). Header/footer render as a band with a ghost page body behind it, sized from `root.props.height` and inset from `maxWidth`, with the bottom/top border reflecting `border.show`. **Unknown block types - i.e. every block a module ships - fall back to a plain box**, with shape hints keyed on ordinary English words in the type name (`/Header$/`, `/List|Grid|Browser/`, `/Body|Comments|Detail/`); no module is named anywhere, so a module gets previews for free and core stays clean. Used by both the Layouts list cards and the starter picker; replaces the old `LayoutThumbnail` that guessed a layout's shape from substrings of its **name** (`n.includes('sidebar')`). Colour tokens only, no hex.
- `NotificationBell.tsx` - bell + unread badge, portal dropdown listing notifications with view/redeploy/read-toggle/delete actions (same handlers as the notifications page). While a redeploy is in flight the dropdown shows a compact live status section at the top (spinner, state badge, ~3-line scrollable translated log fed by `lib/deploy-status-client.ts`); the dropdown auto-opens on the `cactus:redeploy-started` window event. Also renders the **live media-upload batch** (`UploadSection`) as its own section below the deploy status, fed by the shared `lib/upload-status-client.ts` store (subscribed via `useSyncExternalStore`) - per-file progress bars, a Clear for finished files, per-file dismiss; these entries have **no read/unread state** and don't touch `unreadCount`. The bell shows the spinner (not the count badge) while uploads are active, and auto-opens on the `cactus:upload-started` window event. Props: adminPath, unreadCount, collapsed.
- `DeployLogViewer.tsx` - renders translated deploy-log messages (via `translateLogLine`), deduped, last 8 visible, `onComplete` on the final line. Props: rawLines, onComplete, onError.
- `UnsavedChangesModal.tsx` - cancel/discard/save-and-leave dialog. Props: pendingHref, saving, message, onCancel, onDiscard, onSave?.
- `useUnsavedChanges.ts` - hook: `dirtyRef` + beforeunload warning + in-app link interception → `pendingHref`.
- `TabStrip.tsx` - shared underline-style horizontal tab bar (flush edges, no side gaps); scrolls with edge fade + click arrow overlay when tabs overflow. Items render as `<Link>` (if `href`) or `<button>` (if `onClick`). Props: items (key, label, href?, onClick?, active), trailing?, style?. Used by Settings, Appearance→Styles, Layouts, and by Gazette/Boards/Contact-form module nav and list tabs.

Public/shared:

- `components/ThemeToggle.tsx` - light/auto/dark toggle; persists `cactus-theme`, applies `data-theme`, follows system in auto. `style` prop selects one of 6 presentations (`segmented` icon pill (default), `text` label pill, `expand` icon+hover menu, `dropdown` icon+click menu, `switch` two-state sun/moon slider light↔dark no-auto, `cycle` single icon click-to-step); admin `collapsed` prop still forces `cycle` regardless of `style`. Shared `useThemeMode` hook + `ThemeMenu` popover; CSS for all variants in `app/globals.css` (`.theme-toggle--text`, `.theme-switch*`, `.theme-menu-wrap`/`.tt-menu*`).
- `components/consent/ConsentBanner.tsx` - GDPR banner (bottom-bar or modal): accept-all / reject-all / manage-per-category / notice-only dismiss; writes the `cactus-consent` cookie (versioned payload) + `cactus-consent-id`; POSTs `/api/consent`; re-prompts on categoriesVersion bump or reConsentDays expiry; registers `window.cactusConsent`. Props: config, privacyPolicyUrl.
- `components/EmailDeobfuscator.tsx` - client component mounted once in `app/(public)/layout.tsx`; after hydration walks every `a.cactus-eml[data-eml]` on the page, decodes the address (base64 of reversed string) and sets `href="mailto:…"`. Server half is `lib/email-obfuscate.tsx`; see Puck Integration → Email spam-protection.

Members (`components/members/`, listed with their routes above): `RegisterForm.tsx`, `LoginForm.tsx`, `TurnstileWidget.tsx`, `MemberAvatar.tsx`, `GeneratedAvatar.tsx`; `components/members/account/`: `AccountNav.tsx` (reuses `components/admin/TabStrip.tsx`), `DeletionBanner.tsx`, `ProfileSection.tsx`, `SecuritySection.tsx`, `NotificationsSection.tsx`, `ActivitySection.tsx`, `DangerZoneSection.tsx`.

Route-colocated client components (listed with their routes above): `PagesTable`, `PuckEditor`, `LayoutPuckEditor`, `DisplayConditionsPanel`, `MediaUpload`, `MediaStatsBar`, `MediaToolbar`, `MediaList`, `MediaCard`, `MediaDetailPanel`, `MediaToasts`, `MediaImageEditor`, `NotificationActions`, `UserActions`, `RolesClient`, `NavBuilder` (Settings → Navigation admin-menu builder).

### Types

No standalone `types/` directory or `.d.ts` files beyond `next-env.d.ts` (generated). Types are colocated:

- `lib/auth/session.ts` - `SessionUser` (User & {role}).
- `lib/config/env.ts` - `EnvVarStatus`, `GitHubConfigStatus`.
- `lib/consent/types.ts` - `ConsentCategory`, `ConsentBannerConfig`, `ConsentDecision`, `ConsentCookiePayload`.
- `lib/design/tokens.ts` - `DesignTokens`, `GlobalColour`, `GlobalFont`, `Typo`, `ColourPreset`, `ButtonVariantStyle`, `BadgeColourKey`, `BadgeStyle`, `BADGE_COLOUR_KEYS`.
- `lib/layout/displayConditions.ts` - `ConditionType`, `ConditionRule`, `DisplayConditions`, `RenderContext`.
- `lib/media/providers.ts` - `ProviderKind`, `ProviderEnvVar`; `lib/media/upload.ts` - `UploadResult`; `lib/media/migration.ts` - `FailedItem`, `BatchResult`.
- `lib/modules/manifest.ts` - `ModuleManifest`, `ThemeManifest` (zod-inferred).
- `lib/updates/core.ts` - `CoreUpdateStatus`, `SyncResult`, `ModuleRegistryEntry`; `lib/modules/updates.ts` - `ModuleUpdateInfo`.
- `lib/menu/resolve.ts` - `PublicMenuItem`, `MenuViewer` (`{isAuthenticated,isAdmin}`). `resolveMenu(menuId, viewer?)`/`resolveMainMenu(viewer?)` filter each item through `MenuItem.visibility` before building the tree (default viewer = anonymous). `itemVisibleTo` maps PUBLIC→all, AUTHENTICATED→signed-in, GUEST→signed-out, ADMIN→admin staff; unknown values fall through to shown.
- `lib/nav/admin-menu.ts` - `CanonicalNavItem`, `CanonicalSection`, `AdminMenuConfig`, `NavVisibility`/`NavVisibilityMode`, `ResolvedNavItem`/`ResolvedNavSection`, `EditorNavItem`/`EditorNavSection`, `ModuleNavGroup`/`ModuleManifestNav` (single source of truth for the admin sidebar; helpers `resolveAdminMenu`/`resolveAdminMenuForEditor`/`buildModuleNavGroups`/`parseAdminMenuConfig`, zod `AdminMenuConfigSchema`, consts `CORE_NAV_ITEMS`/`CORE_SECTIONS`/`CORE_NAV_PERMISSION_KEYS`).
- `lib/puck/config.tsx` - `PuckConfig`.
- `app/api/setup/env-check/route.ts` - `DatabaseState` (imported by the setup wizard).
- `workers/media-worker/index.ts` - `Env` (Worker bindings).
- Module types: `modules/contact-form/lib/types.ts`, `modules/contact-form-reply-catcher/lib/types.ts` (listed under Modules).

### Configuration Files

- `package.json` - name `cactus`, version 0.5.179, private; Node `22.x`; npm override `uuid ^11`. Scripts: dev, dev:warm, build, start, lint, typecheck, test(/watch), test:backup-roundtrip (`RUN_BACKUP_ROUNDTRIP=1 vitest run lib/backup/roundtrip.test.ts` - network + `NEON_API_KEY`, excluded from plain `npm test`), db:migrate/studio/generate/status, db:push (blocked), sync-wiki. Key deps: next ^16, react 19, @prisma/client 6, @puckeditor/core ^0.22, @simplewebauthn 13, @octokit/rest 21 + auth-app 8, AWS SDK S3, cloudinary, @imagekit/nodejs, @supabase/storage-js, @vercel/blob, @vercel/edge-config, aos, bcryptjs, dompurify + jsdom (pinned ^26), imapflow, mailparser, email-reply-parser, marked, nanoid, nodemailer, otpauth, pg, qrcode, sharp, zod, date-fns(-tz). Dev: vitest 2, eslint 9 + eslint-config-next 16, typescript 5.6, prisma 6.
- `next.config.ts` - injects `NEXT_PUBLIC_APP_VERSION` + `NEXT_TELEMETRY_DISABLED`; image remotePatterns (Worker hostname from env, cloudinary, imagekit); custom image loader file; production-only CORS header for `/_next/static/*`; security headers deliberately not here (proxy.ts).
- `proxy.ts` - see Middleware.
- `tsconfig.json` - strict, `noUncheckedIndexedAccess`, `noImplicitOverride`, bundler resolution, path alias `@/*` → `./*`; excludes `workers/media-worker`.
- `vitest.config.ts` - exists only to mirror tsconfig's `@/*` → `./*` path alias into vitest's resolver. Without it any test that (transitively) imports an app module by its `@/lib/...` specifier fails to collect with "Failed to load url @/lib/...".
- `eslint.config.mjs` - flat config, `eslint-config-next/core-web-vitals`; ignores `lib/modules/**`, `lib/puck/module-components.ts`, `.next`, `node_modules`, `.claude`.
- `prisma/schema.prisma` - see Database Schema. `prisma/migrations/20260626000000_init/migration.sql` is the single init migration, edited in place.
- `vercel.json` - AUTO-GENERATED by `generate-module-cron.mjs`, gitignored. Current content: one cron - `/api/m/contact-form-reply-catcher/cron/poll` at `0 6 * * *`.
