- `lib/modules/settings-tabs.ts` - AUTO-GENERATED by `generate-module-settings-tabs.mjs`, gitignored (covered by the `lib/modules/**` eslint ignore). Current content: one tab - `contact-form-reply-catcher`.
- `lib/modules/sms-providers.ts` - AUTO-GENERATED by `generate-module-sms-providers.mjs`, gitignored (covered by the `lib/modules/**` eslint ignore). SMS provider registry consumed by `lib/auth/sms.ts`.
- `lib/modules/extension-points.ts` - AUTO-GENERATED by `generate-module-extension-points.mjs`, gitignored (covered by the `lib/modules/**` eslint ignore). Current content: three entries - `contact-form-reply-catcher` contributing two to `contact-form.inbox-actions` and one to `contact-form.thread-messages`.
- `modules.json` - module registry committed to the repo (org `cactus-foundation-modules`), each entry `{name, repoUrl, version}` pinned to a tag: `shop` v0.1.27, `directory` v0.1.9, `boards` v0.1.9, `gazette` v0.1.9, `contact-form` v0.1.26, `twilio` v0.1.1, `gemini-watermark-remover` v0.1.7. (`contact-form-reply-catcher` exists on disk but is not in the registry.)
- `.claudeignore` - `.next/`, `node_modules/`, `prisma/migrations/`, `.git/`, `*.log`, `.env*`, `coverage/`, `dist/`, `out/`.
- No tracked `.gitignore` exists. All ignore rules live machine-locally in `.git/info/exclude`: node_modules, .next, env files, PROGRESS.md, tsbuildinfo, next-env.d.ts, .vercel, `/modules/`, `/lib/modules/router.ts`, `/lib/puck/module-components.ts`, `/vercel.json`, `.claude/`, `CLAUDE.md`, `.claudeignore` (CLAUDE.md itself is untracked).
- No `.gitmodules` - modules are build-time clones, not git submodules.
- `.env.example` - annotated reference for every env var (required/optional split, local-mode notes).
- `workers/media-worker/wrangler.toml` - Worker name `cactus-media-worker`, tsc type-check as the build command, secrets via `wrangler secret put`.
- `.claude/settings.json` - Claude Code permission allowlist + `caveman@caveman` plugin.
- `app/globals.css` - 1,719-line design system: primitive palette, semantic CSS variables (`--color-*`, `--text-*`, `--space-*`, `--radius-*`, `--shadow-*`), light/dark via `data-theme`, admin shell/nav/table/card/badge/btn/field classes, setup-shell, theme-toggle, account grid.
- `public/` - favicons (`favicon.ico/svg/-96x96.png`), `apple-touch-icon.png`, web-app manifest icons, `site.webmanifest`, `cactus.svg`.
- Root docs (untracked working notes aside): `README.md` (project readme), `PROGRESS.md` (build-phase tracker, gitignored), `cactus-design-system.md` + `cactus-design-system-visual.html` (admin design-language reference), `CLAUDE.md` (agent instructions, untracked).
- `BOARDS_SPEC.md` - full implementation spec for the planned Boards forum module (`brd_` prefix, `boards.*` permissions, publicBasePath `boards`); spec only, nothing implemented. Its final section lists protected items awaiting Chris's sign-off: core per-user notifications (see below) and the Tiptap/editor dependency question.
- `NOTIFICATIONS_SPEC.md` - DRAFT spec for extending the admin-only Notification system to per-user notifications (new `UserNotification`/`UserNotificationPrefs` models, member bell, shared `lib/notifications/user.ts` writer, digest cron). Review required before any implementation; touches core schema.
- No vitest config file; vitest runs on defaults (single test file: `lib/deploy-log-translator.test.ts`).

## Modules

Modules live in `/modules` (gitignored), cloned at build time by `scripts/checkout-modules.mjs` from the tags pinned in `modules.json`. Wiring into core is exclusively via the generated files (router, puck components, cron, settings tabs, extension points). Fourteen modules are present on disk (boards, contact-form, contact-form-reply-catcher, directory, gazette, gemini-watermark-remover, gocardless-instant-bank-pay-for-shop, product-3d-views-for-shop, product-attributes-for-shop, product-downloads-for-shop, shop, shop-variations, twilio, ultimate-seo). product-3d-views-for-shop joined the registry in v0.5.465.

**The pin is the build (v0.5.459).** The clone is `--branch <version>` at the pinned tag - "the build always gets exactly the module code the registry says it should, never silently ahead of it" - and default-branch HEAD is only the fallback for an entry with no `version` or a tag that has gone. So **releasing a module ships nothing on its own**; its `modules.json` pin has to move too. Every pin had drifted behind its module's latest release (shop v0.1.28 vs 0.1.39, shop-variations v0.1.0 vs 0.1.7, twilio v0.1.1 vs 0.1.12, …) and all eleven were reconciled to their latest release in v0.5.459. **A pin bump is not a free-standing act:** shop-variations 0.1.7 and product-attributes-for-shop 0.1.2 both declare `requiresModules: shop >= 0.1.38`, so bumping either while shop sat at v0.1.28 would have cloned a shop with no `product-editor/context` and failed the build on a missing module import. Pins joined by a `requiresModules` edge move together; check the whole graph against the pinned set and the core version (`requiresCoreVersion`) before writing.

**`npm run check:module-pins` enforces the above.** `lib/modules/pin-check.ts` is a pure planner (IO-free, mirroring `lib/updates/core-plan.ts`): given the registry, each module's latest release tag, the manifests at those tags and core's `package.json` version, it reports pins behind their release, entries with no `version` at all (the build silently takes HEAD), and - the part per-module staleness can't catch - whether the **current** and **proposed** sets actually resolve. It reuses `findUnmetModuleDependencies` (`lib/modules/dependencies.ts`, v0.5.458) and `compareVersions` rather than second-guessing them, and judges each module against the manifest **at the tag being proposed**, since 0.1.7 requiring `shop >= 0.1.38` says nothing about what 0.1.9 will require. An unread manifest is reported, never assumed dependency-free.

`lib/modules/pin-check.live.test.ts` is the network half (gh: `release list`, then the manifest via `contents/cactus.module.json?ref=<tag>`), gated on `CHECK_MODULE_PINS=1`. **It is deliberately not in the commit gate.** It needs network + gh auth, so in CI it would skip, and a check that skips where it matters is a false pass; and pin lag isn't a property of the working tree - it appears when someone *else* publishes a release, so gating commits on it would fail unrelated work. It is a manual/cron command that exits non-zero on lag, and skips cleanly (exit 0, loud warning) where gh is missing or unauthenticated. The resolution logic itself is covered offline with **no skip** in `lib/modules/pin-check.test.ts`, which encodes the v0.5.459 trap as a regression. gh calls retry 3× on transient failures (a 404 is definitive and isn't retried) - a first run failed on a blip reading a manifest that was plainly there a second later.

### Contact Form

- Slug: `contact-form` (table prefix `cf_`), repo `github.com/cactus-foundation-modules/contact-form`, manifest version 0.1.26 (registry pin v0.1.26).
- A contact form placed on any page or layout through the Puck builder, configured per-block. Submissions land in an admin inbox with read/archive state, a markdown reply composer with per-admin signatures, notification and auto-reply emails, Turnstile and per-block rate limiting, GDPR consent capture, per-block retention, and CSV export.

**Database**
Table prefix: `cf_`

- `cf_contact_submissions` - `id` (text PK, gen_random_uuid), `created_at`, `updated_at`, `name`, `email`, `phone?`, `company?`, `subject?`, `message`, `ip_address?`, `user_agent?`, `gdpr_consent` (bool, default false), `status` (text: unread | read | archived, default unread), `source_type?` (page | layout), `source_id?`, `source_block_id?` (Puck block id), `source_label?`. Indexes: status, created_at, email, (ip_address, created_at), source_block_id.
- `cf_contact_submission_replies` - `id`, `created_at`, `submission_id` FK → cf_contact_submissions (cascade), `sent_by_id` FK → core `User` (restrict), `body`, `signature_snapshot?`. Index: submission_id.
- `cf_user_profiles` - `id`, `created_at`, `updated_at`, `user_id` FK → core `User` (cascade, unique), `signature?`. One row per admin, created on first signature save.

**Permissions**

- `contact.view` - inbox pages, submission list/read/status changes.
- `contact.reply` - posting replies.
- `contact.delete` - deleting submissions (single + bulk).
- `contact.export` - CSV export.

**API Routes** (all served through `/api/m/contact-form/…` via the generated router)

- `POST /api/m/contact-form/contact/submit` - public submission endpoint. Re-derives the form config server-side from the saved Puck data (page by path/homepage, else all layouts, matching block type+id); Turnstile when enabled+configured; per-block IP rate limit; field validation per config; HTML-stripping sanitisation; stores the submission with source tracking; syncs the rolling unread notification; fires notification + optional auto-reply emails.
- `GET /api/m/contact-form/admin/submissions` - paginated list, status filter (`contact.view`).
- `PATCH /api/m/contact-form/admin/submissions` - bulk status change (`contact.view`) or bulk delete (`contact.delete`).
- `GET/PATCH/DELETE /api/m/contact-form/admin/submissions/[id]` - read (auto-marks unread→read), status patch, delete.
- `POST /api/m/contact-form/admin/submissions/[id]/reply` - stores the reply with a signature snapshot, marks read, sends the reply email (`contact.reply`).
- `GET /api/m/contact-form/admin/export` - CSV download, optional status filter (`contact.export`).
- `GET/PATCH /api/m/contact-form/admin/signature` - per-admin signature read/save (session only).
- `GET /api/m/contact-form/cron/retention` - Vercel cron target; requires `Authorization: Bearer $CRON_SECRET`; runs `runRetentionPolicy()`; returns `{ok: true, deleted: N}`.

Admin pages (served through `/cactus-admin/m/contact-form/…`): `inbox` (list, tabs, bulk actions - `SubmissionList.tsx`), `inbox/[id]` (detail + reply thread incl. caught replies + `ReplyComposer` markdown editor), `my-signature` (markdown signature editor).

Both `inbox` and `inbox/[id]` publish extension points other modules can contribute to (permission-filtered live from `Module.manifest`, resolved via the generated `lib/modules/extension-points.ts`, see `scripts/generate-module-extension-points.mjs` above): `contact-form.inbox-actions` (button row on `inbox`, left of "Edit My Signature", receives `{adminPath}`), `contact-form.submission-detail` (component block on `inbox/[id]`, rendered after the merged Replies thread and before the reply composer, receives `{submissionId}`; currently no consumers), and `contact-form.thread-messages` (data contract, not a component - contributing modules export an async `(submissionId) => Promise<ThreadMessageContribution[]>`, `{id, createdAt, senderLabel, body, badge?}` per `modules/contact-form/lib/types.ts`; core merges the results with the submission's own replies by `createdAt` into one chronological "Replies" list, giving any message with a truthy `badge` a muted `--color-bg-subtle`/`--color-border-strong` card instead of the default `--color-accent` border - `badge` is not rendered as visible text, it's purely the style trigger). `contact-form.inbox-actions` and `contact-form.thread-messages` are currently consumed only by `contact-form-reply-catcher` (Caught Replies button + inline caught-reply timeline entries, muted card colour, no visible label).

**Puck Blocks**

- `ContactForm` (client `contactFormPuckComponent`, RSC `contactFormPuckRscComponent` from `components/puck/ContactFormBlock.tsx`). Props: formTitle, introText, submitLabel, padding; showPhone/showCompany/showSubject + require* (yes/no strings), nameValidationMode (first_only | both); notificationEmail, emailNotifyMode (full | notify | off), ccEmails (newline list), autoReplyEnabled, autoReplyBody (markdown); turnstileEnabled, rateLimitEnabled, rateLimitMaxAttempts (default 3), rateLimitWindowMin (default 10); gdprConsentEnabled, gdprConsentLabel; retentionDays (0 = never); successMessage. `resolveFields` swaps the field set for a "email not configured" notice and disables the Turnstile toggle when unconfigured. Renders the public form (`ContactFormClient.tsx`) posting to the submit endpoint.

**Configuration**
Stored entirely in the Puck block's props (per form instance) inside the owning page/layout `builderData`; converted server-side by `blockPropsToConfig`. No module-global settings and no settings rows in the database.

**External Integrations**
Core email (Brevo/SMTP) for notification, auto-reply, and reply emails; Cloudflare Turnstile via core config. No credentials of its own.

**Cron Jobs**

- `0 3 * * *` (daily 03:00, clear of the reply-catcher poll at 06:00) → `/api/m/contact-form/cron/retention`; registered via `cronJobs` in `cactus.module.json`, emitted into the generated `vercel.json`. Calls `runRetentionPolicy()` (`lib/retention.ts`), which prunes `cf_contact_submissions` past each Puck block's `retentionDays` setting.

**Scripts**
None.

**Known Limitations**

- `requiredEnvVars` is empty: the form block degrades in the editor when email is unconfigured, but submissions still store even if notification emails fail.
- README's install instructions (git submodule, "Admin > Contact > Settings") describe an older mechanism; installation actually flows through the Cactus Modules admin and `modules.json`, and there is no settings page.

### Contact Form Reply Catcher

- Slug: `contact-form-reply-catcher` (table prefix `rc_`), manifest version 0.1.6. Not in `modules.json` (present on disk only; not part of the shipped registry).
- Polls the site admin's real mailbox (plain IMAP or Outlook OAuth) and threads submitter replies - and the admin's own personally-sent replies - back into the contact-form inbox, so conversations continued over ordinary email stay visible in Cactus. Read-only against the mailbox: never marks read, moves, or deletes.

**Database**
Table prefix: `rc_`

- `rc_mailbox_config` - singleton (`id = 'singleton'`): `provider` (imap | outlook_oauth, checked), `imap_host?`, `imap_port` (default 993), `imap_username?`, `imap_password_encrypted?`, `oauth_client_id_encrypted?`, `oauth_client_secret_encrypted?`, `oauth_access_token_encrypted?`, `oauth_refresh_token_encrypted?`, `oauth_token_expires_at?`, `inbox_folder?` / `sent_folder?` (null = auto-detect), `last_poll_at?`, `last_poll_status?` (ok | error), `last_poll_error?`, timestamps.
- `rc_processed_messages` - dedupe ledger: `id`, `imap_uid`, `imap_folder`, `message_id_header?`, `matched_submission_id?`, `processed_at`. Unique (imap_folder, imap_uid); index on message_id_header.
- `rc_caught_replies` - `id`, `created_at`, `submission_id` FK → `cf_contact_submissions` (cascade; one-way pointer, contact-form's schema untouched), `body`, `sender_type` (submitter | admin, checked), `external_email?`. Index: submission_id.

**Permissions**

- `replycatcher.manage` - settings tab/API, OAuth flow, check-now, caught-replies inbox pages.

**API Routes** (via `/api/m/contact-form-reply-catcher/…`)

- `GET /api/m/contact-form-reply-catcher/cron/poll` - Vercel cron target; requires `Authorization: Bearer $CRON_SECRET`; runs `pollMailbox()`.
- `POST /api/m/contact-form-reply-catcher/admin/check-now` - manual poll (`replycatcher.manage`), 60-second cooldown.
- `GET/PATCH /api/m/contact-form-reply-catcher/admin/settings` - mailbox config; secrets returned only as booleans; PATCH requires ENCRYPTION_KEY and encrypts IMAP password / OAuth client credentials at rest.
- `GET /api/m/contact-form-reply-catcher/admin/oauth/microsoft/start` - builds the Microsoft authorize URL (scope `offline_access` + `IMAP.AccessAsUser.All`), state cookie `cactus_rc_oauth_state` (10 min).
- `GET /api/m/contact-form-reply-catcher/admin/oauth/microsoft/callback` - state check, code→token exchange, stores encrypted token pair, redirects to `/<adminPath>/config?tab=contact-form-reply-catcher` with `oauth=connected|error`.

Settings live as a tab on core `/cactus-admin/config` (id `contact-form-reply-catcher`, registered via manifest `settingsTabs`, component `modules/contact-form-reply-catcher/components/SettingsTab.tsx`) rather than a standalone admin page - provider choice, IMAP/Outlook credentials, folder overrides, last-poll status, check-now, OAuth connect. Admin pages: `inbox` + `inbox/[id]` (own "Caught Replies" list + merged per-submission timeline, unchanged) only; `navEntries` is empty - no sidebar link at all any more.

Discoverability instead runs through three `extensionPoints` entries registered in `cactus.module.json` (see `scripts/generate-module-extension-points.mjs` above), all gated on `replycatcher.manage`: `contact-form.inbox-actions` → `components/CaughtRepliesButton.tsx` (a "Caught Replies" button on the core contact-form inbox list, left of "Edit My Signature", linking to this module's own `inbox` page) and `components/FetchLatestRepliesButton.tsx`; and `contact-form.thread-messages` → `lib/thread-messages.ts` (`getCaughtReplyThreadMessages`, an async function - not a component - querying `listCaughtRepliesBySubmission` and mapping to `ThreadMessageContribution[]`, `senderLabel` "You (caught from your mailbox)" for admin-sourced catches else the submitter's external email, `badge: 'Caught'` - used only to trigger the muted card styling on the core thread, not rendered as visible text). Core merges these by `createdAt` with contact-form's own replies into one chronological thread; no more separate "Caught replies" block/header (former `components/CaughtRepliesPanel.tsx`, removed).

**Puck Blocks**
None.

**Configuration**
Global, in the `rc_mailbox_config` singleton row (see Database). Secrets encrypted with core `ENCRYPTION_KEY`. Keys as columns above; defaults: `imap_port` 993, folders auto-detected (INBOX + SPECIAL-USE `\Sent`, falling back to common sent-folder names).

**External Integrations**

- IMAP mailboxes via `imapflow` (TLS, app-password auth) - any provider.
- Microsoft Outlook via user-supplied Azure app (client id/secret entered in settings): OAuth2 authorization-code + refresh flow against `login.microsoftonline.com`, XOAUTH2 IMAP to `outlook.office365.com:993`; access token auto-refreshed when within 5 minutes of expiry.
- Message parsing: `mailparser` (bodies) + `email-reply-parser` (quoted-text stripping).

**Cron Jobs**

- `0 6 * * *` (daily 06:00) → `/api/m/contact-form-reply-catcher/cron/poll`; registered via `cronJobs` in `cactus.module.json`, emitted into the generated `vercel.json`. Poll walks Inbox (sender = submitter) and Sent (sender = admin, only when genuinely from the configured address), first run limited to a 30-day lookback, then UID-incremental; matches by sender/recipient email against recent `cf_contact_submissions` preferring subject overlap; matched submitter replies mark the submission unread.

**Scripts**
None.

**Known Limitations**

- Matching is a documented best-effort heuristic (no Message-ID threading, because contact-form's schema is never touched); a genuinely new email from an address with no recent submission does not match.
- Requires `ENCRYPTION_KEY` (declared required) and `CRON_SECRET` (declared optional, but the cron endpoint returns 503 without it - only manual check-now works then).
- Hard-depends on `contact-form` ≥ 0.1.0 (enforced at install/uninstall by core).
- Vercel Hobby plan caps crons at one invocation per day, so the daily schedule is the effective floor there.

### Gazette

- Slug: `gazette` (table prefix `gz_`), repo `github.com/cactus-foundation-modules/gazette`, manifest version 0.1.9, pinned in `modules.json` to v0.1.9.
- Writing-first blog/news module: Posts with Tags, Series, comments, reactions, view counts, an RSS feed, a WordPress/Medium/Substack importer, and a Puck-based body palette (five prose-focused blocks) separate from the page-builder palette. First consumer of the new core `publicBasePath` mechanism (`publicBasePath: "gazette"` → `/gazette/*`).
- Layout system integration (core mechanism, see Puck Integration above): declares `layoutTypes` group "Gazette" with `gazetteCategory` (all 6 listing pages - index/tag/series/author/archive-year/archive-month - share this one type) and `gazetteEntry` (the single post page). 9 new Puck blocks in `components/puck/`: `GazetteCategoryHeaderBlock`, `GazetteEntryListBlock` (category, both anchors); `GazetteEntryHeaderBlock`, `GazettePostBodyBlock` (entry anchors - post body nests reactions/share buttons), `GazetteAuthorBioBlock`, `GazetteSeriesNavBlock`, `GazetteRelatedPostsBlock`, `GazetteTableOfContentsBlock`, `GazetteCommentsBlock` (entry, removable). The two pre-existing blocks `GazetteFeed`/`GazetteFeatured` are retagged `layoutTypes: ["gazetteCategory"]` (purely additive - still usable everywhere they were before). `lib/inject-category-context.ts`/`lib/inject-entry-context.ts` inject `{heading, description?, page, baseUrl, tagSlug?, seriesSlug?, authorId?, year?, month?}` / `{entrySlug}` into tagged blocks' props. `lib/starterLayouts.ts` provides 3 category + 3 entry starter templates. All 6 category pages and the entry page try `resolveThemeLayout` first, falling through to the original hardcoded JSX untouched when no starter is published. Admin Layouts page sub-tab labels are "Listing"/"Post" (not the generic "Category"/"Entry" - Gazette has no real category entity, tags/series/authors/archives all share the one listing type, and posts are always called posts elsewhere in Gazette's own admin nav) - label only, the underlying type keys are unchanged.

**Database**
Table prefix: `gz_`

- `gz_posts` - `id`, `title`, `slug` (unique), `excerpt?`, `status` (DRAFT | PUBLISHED | SCHEDULED, checked, default DRAFT), `published_at?`, `scheduled_for?`, `featured_image_id?` (Media.id, no FK), `author_id?` FK → core `User` (set null), `imported_author_name?`, `seo_title?`, `seo_description?`, `canonical_url?`, `builder_data?` (JSONB, Puck Data), `is_pinned` (default false), `is_private` (default false), `view_count` (default 0), `series_id?` FK → gz_series (set null), `series_order?`, `preview_token_hash?`, `preview_token_expires_at?`, timestamps. Indexes: (status, published_at desc), scheduled_for, author_id, (series_id, series_order), is_pinned (partial), preview_token_hash.
- `gz_series` - `id`, `title`, `slug` (unique), `description?`, timestamps.
- `gz_tags` - `id`, `name`, `slug` (unique), `created_at`. `gz_post_tags` - (post_id, tag_id) join, cascade both ways.
- `gz_author_profiles` - `id`, `user_id` FK → core `User` (cascade, unique), `bio?` (markdown), `avatar_id?`, timestamps.
- `gz_comments` - `id`, `post_id` FK → gz_posts (cascade), `parent_id?` FK → self (cascade, one level enforced in app code), `author_name`, `author_email`, `author_user_id?` FK → core `User` (set null, set when an editor replies from the admin), `body`, `status` (PENDING | APPROVED | REJECTED, checked, default PENDING), `ip_address?`, timestamps. Indexes: (post_id, status), (status, created_at desc), parent_id, (ip_address, created_at).
- `gz_reactions` - `id`, `post_id` FK → gz_posts (cascade), `emoji`, `visitor_token`, `created_at`. Unique (post_id, emoji, visitor_token).
- `gz_post_views` - `id`, `post_id` FK → gz_posts (cascade), `visitor_token`, `viewed_at`. Unique (post_id, visitor_token) - dedup gate for the view-count increment.
- `gz_settings` - singleton (`id = 'singleton'`): `posts_per_page` (default 10), `rss_enabled` (default true), `feed_title?`, `feed_description?`, `comments_enabled` (default true), `comments_visibility` (PUBLIC | MEMBERS_ONLY, checked, default PUBLIC), `comment_moderation` (PRE | POST, checked, default PRE), `comments_threaded` (default true), `reactions_enabled` (default true), `reaction_set?` (JSONB array; null falls back to code default `['👍','❤️','🔥','💡']`), `show_view_counts` (default false), `updated_at`.
- `gz_post_templates` - `id`, `title`, `builder_data?` (JSONB), timestamps.

**Permissions**

- `gazette.access` - gates all six Gazette admin sidebar links (Posts/Tags/Series/Authors/Comments/Templates). Unlike ungrouped modules (contact-form), these render under their own `admin-nav-section-label` ("Gazette", via manifest `navGroupLabel`) rather than as plain links under Dashboard - see `app/cactus-admin/layout.tsx` note above. Page-level access is independently governed by the three writing-tier permissions below - a user can have `gazette.access` with none of them (sees a "no permission" alert) or a tier with no `gazette.access` (can still deep-link to admin pages, just has no sidebar link).
- `gazette.contributor` - write/edit own posts while DRAFT only; cannot publish.
- `gazette.author` - write/edit/publish own posts.
- `gazette.editor` - edit/publish anyone's posts; manage tags, series, comments, templates, settings; reassign a post's author.
- These three tiers used to live in a module-owned `gz_user_roles` table (one row per user, at most one role each); that table is now dropped. `getGazetteAccess()` instead calls `hasPermissions(user, ['gazette.editor','gazette.author','gazette.contributor'])` against the standard core `RolePermission` table and takes the highest tier granted (Editor beats Author beats Contributor); `isAdmin` always resolves to Editor regardless. Being Role-level rather than per-user, giving two people different tiers now means giving them different core Roles - there's no way to hand one specific individual a tier without it applying to everyone sharing their Role.
- Tier assignment is therefore just the ordinary core permission matrix (Settings → Users → Roles, `RolesClient.tsx`, grouped under the "gazette" heading alongside `gazette.access`) - no more `GazetteRolesSection.tsx` card, no `core.roles-page` extension point contribution, no separate admin-only role-assignment API.

**API Routes** (all served through `/api/m/gazette/…` via the generated router)

Admin (`/api/m/gazette/admin/…`, session + permission gated per-route via `canViewGazetteAdmin`/`isAdmin`):
- `GET/POST /posts`, `GET/PATCH/DELETE /posts/[id]`, `POST /posts/bulk` (bulk delete), `POST /posts/[id]/publish` (publish | schedule | unpublish), `POST /posts/[id]/duplicate`, `POST /posts/[id]/preview-token` (regenerate; overwrites the previous hash, invalidating the old link).
- `GET/POST /tags`, `PATCH/DELETE /tags/[id]` (editor only; DELETE 409s with `{count}` if still in use).
- `GET/POST /series`, `GET/PATCH/DELETE /series/[id]`, `PATCH /series/[id]/reorder` (editor only).
- `GET /authors`, `GET/PATCH /authors/[userId]` (PATCH: editor any, else self only).
- `GET /comments`, `PATCH/DELETE /comments/[id]`, `POST /comments/[id]/reply`, `POST /comments/bulk` (editor only).
- `GET /users` (picker, editor only), `GET/POST /templates`, `PATCH/DELETE /templates/[id]` (editor only), `GET/PATCH /settings` (editor only, backs `GazetteSettingsTab.tsx` on core `/cactus-admin/config`), `POST /import` (multipart, editor only, backs the import wizard appended below that same settings tab).

Public (`/api/m/gazette/public/…`, no session required):
- `POST /comments` - zod-validated; checks post visibility, `comments_enabled`, `MEMBERS_ONLY` → session required else 403 with "Only members can comment.", Turnstile (fail-open if unconfigured), IP rate limit (5 per 10 min), threading rules; status PRE→PENDING / POST→APPROVED.
- `POST /reactions` - toggle (insert or delete on conflict), validates emoji against the configured set, returns fresh counts.
- `POST /views` - `recordView`, dedup via `gz_post_views` unique constraint before incrementing `view_count`.

Admin pages (`/cactus-admin/m/gazette/…`, all RSC-gated on `canViewGazetteAdmin`): `posts` (list, tabs/search/bulk - `PostList.tsx`), `posts/new` (template chooser), `posts/[id]` (two-column editor - `PostEditor.tsx`, embeds a gazette-only Puck config for the body), `tags`, `series`, `series/[id]` (drag-to-reorder), `authors`, `authors/[userId]`, `comments`, `templates`. No `settings`, `import`, or `roles` page any more - settings/import moved to core `/cactus-admin/config` (Gazette tab, import wizard appended beneath it); role/tier assignment folded into the ordinary permission matrix on core Settings → Users → Roles (no dedicated page or extension-point section needed any more). `GazetteNav.tsx` (the in-page tab bar across these six pages) now only lists Posts/Tags/Series/Authors/Comments/Templates.

Public pages (`/gazette/…`, via the core `publicBasePath` mechanism, `force-dynamic`): index (paginated, pinned-first), `[slug]` (post - TOC, reading time, reactions, share buttons, series nav, author bio, related posts, comments), `tag/[slug]`, `series/[slug]`, `archive/[year]`, `archive/[year]/[month]`, `preview/[token]` (no auth, `noindex`), `feed.xml` (RSS 2.0, 20 items), `author/[username]` (new - lists an author's published posts + bio; backs the "Author" menu-link kind, also linkable directly).

**Extension Points**
- `core.menu-entity-provider` (id `gazette`, `lib/menu-entity-provider.ts` → `gazetteMenuEntityProvider`) - lets the admin Menus builder link to a post/tag/series/author. `getVisiblePosts()` in `lib/db.ts` gained an `authorId` filter to back the new author page.

**Puck Blocks**

- `GazetteFeed` (client `gazetteFeedPuckComponent`, RSC `gazetteFeedPuckRscComponent` from `components/puck/GazetteFeedBlock.tsx`) - registered in the manifest, appears in the site-wide "Modules" palette. Layout (Grid/List/Compact), count, tag filter (resolved live from `/api/m/gazette/admin/tags`), show excerpt/author/date/image toggles, "Read more" label. RSC render calls `connection()` first so any page embedding it renders dynamically.
- `GazetteFeatured` (client `gazetteFeaturedPuckComponent`, RSC `gazetteFeaturedPuckRscComponent`) - source (Latest/Pinned), layout (Hero/Card/Minimal). Same `connection()` treatment.
- Body palette (module-internal, NOT in the manifest, only used inside the post editor's own embedded Puck config): `GazetteProse` (richtext, heading levels 2-4 only, code/codeBlock/strike/underline/horizontalRule/textAlign disabled - no Image extension available, see Known Limitations), `GazettePullQuote`, `GazetteCode` (editor: plain `<pre>`; RSC: `shiki` `codeToHtml` with `createCssVariablesTheme`, `--gz-shiki-*` CSS variables), `GazetteImage` (custom media-picker field, editor-only), `GazetteDivider`.

**Configuration**
Global, in the `gz_settings` singleton row (see Database). No `requiredEnvVars`.

**External Integrations**
Core Turnstile (comment spam check, fail-open if unconfigured), core media (`Media.id` for featured images/avatars), `shiki` (core dependency, added for this module) for code-block highlighting.

**Cron Jobs**
None - scheduled posts go live lazily: `PUBLIC_VISIBLE_SQL` treats a SCHEDULED row as visible once `scheduled_for <= NOW()`, and `normaliseScheduledPosts()` opportunistically flips the DB status to PUBLISHED on admin reads/writes. No Vercel Cron needed for correctness.

**Scripts**
None.

**Known Limitations**

- `@tiptap/extension-image` is not a transitive dependency of `@puckeditor/core` and modules can't add npm packages, so the prose richtext schema has no Image node - an `<img>` inside imported HTML is silently dropped rather than embedded (images are handled as a separate `GazetteImage` block instead).
- `MEMBERS_ONLY` comment visibility currently just means "any logged-in core user" - there's no public membership system yet. Documented as designed interim behaviour in `wiki/Gazette.md`, not a bug.
- Zip imports (Medium/Substack raw exports) aren't supported - no zip dependency available to modules. Admins unzip first and select the extracted files.
- `teardown` in the manifest correctly lists literal snake_case table names (`gz_posts` etc) - contact-form's manifest gets this wrong (PascalCase); do not copy that pattern.

### Boards

- Slug: `boards` (table prefix `brd_`), repo `github.com/cactus-foundation-modules/boards`, manifest version 0.1.9, pinned in `modules.json` to v0.1.9.
- A discussion forum: boards, one level of sub-boards, threads and replies for registered users, with polls, reactions, subscriptions, bookmarks, read tracking, full-text search, moderation (queue/reports/bans/IP bans/log), a phpBB/Discourse importer, RSS feeds and a daily email digest. Thread openers are composed with a module-internal Puck body palette (six blocks), separate from the page-builder palette; replies use a standalone richtext composer (not Puck). First consumer of a generic core dashboard-widget extension point and of two new generic nested `feed.xml` core delegates (see Routes and Admin UI sections above).
- Layout system integration (core mechanism, see Puck Integration above; Boards' first-ever `puckBlocks`): declares `layoutTypes` group "Boards" with `boardsCategory` (board and sub-board listing pages share this one type) and `boardsEntry` (the thread page). 6 new blocks in `components/puck/`: `BoardHeaderBlock` (anchor), `SubBoardListBlock` (removable - renders null on a sub-board page), `ThreadListBlock` (anchor) for category; `ThreadHeaderBlock`, `ThreadBodyBlock` (anchors - body nests share/subscribe buttons), `ReplyListBlock` (anchor, `delete:false` - replies are core content) for entry. `lib/inject-category-context.ts` injects `{boardSlug, subBoardSlug?, kind: 'board'|'sub-board', page}`; `lib/inject-entry-context.ts` injects `{threadSlug, boardSlug, page, sort?}`. `lib/starterLayouts.ts` provides 3 category + 3 entry starters. Out of scope for this pass (lower-priority/structurally different): the top-level `/boards` index, `tag/[slug]`, `u/[username]`. Board/sub-board/thread pages try `resolveThemeLayout` first (after the existing visibility/status gating), falling through to the original hardcoded JSX untouched when no starter is published. Admin Layouts page sub-tab labels are "Board"/"Thread" (not the generic "Category"/"Entry" - matches Boards' own vocabulary elsewhere, e.g. its "Threads"/"Structure" nav entries) - label only, the underlying type keys are unchanged.

**Database**
Table prefix: `brd_` (29 tables)

- `brd_categories` - `id`, `title`, `position`, timestamps.
- `brd_boards` - `id`, `category_id?` FK → brd_categories (set null), `title`, `slug` (unique), `description?`, `position`, `icon_emoji?`, `icon_media_id?` (Media.id, no FK), `is_locked`, `visibility` (PUBLIC | MEMBERS | PRIVATE, checked, default PUBLIC - sub-boards inherit, no column of their own), `noindex` (per-board search-engine opt-out, independent of visibility), `min_post_length?`, `word_filter?` (JSONB lowercase term array), timestamps.
- `brd_sub_boards` - `id`, `board_id` FK → brd_boards (cascade), `title`, `slug` (unique per board), `description?`, `position`, `is_locked`, timestamps. One level of nesting only.
- `brd_tags` - `id`, `name`, `slug` (unique), `created_at`.
- `brd_threads` - `id`, `board_id` FK → brd_boards (cascade), `sub_board_id?` FK → brd_sub_boards (cascade), `title`, `slug` (unique, globally), `author_id?` FK → core `User` (set null), `author_name` (snapshot), `opener_data?` (JSONB, Puck Data), `status` (PUBLISHED | PENDING | HIDDEN | DELETED | ARCHIVED, checked), `is_pinned`, `is_locked`, `is_global_announcement`, `view_count`, `reply_count` (denormalised), `last_post_at?` (denormalised, set on post creation only), `ip_address?`, `imported_from?`, timestamps. Indexes incl. GIN full-text on `title`.
- `brd_posts` - replies; opener body lives on the thread row. `id`, `thread_id` FK → brd_threads (cascade), `author_id?` FK → User (set null), `author_name` (snapshot), `body_html`, `body_source?` (JSONB, editor doc), `reply_to_post_id?` FK → self (set null, flat quoted-reply pointer), `status` (PUBLISHED | PENDING | HIDDEN | DELETED, checked), `edited_at?`, `edited_by?` FK → User (set null), `ip_address?`, `imported_from?`, timestamps. GIN full-text on `body_html`.
- `brd_post_revisions` - `id`, `post_id` FK → brd_posts (cascade), `body_html`, `body_source?`, `edited_by?` FK → User (set null), `created_at`.
- `brd_thread_tags` - (thread_id, tag_id) composite PK, cascade both ways.
- `brd_drafts` - composer auto-save. `id`, `user_id` FK → User (cascade), `thread_id?` FK → brd_threads (cascade, reply drafts), `board_id?` FK → brd_boards (cascade, new-thread drafts), `title?`, `opener_data?`, `body_source?`, timestamps. Partial unique on (user_id, thread_id) WHERE thread_id IS NOT NULL.
- `brd_post_reactions` - registered users only (not visitor-token, unlike Gazette). `id`, `post_id` FK → brd_posts (cascade), `user_id` FK → User (cascade), `emoji`, `created_at`. Unique (post_id, user_id, emoji).
- `brd_thread_views` - anonymous view dedupe, mirrors `gz_post_views` + cookie `cactus-boards-vid`. Unique (thread_id, visitor_token).
- `brd_bookmarks` - `id`, `thread_id` FK → brd_threads (cascade), `user_id` FK → User (cascade), `created_at`. Unique (thread_id, user_id).
- `brd_read_state` - `user_id` FK → User (cascade), `thread_id` FK → brd_threads (cascade), `last_read_post_at`, `updated_at`. Composite PK.
- `brd_polls` - one per thread. `id`, `thread_id` FK → brd_threads (cascade, unique), `question`, `allow_multiple`, `closes_at?`, `created_at`.
- `brd_poll_options` - `id`, `poll_id` FK → brd_polls (cascade), `label`, `position`.
- `brd_poll_votes` - `id`, `option_id` FK → brd_poll_options (cascade), `poll_id` FK → brd_polls (cascade), `user_id` FK → User (cascade), `created_at`. Unique (option_id, user_id).
- `brd_user_profiles` - forum identity, deleted with the user. `id`, `user_id` FK → User (cascade, unique), `username` (unique), `signature?`, `avatar_id?` (Media.id, no FK), `bio?`, `post_count` (denormalised), `last_seen_at?`, timestamps.
- `brd_bans` - `id`, `user_id` FK → User (cascade), `reason?`, `expires_at?` (null = indefinite), `created_by?`, `created_at`.
- `brd_ip_bans` - `id`, `ip_address` (unique), `reason?`, `expires_at?`, `created_by?`, `created_at`.
- `brd_moderation_queue` - `id`, `item_type` (THREAD | POST, checked), `item_id` (no FK, polymorphic), `reason`, `status` (OPEN | APPROVED | REJECTED, checked), `resolved_by?` FK → User (set null), `resolved_at?`, `created_at`.
- `brd_reports` - member-filed flags, same polymorphic shape as the queue plus `reporter_id?` FK → User (set null), `status` (OPEN | RESOLVED | DISMISSED, checked).
- `brd_moderation_log` - append-only audit. `id`, `actor_id?` FK → User (set null), `actor_name` (snapshot), `action`, `item_type?` (free text - THREAD/POST/USER, no CHECK, unlike the queue/reports tables), `item_id?`, `detail?` (JSONB), `created_at`.
- `brd_thread_subscriptions`, `brd_board_subscriptions` - same (item_id, user_id) shape, cascade both ways, unique pair.
- `brd_notification_prefs` - `user_id` PK FK → User (cascade), `mode` (IMMEDIATE | DIGEST | OFF, checked, default IMMEDIATE), `email_enabled`, `last_digest_at?`, `updated_at`.
- `brd_thread_templates` - mirrors `gz_post_templates`: `id`, `title`, `builder_data?`, timestamps.
- `brd_import_jobs` - `id`, `source` (PHPBB | DISCOURSE, checked), `status` (PENDING | RUNNING | DONE | FAILED, checked), `stats?` (JSONB), `error?`, `created_by?`, timestamps.
- `brd_settings` - singleton (`id = 'singleton'`): `threads_per_page` (20), `posts_per_page` (20), `rss_enabled` (true), `feed_title?`, `feed_description?`, `reactions_enabled` (true), `reaction_set?` (JSONB, null falls back to code default `['👍','❤️','🔥','💡']`), `signatures_enabled` (true), `signature_max_length` (500), `min_account_age_days` (0), `first_post_count` (3), `first_post_account_age_days` (7), `post_cooldown_seconds` (30), `posts_per_hour_limit` (20), `edit_window_minutes` (0 = unlimited), `show_view_counts` (true), `updated_at`.

**Permissions**

- `boards.access` - the Boards admin sidebar section (Threads/Structure/Moderation/Analytics nav entries) and baseline module admin screens.
- `boards.manage` - structural admin (boards/sub-boards/categories/tags/templates CRUD, settings, imports); also gates the `settingsTabs`-registered "Boards" tab on core `/cactus-admin/config`.
- `boards.moderate` - the full moderator toolkit, sitewide: hide/delete/lock/pin/archive/move/split threads and posts, resolve reports, bans/IP bans, global announcements. Replaces the old `brd_moderator_assignments` table (module-side, one row per user per board plus an optional Global Moderator row - dropped entirely). `BoardsAccess` is now just `{ isAdminUser, canModerate }`; `canModerate` is sitewide only - there is no more per-board scoping and no more separate "Global Moderator" tier, a user either can moderate every board or none. Assigned like any other permission from core Settings → Users → Roles; the standalone `/cactus-admin/m/boards/moderators` page, its API routes, and the `Moderators` sidebar tab are all gone.

**API Routes** (all served through `/api/m/boards/…` via the generated router)

Admin (`/api/m/boards/admin/…`): full CRUD for `categories`, `boards` (+ `reorder`), `sub-boards`, `tags`; `threads` list/patch/delete + `pin`/`lock`/`archive`/`move`/`split`/`announce` actions (`boards.moderate`-gated); `posts` list/patch/delete + `revisions` (moderator hard-delete vs public author soft-delete); `threads/bulk` and `posts/bulk` (hide/delete/lock/archive/move/approve/reject, `{done, skipped}` response); `users/[id]/warn`; `moderation/queue` + per-item approve/reject; `reports` + per-item resolve/dismiss; `bans`/`ip-bans` CRUD; `moderation/log` (read-only); `users` picker; `templates` CRUD; `settings`; `import` (multipart, creates a `brd_import_jobs` row, processes synchronously within the request - same platform constraint as Gazette's importer) + `import/[jobId]` poll; `analytics`; `dashboard-summary` (feeds the core widget).

Public (`/api/m/boards/public/…`): `POST /threads` (submission gauntlet: ban/IP-ban/account-age → lock check → min length → Turnstile → cooldown/hourly rate limit → word-filter/new-account moderation queue gate; materialises polls, tags, fires mention + board-subscriber notifications); `POST /threads/[id]/posts` (same gauntlet, quote + mention + thread-subscriber notifications, bumps `reply_count`/`last_post_at`); `PATCH/DELETE /posts/[id]` (author within `edit_window_minutes` or moderator; author delete is soft, renders "Post removed"); `POST /posts/[id]/reactions` (toggle); `POST /threads/[id]/views` (visitor-token dedupe); `POST /polls/[id]/votes` (toggle, enforces `allow_multiple`/`closes_at`); `PUT/DELETE /subscriptions/thread|board/[id]`; `GET /bookmarks`, `PUT/DELETE /bookmarks/thread/[id]`; `PUT/GET/DELETE /drafts`; `POST /threads/[id]/read`, `POST /boards/[id]/read` (bulk mark-read); `POST /reports`; `GET /search` (Postgres `ts_rank`, scoped to boards visible to the requester); `GET/PATCH /profile` (username settable once, then admin-only); `GET /account/export` (GDPR JSON); plus small read-only `GET /tags` and `GET /templates` backing the public composer's tag picker and template chooser (not in the original spec table, added because the composer needs them).

Cron: `GET|POST /api/m/boards/cron/digest` (`Authorization: Bearer $CRON_SECRET`) - both methods accepted since Vercel Cron always invokes via GET (same as contact-form's retention cron) while BOARDS_SPEC labels the endpoint POST; `lib/digest.ts` `runDigest()` emails `DIGEST`-mode subscribers their new subscribed-board threads and subscribed-thread replies since `last_digest_at`.

Admin pages (`/cactus-admin/m/boards/…`, tab bar `BoardsNav.tsx`): `threads` (the manifest nav-entry landing page - list/filter/bulk moderation), `structure` (sub-tabbed via shared `TabStrip`: Categories/Boards/Sub-boards/Tags/Templates, `boards.manage`), `moderation` (sub-tabbed via shared `TabStrip`: Queue/Reports/Bans/IP Bans/Log), `analytics` (`boards.access`). No `moderators` page any more - moderator status is now a plain `boards.moderate` permission assigned from core Settings → Users → Roles, same as everything else. `settings` and `import` pages removed - moved into a `settingsTabs`-registered "Boards" tab on core `/cactus-admin/config` (`BoardsSettingsTab.tsx`, replacing the old `SettingsScreen.tsx`), with the import wizard appended below it, same reshuffle Gazette got.

Public pages (`/boards/…`, via the core `publicBasePath` mechanism): index (categories/boards/sub-boards, global announcements strip, search - `?q=` re-renders the same page as search results rather than a new route; category sections gained an `id="cat-{id}"` anchor so a menu link can jump straight to one), `[board]` (sub-board list + thread list, inline "New Thread" composer toggle), `[board]/[sub]`, `t/[slug]` (opener via Puck RSC incl. live poll results, tags, share buttons, subscribe/bookmark, reactions, paginated replies with oldest/newest sort toggle, reply composer, inline moderator controls), `tag/[slug]` (new - lists PUBLISHED threads carrying a tag, scoped to boards visible to the requester; boards has no dedicated category page, unlike Gazette/Directory, so only tags got a real archive route), `u/[username]` (public profile), `feed.xml` + `[board]/feed.xml` + `[board]/[sub]/feed.xml` (RSS, `PUBLIC` non-`noindex` boards only).

**Extension Points**
- `core.menu-entity-provider` (id `boards`, `lib/menu-entity-provider.ts` → `boardsMenuEntityProvider`) - lets the admin Menus builder link to a category, board, sub-board or tag.

**Puck Blocks**

Thread-opener-only body palette (module-internal, NOT in the manifest, mirrors Gazette's body palette pattern): `BoardsProse` (richtext, headings 2-4, no image node - same restricted schema as `GazetteProse`), `BoardsPullQuote`, `BoardsCode` (editor `<pre>`, RSC `shiki` highlighted, `--brd-shiki-*` CSS variables), `BoardsImage` (media-picker field), `BoardsPoll` (question/options/allow-multiple/closes-at; the thread API materialises it into `brd_polls`/`brd_poll_options` on save; RSC render swaps to a `makeBoardsPollRscFieldDef(pollContext)` factory - same technique as Gazette's TOC heading injection - so public rendering shows live vote counts via `PollWidget.tsx` instead of the authored draft options), `BoardsEmbed` (URL field, whitelist-rendered YouTube/Vimeo iframes else a plain link card, no oEmbed fetching).

Replies don't use Puck at all - the standalone `ReplyComposer.tsx` embeds a minimal single-block Puck instance (`ReplyBody`, reusing `boardsProseFieldDef`) purely to get the same richtext field without a new `@tiptap/*` dependency (BOARDS_SPEC protected item 2); the full page-builder chrome this drags in in this speed edition is a known rough edge, not hidden.

**Configuration**
Global, in the `brd_settings` singleton row (see Database), edited via the "Boards" tab on core `/cactus-admin/config` (`BoardsSettingsTab.tsx`, `settingsTabs` manifest entry, `boards.manage`) - same pattern as Gazette, no longer a standalone module admin page. Per-board config (lock, visibility, icon, min post length, word filter, ordering) lives as columns on `brd_boards`/`brd_sub_boards`, edited in the Structure screen.

**External Integrations**
Core Turnstile (submission gauntlet, fail-open if unconfigured), core media (`Media.id` for avatars/board icons/inline images), core email (Brevo/SMTP) for the daily digest and immediate-mode notification emails, `shiki` (existing core dependency) for code-block highlighting.

**Cron Jobs**
`0 7 * * *` → `/api/m/boards/cron/digest`; registered via `cronJobs` in `cactus.module.json`, emitted into the generated `vercel.json`.

**Scripts**
None.

**Known Limitations**

- Per BOARDS_SPEC protected item 1, per-user notifications degrade to email-only (`lib/notify.ts` `notifyUser`) - no bell, no in-app read/unread - until the separate core per-user notification system (`NOTIFICATIONS_SPEC.md`) ships; `DIGEST`-mode users get the daily email, `OFF` suppresses everything, and there is currently no admin-visible notification history at all for Boards items.
- The import wizard (`POST /import`) processes synchronously within the request (`maxDuration = 60`), same as Gazette's importer - very large forum exports may exceed the Vercel function timeout. Idempotent via `imported_from` on threads/posts (safe to re-run); boards/categories are matched by title, not a source id, since `brd_boards` has no `imported_from` column.
- `ReplyComposer.tsx` embeds a full Puck editor instance (with its default component-picker chrome) to reuse the richtext field for a single always-present block, rather than a purpose-built minimal text box - a deliberate corner cut per BOARDS_SPEC protected item 2 ("start with the zero-new-dependency Puck richtext path").
- The two new generic nested `feed.xml` core delegates (`app/(public)/[slug]/[a]/feed.xml/route.ts`, `.../[a]/[b]/feed.xml/route.ts`) introduce dynamic segment names (`[a]`, `[b]`) as siblings of the existing `[...path]` catch-all under `app/(public)/[slug]/` - confirmed via a full `next build` that Next.js does not treat a `route.ts`-only dynamic segment as conflicting with a `page.tsx` catch-all at the same directory level (only same-file-type siblings need matching dynamic names).

### Directory

- Slug: `directory` (table prefix `dir_`), repo `github.com/cactus-foundation-modules/directory`, manifest version 0.1.9, pinned in `modules.json` to v0.1.9.
- Map-based listings module: Categories (drag-to-reorder, emoji icon, entry-count guard against deletion), Entries (draft/published, Featured with an optional auto-expiring `featured_until`, free-text geocoding via Nominatim - no API key, just a site-name User-Agent header - multi-image picker, tags, a Puck-based single-block description palette), a public directory front page with a Leaflet/OpenStreetMap map (marker-clustered, custom coloured div-icon pins, no default-marker-asset bundler issues since no PNG icons are used), per-category pages (area filter, sort, client-side keyword search), draft preview links (Gazette's `preview.ts` mechanism verbatim - `sha256(token + SESSION_SECRET)`, 7-day expiry, no `ENCRYPTION_KEY`), and a hand-rolled CSV importer (no `papaparse` - not a dependency anywhere in this codebase, modules can't add npm packages).
- Layout system integration (core mechanism, first of the three - see Puck Integration above): declares `layoutTypes` group "Directory" with `directoryCategory`/`directoryEntry`. 7 new blocks in `components/puck/`: `DirectoryCategoryHeader`, `DirectoryEntryBrowser` (category anchors), `DirectoryCategoryMap` (category, removable); `DirectoryEntryHeader` (entry anchor - also folds in the entry's rich description/tags, which the plan's block list didn't separately cover), `DirectoryContactCard`, `DirectoryLocationMap`, `DirectoryRelatedEntries` (entry, removable). Each block renders its own `<DirectoryStyles/>` since the shared `dir-*` CSS classes are otherwise only injected by the page-level fallback JSX. `lib/inject-category-context.ts` injects `{categorySlug, categoryId, area?, sort?}`; `lib/inject-entry-context.ts` injects `{entrySlug, categorySlug}`. `lib/starterLayouts.ts` provides 3 category + 3 entry starters. Both public pages try `resolveThemeLayout` first, falling through to the original hardcoded JSX untouched when no starter is published.

**Database**
Table prefix: `dir_`

- `dir_categories` - `id`, `name`, `slug` (unique), `description?`, `icon?` (free-text emoji), `display_order` (default 0), timestamps.
- `dir_entries` - `id`, `category_id` FK → dir_categories (**ON DELETE RESTRICT** - a category with entries in it cannot be deleted, by design; no confirm-to-override), `name`, `slug` (unique), `short_description?`, `description?` (JSONB, Puck Data - a single vendored `DirectoryProse` richtext block, module-private Puck config, not in the manifest's `puckBlocks`), `status` (draft | published, checked, default draft), `featured` (default false), `featured_until?` (cleared by the daily cron once past), `lat?`/`lng?` (NUMERIC(9,6)), `address?`, `area?`, `sub_area?`, `route_marker?` (NUMERIC(5,2), optional ordering value for route-style categories), `phone?`, `email?`, `website?`, `images` (JSONB array of `Media.id`, default `[]`, no FK - first entry is the cover), `tags` (JSONB array of strings, default `[]` - **not** `TEXT[]`, see note below), `preview_token_hash?`, `preview_token_expires_at?`, timestamps. Indexes: category_id, status, featured, area, preview_token_hash.
- `dir_settings` - singleton (`id = 'singleton'`): `intro_text?`, `map_centre_lat` (default 51.505), `map_centre_lng` (default -0.09), `map_zoom` (default 11), `featured_label` (default 'Featured'), `csv_import_enabled` (default true), `updated_at`.
- `tags` is JSONB rather than a Postgres `TEXT[]` deliberately - no `TEXT[]` column exists anywhere else in this codebase, and `$queryRaw` tagged-template parameterisation of a raw JS array against a native Postgres array type is unproven here, so it follows the same `${JSON.stringify(x)}::jsonb` pattern already used for `images` and Gazette's `gz_settings.reaction_set`.
- **PROTECTED at time of writing**: `migrations/001_initial.sql` is written and left on disk but has **not** been executed against the shared Neon test DB, and no `Module` DB row has been inserted - both need Chris's review of the SQL first (per the module's build plan's explicit review gate), separate from the code itself being complete.

**Permissions**

- `directory.access` - see the Directory sidebar section (Entries/Categories) and its dashboard summary widget.
- `directory.manage` - create/edit/delete categories and entries, change settings, run CSV imports. Checked via the standard `hasPermission(user, 'directory.manage')` against core `RolePermission` - no bespoke per-user tiers like Gazette's old contributor/author/editor system.

**API Routes** (all served through `/api/m/directory/…` via the generated router)

Admin (`/api/m/directory/admin/…`, session + `directory.access`/`directory.manage` gated per-route):
- `GET/POST /categories`, `PATCH/DELETE /categories/[id]` (DELETE 409s with `{entryCount}` if the category still has entries - no confirm-to-override, matches the DB's RESTRICT FK), `PATCH /categories/reorder`, `GET /categories/check-slug`.
- `GET/POST /entries` (list: category/status/featured/missingLocation/q filters + pagination), `GET/PATCH/DELETE /entries/[id]`, `POST /entries/[id]/duplicate`, `POST /entries/[id]/preview-token` (regenerate; overwrites the previous hash, invalidating the old link), `DELETE /entries/bulk`, `PATCH /entries/bulk-status`, `GET /entries/tags` (distinct tags across all entries), `POST /entries/import` (CSV rows already parsed/validated client-side; always inserts as drafts; per-row errors returned, not thrown).
- `POST /geocode` (server-side Nominatim proxy - `directory.manage` gated so the free lookup service isn't exposed to arbitrary callers), `GET/PATCH /settings`.

Public (`/api/m/directory/public/…`, no session required): `GET /entries` (published map pins, optional `?category=` slug filter) - currently unused by the shipped public pages (which fetch pins server-side directly via `lib/db.ts`), kept for any future client-side dynamic map reload.

Admin pages (`/cactus-admin/m/directory/…`): `entries` (list - `EntriesScreen.tsx`; skeleton-row loading state, result count + "Clear filters", clickable rows open the editor, ⚠️ flag on rows missing lat/lng, `?category=` query param preselects the category filter for deep-links from Categories), `entries/new` / `entries/[id]` (editor - `EntryEditor.tsx`, embeds the module-private Puck config for the description field; transient "Saved ✓" confirmation, error banner auto-scrolls into view, "View live ↗" link once published, preview-link button shows "Link copied ✓"), `entries/import` (CSV wizard - `CsvImport.tsx`, redirects to the entries list if `csv_import_enabled` is off; drag-and-drop drop zone plus a "Download example CSV" template button, "Choose another file"/"Import another file" resets, post-import "View entries" link), `categories` (`CategoriesScreen.tsx` - drag-to-reorder plus ↑/↓ buttons as a non-drag alternative, entry count links through to the entries list filtered to that category). No modal/overlay system used anywhere except the multi-select image picker (`EntryImagesField.tsx`, generalises core's `MediaPickerField.tsx` single-select overlay pattern) - everything else is inline-edit-in-table, matching Boards/Gazette convention.

Public pages (`/directory/…`, via the core `publicBasePath` mechanism): index (category grid + full map + "All listings" heading with a result count + paginated flat list, featured pinned first), `[category]` (category page - breadcrumb back to the directory index, collapsible filtered map, area filter, sort incl. route-marker order when any entry has one set, client-side keyword search with a live result count; 404s if the category has zero published entries, independent of any area-filter result), `[category]/[slug]` (entry detail - breadcrumb trail, gallery/cover with real `alt` text, Puck-rendered description, contact card with a `tel:` link for phone, single-pin location map plus a "Get directions ↗" link to Google Maps (coords if set, else the address), tag chips; 404s on missing/wrong-category/draft), `preview/[token]` (hash lookup, `noindex`, renders regardless of status with a warning banner - Gazette's preview-page pattern verbatim). Breadcrumb/section-heading/result-count styling lives in shared `.dir-breadcrumb`/`.dir-section-heading`/`.dir-result-count` classes in `DirectoryStyles.tsx`.

**Extension Points**
- `core.admin-dashboard-widgets` (id `directory-summary`) - dashboard summary widget.
- `core.menu-entity-provider` (id `directory`, `lib/menu-entity-provider.ts` → `directoryMenuEntityProvider`) - lets the admin Menus builder link to a category or a listing.

**Puck Blocks**

- No manifest-registered `puckBlocks` (nothing site-embeddable, unlike Gazette's `GazetteFeed`/`GazetteFeatured`).
- Module-private only (not in the manifest, only used inside the entry editor's own embedded Puck config and the public/preview RSC render): `DirectoryProse` - one block, richtext only (heading levels 2-4, code/codeBlock/strike/underline/horizontalRule/textAlign all disabled), same minimal single-block shape as Gazette/Boards' own prose blocks but with no pull-quote/code/image/divider siblings, since the spec only calls for one rich-text field per entry.

**Configuration**
Global, in the `dir_settings` singleton row (see Database), edited via the "Directory" tab on core `/cactus-admin/config` (`DirectorySettingsTab.tsx`, `settingsTabs` manifest entry, `directory.manage`). No `requiredEnvVars` - geocoding needs no API key, just a `User-Agent` header built from the site's own configured name.

**External Integrations**
OpenStreetMap Nominatim (free geocoding, no key, `User-Agent: "<siteName> (Cactus Directory)"` per Nominatim's usage policy), OpenStreetMap tile server (public map tiles, no key), core media (`Media.id` for the ordered `images` array, no FK), `leaflet` + `leaflet.markercluster` (new **core** runtime dependencies - modules compile inside core's Next build so map-rendering deps had to land in core `package.json`, the only core code diff this module needed besides `FIELD_NOTES.md`/wiki, precedent: `shiki` was added the same way for Gazette).

**Cron Jobs**
`0 1 * * *` → `/api/m/directory/cron/expire-featured` (clears `featured`/`featured_until` on any entry whose `featured_until` has passed); registered via `cronJobs` in `cactus.module.json`, emitted into the generated `vercel.json`. `CRON_SECRET` bearer-gated, same pattern as Boards' digest cron.

**Scripts**
None.

**Known Limitations**

- CSV import validation (required fields, lat/lng ranges, email/website format, parseable `featured_until`, duplicate-name-within-file) runs entirely client-side against the parsed file before the "ready" rows are POSTed; the server re-validates via the same zod schema but does not repeat the duplicate-within-file check (a DB-level clash is impossible anyway since `ensureUniqueEntrySlug` auto-suffixes).
- The multi-image picker (`EntryImagesField.tsx`) has no existing multi-select precedent anywhere else in the codebase to follow - it's a from-scratch generalisation of `lib/puck/MediaPickerField.tsx`'s single-select `MediaPickerModal` overlay, not a shared core component.
- `leaflet`/`leaflet.markercluster` default marker icon assets are deliberately not used (they resolve via relative image paths that don't survive Next's bundler without extra webpack config) - pins are plain CSS-coloured `L.divIcon` circles instead, sidestepping the issue entirely rather than configuring asset resolution.

### Shop

- Slug: `shop` (table prefix `shp_`), repo `github.com/cactus-foundation-modules/shop`, manifest version 0.1.43, pinned in `modules.json` to v0.1.43.
- **Product image filing (v0.1.36, fixed v0.1.41):** images belong in `Shop / <master category> / <product> / <slug><n>`, and v0.1.36 filed them there on save via `reorganiseProductMedia`. In practice they sat in the library root, because two things fought it: the editor's `MediaPickerModal` POSTed to core `/api/admin/media` with **no `folderId`**, so every upload landed in the root by definition; and the same modal listed the library with no `folder` param, which `parseLibraryQuery` defaults to the **root scope**, so any image the save did file correctly then vanished from the picker - making the root look like the only place an image could live. v0.1.41: `getProductMediaFolderId(productId, {folderProductId?, masterCategoryId?})` is split out of `reorganiseProductMedia` (one definition of the target folder, shared by both paths) and exposed as `POST app/api/admin/products/[id]/media-folder` (gate `shop.products`, optional `masterCategoryId` query so a first upload follows the category picked on screen, not the last-saved one). POST, not GET, because it creates the folder: `MediaPanel` hands the picker a `resolveFolderId` callback that it calls **per upload** rather than on mount, so nothing is created for a product whose Images tab was merely opened and no upload can race ahead of a pre-fetched id. The picker appends the answer to the upload FormData and lists with `folder=all&type=image`. Save-time filing stays as the backstop for renames, reorders and category changes, but its per-image `catch` now `console.warn`s instead of swallowing silently - that silence is why every image sat in the root with nothing reporting a problem. Relies only on core media APIs from v0.5.338 (`folderId` on the media POST, `folder=all` on the GET), the same release `reorganiseProductMedia` already needed, so no new core-version floor.
- **Variations hooks (v0.1.26):** shop gained three generic, reusable capabilities with `shop-variations` as the live consumer (nothing variations-specific in shop): (1) the `catalogue_hidden` product flag + `excludeHidden` filter on `listProducts` (public grid/search, admin product list, sitemap and product export all pass `true`; the public product page/route 404 a hidden row); (2) a `shop.product-editor-sections` component slot rendered below `<ProductEditor/>` on `app/cactus-admin/shop/products/[id]/page.tsx` (mirrors `shop.order-messages`); (3) a `shop.cart-line-resolver` **server-function** extension point (precedent: `contact-form.thread-messages`) consumed in `lib/checkout.ts` - `lib/line-meta.ts` collects registered resolvers, and `resolveCartLines` calls each with `(product, line.meta)`, folding a server-authoritative `priceAdjust` into `unitPrice` and a normalised `persistMeta` onto the line (failing the line on invalid input). `CartLine` gained `lineId?`/`meta?` (personalised lines merge by `lineId`, plain lines by `productId` as before), `shp_order_items.line_meta` persists it, and shop renders the `{label,value,href?}` pairs generically wherever it lists line items (cart, order confirmation, confirmation email, admin order detail, member order detail).
- Full ecommerce foundation: catalogue (products - physical/digital/service, categories, tags, collections), checkout with a pluggable payment-provider interface (Stripe, PayPal, bank transfer, cash - all four fully built), orders with per-item refunds and a manual-order-entry route, customers (derived from orders by email, no dedicated table), discounts (coupon codes + priority-ordered automatic discounts), tax (per-zone rates, inclusive/exclusive mode) and shipping (postcode-prefix zones, flat/weight-banded/free rates), back-in-stock email subscriptions, pre-orders, CSV product import/export, and related-products/upsells (manual curation with an automatic same-category fallback). Optional integration with Members (guest checkout always works; saved addresses, order history, post-purchase account prompt when Members is enabled) and Reply Catcher (shop's side of a Customer Communications tab only - see Extension Points).
- Layout system integration (core mechanism, see Puck Integration above - Shop is the 4th module on it, joining Directory/Gazette/Boards): declares `layoutTypes` group "Shop" with seven types - `shopIndex` ("Shop Home"), `shopCategory` ("Category"), `shopCollection` ("Collection"), `shopProduct` ("Product"), `shopCheckout` ("Checkout"), `shopConfirmation` ("Confirmation"), `shopCart` ("Cart", added later when the cart page joined the layout system) - more types than any other module since Shop has more distinct page kinds than a category/entry pair. 2 new blocks in `components/puck/`: `ShopCategoryHeader`, `ShopCollectionHeader` (both `[ANCHOR]`, same shape as `DirectoryCategoryHeader` - re-fetch their own data from an injected slug, nothing else to inject). Existing blocks retagged by page: `ShopProductGrid`/`ShopProductCard` → `shopIndex`+`shopCategory`+`shopCollection` (one grid block reused across all three listing contexts, exactly like Gazette's `gazetteCategory` reuse); `ShopFeaturedCollection`/`ShopCategoryBrowser`/`ShopPromoBanner` → `shopIndex` only; `ShopProductDetail`/`ShopBackInStockForm`/`ShopRelatedProducts` → `shopProduct`; `ShopCheckoutContact`/`Shipping`/`Payment`/`Review` → `shopCheckout`; `ShopUpsellProducts` → `shopProduct` + `shopCheckout` + `shopCart` (later); `ShopOrderConfirmation` → `shopConfirmation`; `ShopCartFull` (later) → `shopCart`. `ShopCartSummary` stays untagged (header-placement mini-cart widget, not part of any of these page types). `lib/inject-category-context.ts`/`lib/inject-collection-context.ts` inject `{categorySlug}`/`{collectionSlug}`; `lib/inject-product-context.ts` (pre-existing) injects `{productSlug, productId, inStock}` - unchanged, just now called from the generic path instead of the retired bespoke one. `lib/starterLayouts.ts` provides 3 starters per type (21 total) - `shopCategory`/`shopCollection` seed all-draft with the pre-existing hardcoded plain-grid pages as fallback (new templating, same principle as Directory/Gazette/Boards); `shopIndex`/`shopProduct`/`shopCheckout`/`shopConfirmation` have **no** hardcoded fallback (they were Puck-only from day one via the old table) so exactly one starter per type sets `publishByDefault: true`, carrying over the old table's default block arrangement so the storefront looks identical to before on first seed. `shopCart` is the hybrid: it KEEPS its hardcoded cart (`CartPageClient`) as a fallback like category/collection, yet still ships one `publishByDefault` starter (Cart block + upsells) so the basket is designable out of the box but can never go blank if the layout is unpublished. This replaced Shop's own pre-existing bespoke mechanism entirely (see "Retired" note under Database below) rather than running the two side by side.

**Database**
Table prefix: `shp_` (30 tables total, incl. addendum). Full DDL in `modules/shop/migrations/001_initial.sql`; later per-change files are numbered (`002_master_category.sql` adds the product master category to existing installs, idempotently; `003_category_nesting.sql` adds `shp_categories.product_display_mode` and flips the `parent_id` FK to ON DELETE CASCADE for the nested-category feature; `004_variations_hooks.sql` adds `shp_products.catalogue_hidden` BOOLEAN (purchasable but hidden from grid/search/sitemap/own URL - backs the shop-variations child rows) + index, and `shp_order_items.line_meta` JSONB (normalised per-line personalisation, `{fields:[{label,value,href?}]}`) - both mirrored in 001 for fresh installs).

- `shp_products` - name/slug(unique)/type(PHYSICAL\|DIGITAL\|SERVICE)/status(DRAFT\|ACTIVE\|ARCHIVED)/description/short_description/sku(unique)/barcode, pricing (price/compare_at_price/cost_price/tax_class_id FK), inventory (track_inventory/stock_count/low_stock_threshold/out_of_stock_behaviour BLOCK\|BACKORDER, `low_stock_alerted_at` dedupe marker for the daily cron - cleared on any stock_count write so a restock re-arms it), physical dimensions, digital_file_id FK + download_limit/download_expiry, SEO fields + `og_image_id` (no FK, core Media table), `master_category_id` (FK shp_categories ON DELETE SET NULL - the product's lead category; one per product, drives its media folder path; FK added via `ALTER` after shp_categories exists since it's a forward ref, plus idempotent `migrations/002_master_category.sql` for existing installs), pre-order fields (is_pre_order/pre_order_dispatch_date/pre_order_note/pre_order_max_quantity/pre_order_count), recommendation fields (related_mode/upsell_mode AUTOMATIC\|MANUAL, related_limit/upsell_limit default 4), timestamps.
- `shp_product_media` - product_id FK cascade, type(IMAGE\|VIDEO_FILE\|VIDEO_URL), url, alt_text, position, is_primary.
- `shp_categories` - self-referencing parent_id (**ON DELETE CASCADE** since `003` - deleting a category deletes its whole sub-tree, unlike Directory's RESTRICT; product links go via `shp_product_categories`' own CASCADE, the products themselves survive since `master_category_id` is SET NULL), name/slug(unique)/description/position/`product_display_mode` (`'rollup'|'exact'|NULL`=inherit the shop default)/SEO fields. Unlimited nesting depth. `shp_product_categories` join table (no position). A product stays a member of any number of categories here; the single lead one is `shp_products.master_category_id`. `getPrimaryCategoryId()` returns the master when set, else falls back to first membership (used by automatic recommendations). Tree helpers in `lib/db/catalogue.ts`: `getCategoryDescendantIds` (recursive CTE, cycle-safe via UNION - powers roll-up listing), `getCategoryAncestorPath` (breadcrumbs), `categoryReparentWouldCycle` (reparent guard), `reorderCategories(orderedIds, parentId?)` (writes `position` = array index for the group; when `parentId` is passed - `null`=top level - also writes `parent_id`, so one call both re-parents a dragged node and reindexes its destination siblings; omitted = position-only, used by the ↑/↓ arrows), `resolveCategoryProductFilter` (slug+default → exact vs roll-up product filter), `getCategoryProductCount` (one category) / `getCategoryProductCounts` (bulk `GROUP BY` map of direct product counts, powers the admin tree's per-row count badge).
- `shp_tags` - name/slug both unique. `shp_product_tags` join table.
- `shp_collections` - name/slug(unique)/description/image_id/position/SEO fields. `shp_product_collections` join table (has its own `position` - product order within that collection).
- `shp_tax_classes` (name/code unique), `shp_shipping_zones` (name, postcodes JSONB array of prefixes - not `TEXT[]`, matches Directory/Gazette's existing JSONB-array precedent), `shp_tax_zone_rates` (zone+class unique, rate NUMERIC(5,4)), `shp_shipping_rates` (zone_id FK, type FLAT\|WEIGHT_BASED\|FREE, flat_rate/weight_rates JSONB array of `{upToKg,rate}`/free_threshold/estimated_days/position/is_active).
- `shp_digital_files` (filename/url/size/mime_type) + `shp_digital_downloads` (order_id/order_item_id/file_id FKs, unique `token`, download_count, expires_at).
- `shp_coupons` (code unique, type PERCENTAGE\|FIXED_AMOUNT\|FREE_SHIPPING, value/minimum_order_value/usage_limit/usage_count/per_customer_limit/starts_at/expires_at/is_active) + `shp_automatic_discounts` (same shape minus code/usage tracking, plus free_shipping_threshold/priority).
- `shp_orders` - order_number (unique, generated from a dedicated `shp_order_number_seq` Postgres sequence, not a COUNT(*) scheme, so concurrent checkouts can never collide), status (8-value CHECK), member_id (nullable, no FK - Members is optional), customer snapshot (email/name/phone), shipping_address/billing_address JSONB (`ShpAddress` shape), financials (subtotal/discount_amount/shipping_amount/tax_amount/total/tax_mode snapshot/currency), coupon_id FK + coupon_code snapshot, payment_method/payment_status/payment_reference/paid_at, shipping_rate_id (no FK, snapshot only) + shipping_rate_name.
- `shp_order_items` - order_id FK cascade, product_id FK **SET NULL** (product may later be deleted, snapshot fields survive it), product_name/sku/type snapshot, quantity/unit_price/tax_rate/tax_amount/total, refunded_qty, is_pre_order + pre_order_dispatch_date snapshot.
- `shp_refunds` (order_id FK, amount/reason/provider_refund_id/status/created_by) + `shp_refund_items` (refund_id FK cascade, order_item_id FK restrict, quantity/amount).
- `shp_order_notes` (is_internal flag - false = customer-visible) + `shp_order_emails` (send log: subject/to/sent_at/trigger - `trigger` values incl. `MANUAL` for admin-composed sends and `REPLY_CATCHER` reserved for the extension point).
- `shp_saved_addresses` - member_id (no FK, bare string), label, is_default (single-default enforced app-side in a transaction), address JSONB.
- `shp_email_templates` - trigger(unique)/subject/body_html/is_active. Seeded (INSERT...ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING) with all 9 triggers: `ORDER_CONFIRMED` (has the one `{{#if hasPreOrderItems}}` conditional block the renderer supports), `STATUS_PROCESSING`/`STATUS_SHIPPED`/`STATUS_COMPLETED`/`STATUS_CANCELLED`, `ADMIN_NEW_ORDER`, `LOW_STOCK`, `BACK_IN_STOCK`, `IMPORT_COMPLETE`.
- `shp_back_in_stock_subscriptions` - product_id FK cascade, email, member_id nullable, unique(product_id,email) (idempotent subscribe), notified_at (null = pending, retained after fulfilment for reporting).
- `shp_import_jobs` - status(PENDING\|PROCESSING\|COMPLETED\|FAILED), filename, total/processed/created/updated/skipped row counts, errors JSONB array of `{row,reason}`, column_map JSONB, created_by, started_at/completed_at.
- `shp_related_products`/`shp_upsell_products` (product_id+related_id or product_id+upsell_id composite PK, position, both self-FK cascade to shp_products) + `shp_auto_exclude_products` (per-product exclusions from the automatic-recommendation fallback).
- `shp_settings` - singleton (`id='singleton'`), single `config` JSONB column holding the whole `ShpConfig` blob (Q2 decision - no `shopConfig` column added to core `SiteConfig`, everything lives in this one module-owned row instead).
- **Retired**: `shp_page_layouts` (key(unique: `index`\|`product`\|`checkout`\|`confirmation`)/builder_data JSONB) - the original single-layout-per-page mechanism, superseded by the generic `Layout` model (see Layout system integration bullet above and Puck Integration section). Dropped from `001_initial.sql` and from the shared test DB; its default block arrangements were carried forward as each type's `publishByDefault` starter so on-site appearance didn't change.

**Permissions**

`shop.access` (read-only GETs across orders/products/customers - every admin route below marked "or access" accepts this in place of its normal key), `shop.manage` (supersedes every other shop key - settings, email templates, tax/shipping config), `shop.products` (products/categories/tags/collections/CSV import-export CRUD), `shop.orders` (orders/refunds/manual payment confirmation), `shop.customers` (customer list/detail), `shop.discounts` (coupons/automatic discounts), `shop.reports` (tax/revenue reports, no read-only fallback). Enforced via `modules/shop/lib/access.ts`'s `requireShopUser(key, {allowAccess?})`/`hasShopPermission`. Page-layout editing is **not** one of these any more - since it moved onto the core Layout system, it's gated by core `layouts.manage` instead (same as Directory/Gazette/Boards' own layout types), not any `shop.*` key.

**API Routes** (all served through `/api/m/shop/…` via the generated router)

Public (`/api/m/shop/public/…`, unauthenticated unless noted; mutating ones rate-limited via a module-owned in-memory limiter in `lib/rate-limit.ts` - not table-backed like contact-form's, since a rate-limit-only IP column on shp_back_in_stock_subscriptions would be a schema change for a secondary guard; resets on cold start, doesn't share state across serverless instances):
- `GET /products` (filters: category/tag/collection/type/search/pagination, ACTIVE only), `GET /products/[slug]`, `GET /products/[slug]/related`, `GET /products/[slug]/upsells`, `GET /categories`, `GET /categories/[slug]`, `GET /collections`, `GET /collections/[slug]`, `GET /tags`.
- `GET /config` (client-safe config slice: currency, tax mode, enabled payment methods filtered by actual env presence, Stripe publishable key, checkout steps, shop status).
- `POST /cart/validate` (re-checks stock/price/status for client localStorage cart lines).
- `POST /checkout/session` (server-only totals - subtotal/discount/shipping/tax/total, never trusts client maths), `POST /checkout/apply-coupon`, `POST /checkout/payment-intent` (**PROTECTED** - creates the PENDING `shp_orders` row + item snapshot per Q8, then the provider's payment intent), `POST /checkout/confirm` (**PROTECTED** - confirms via the provider, idempotent PAID transition, triggers `fulfillPaidOrder`).
- `GET /orders/status?orderNumber=&email=` (guest lookup, both must match - no enumeration), `GET /downloads/[token]` (**PROTECTED** - token/expiry/download-limit checks, then streams the file bytes through this endpoint rather than redirecting, so the permanent underlying storage URL is never exposed to the client). Three things about the response are deliberate: `Content-Disposition` is built by `lib/download-name.ts`, never interpolated from `shp_digital_files.filename` (the upload route writes that verbatim from the admin's `file.name`, and a quote or a CR/LF in it rewrites the header); `Content-Length` is relayed from the upstream response, never the `size` column, since a row disagreeing with its bytes truncates the transfer or hangs it; and `incrementDownloadCount` runs in the stream's `flush()`, so only a transfer that finished costs a customer one of their limited downloads. Always `attachment` + `nosniff`, as its sibling is: the attachment stops a browser rendering the bytes, and nosniff stops it overriding the stored `Content-Type` and rendering them anyway - worth more here than in the sibling, since this route's upload allowlist is by *declared* MIME type rather than by extension.
- `POST /back-in-stock` (idempotent subscribe), `DELETE /back-in-stock?token=` (**PROTECTED** - HMAC-signed unsubscribe token via `ENCRYPTION_KEY`, no DB lookup needed to validate it).

Member (`/api/m/shop/member/…`, `getMemberFromCookie()` gated): `GET /orders`, `GET /orders/[id]`, `GET/POST /addresses`, `PUT/DELETE /addresses/[id]`, `GET /gdpr-export` (internal-bearer only, `verifyInternalExportBearer` - called self-origin by core's member data-export assembler, feeds the `memberExtensions.dataExportPath` manifest entry).

Webhooks (`/api/m/shop/webhooks/…`, unauthenticated, signature-verified, **PROTECTED**): `POST /stripe` (verifies `STRIPE_WEBHOOK_SECRET`, handles `payment_intent.succeeded`/`payment_intent.payment_failed`/`charge.refunded`), `POST /paypal` (verifies via PayPal's own verify-webhook-signature endpoint using `PAYPAL_WEBHOOK_ID`, handles `PAYMENT.CAPTURE.COMPLETED`/`PAYMENT.CAPTURE.REFUNDED`). Both idempotent - `markOrderPaid`'s `WHERE payment_status != 'PAID'` clause makes a replayed event a no-op.
