Cron (`/api/m/shop/cron/…`, `CRON_SECRET` bearer): `GET/POST /low-stock-alerts` - daily 07:00, also covers Q11 import-job retention (30 days) and Q8 abandoned-PENDING-order pruning (24h).

Admin (`/api/m/shop/admin/…`, session + permission gated per route above): full CRUD for `products` (+ `[id]/related`, `[id]/upsells`, `export`/`import-template`/`import`(+`[id]` status poll)), `categories` (GET returns `{categories, productCounts}` - the latter a per-category direct-product-count map for the admin tree; POST/PUT accept `parentId` + `productDisplayMode`; PUT cycle-guards a reparent; DELETE cascades the sub-tree; `+ reorder` persists a sibling order), `tags`, `collections`, `tax-classes`, `tax-zone-rates`, `shipping-zones`(+ nested rates GET), `shipping-rates`, `coupons`, `automatic-discounts`; `orders` (list+manual-create, `[id]` detail, `[id]/status` (**PROTECTED** - decrements stock for pre-order items on SHIPPED per addendum B.4), `[id]/notes`, `[id]/email`, `[id]/refund` (**PROTECTED** - per-item, validates against refundedQty, calls the provider), `[id]/confirm-payment`); `customers` (list, `[id]` keyed by URL-encoded email - no dedicated table); `reports/tax`(+`?format=csv`)/`reports/revenue`; `dashboard-widget`; `email-templates`; `back-in-stock`; `settings` (shopConfig read/merge-update). Layout editing for all six page types goes through the core `/api/admin/layouts*` routes now (see Layout system integration bullet above) - there is no shop-specific layout-editing route any more (`admin/page-layouts/[key]` retired along with the table it served).

**Payment providers** (`modules/shop/lib/payments/`, **PROTECTED - entire directory**)
- `provider.ts` - the `ShpPaymentProvider` interface (`createIntent`/`confirmPayment`/`refundOrder`/optional `handleWebhook`) every provider implements.
- `stripe.ts` - `stripe` npm SDK (new core dependency, see below), no `apiVersion` pinned (uses the account's dashboard default rather than guessing a literal date string the installed major might reject), server always re-fetches the PaymentIntent and validates its own status **and** amount/currency against the order before trusting a client "confirmed" claim.
- `paypal.ts` - raw REST, no SDK (spec's own instruction, keeps the bundle lean), OAuth token cached in-memory with expiry, sandbox/live base URL switches on `PAYPAL_MODE`, capture amount/currency checked against the order on confirm.
- `bank-transfer.ts`/`cash.ts` - instructions-from-config intents, `confirmPayment` always fails (admin confirms manually via the order detail page's "Confirm payment" action), refunds are manual-only.
- `registry.ts` - `paymentProviders: Record<ShpPaymentMethod, ShpPaymentProvider>` lookup used by every route above.

**Sanctioned core diffs** (all outside `modules/shop/`, each minimal/isolated, flagged PROTECTED in-code):
- `package.json`/`package-lock.json` - added `stripe` (^22.x) as a core runtime dependency. Modules can't add their own npm dependencies (they compile inside core's Next build); precedent: `shiki` for Gazette, `leaflet`/`leaflet.markercluster` for Directory.
- `proxy.ts`'s `buildCsp()` - added `https://js.stripe.com` to `script-src`, `https://api.stripe.com` to `connect-src`, and a new `frame-src 'self' https://js.stripe.com https://hooks.stripe.com` directive (didn't exist before - Stripe Elements renders card fields and 3D Secure challenges in hidden iframes).
- Product image filing (`lib/media/product-media.ts`, `reorganiseProductMedia(productId, {folderProductId?})`): runs on every product `PUT` after the media/category writes. Files each `IMAGE` in `shp_product_media` into the core media library under **Shop / <master category> / <product name> / <product-slug><n>** (`<n>` = 1-based position; no master → "Uncategorised"), via core's `getOrCreateFolderByPath(['Shop', <category>, <product name>])` + `moveOrRenameMedia(id, {targetFolderId, newName, exactName:true, collision:'replace'})`. Only urls resolving to a managed core `Media` row are moved (external urls / video embeds left as-is); the row's `url` is rewritten to the relocated one. Idempotent (an already-filed image is a no-op) and best-effort per image (one relocate failure doesn't fail the save). The editor refetches after save so thumbnails follow the moved blobs. `exactName` keeps the stored key nanoid-free so the url reads `…/shop/<category>/<product>/<slug><n>.<ext>` exactly - this filing is the **only** consumer of `exactName`, so it owns the uniqueness contract `lib/media/keys.ts` now keeps (a shared 40-char clip used to break it; see the Media section). `folderProductId` files a product's images under a **different** product's folder while still naming them from its own slug - the one consumer is shop-variations' variant `PATCH`, which passes the parent so variant images land beside the parent's (a variant child is a hidden, category-less product, so unaided it would file under "Uncategorised"). Two products sharing a name share a folder; filenames stay unique because the slug is.
- `lib/media/upload.ts` - purely additive `NonImageUploadMode` type + `validateNonImageUpload(mimeType, sizeBytes, mode)` export for the digital-file upload path (declares its own mime/size allowlist, skips the sharp image-decode sniff entirely since there's no universal "valid PDF/zip" magic-byte check the way there is for images). The existing image-only `validateUpload`/`uploadMedia`/`deleteMedia`/`downloadMedia`/`saveMediaRecord` are untouched. Shop's digital files are **not** wired into the core `Media` table at all (no `saveMediaRecord` call) - they're stored in shop's own `shp_digital_files` table via `uploadMedia()`'s returned key/url only, since they're not part of core's page/logo Media referencing system.
- `.env.example` - added the seven Stripe/PayPal env var rows (all optional; a payment method with unset keys is filtered out of `enabledPaymentMethods` server-side, never offered at checkout - `modules/shop/lib/env.ts`'s `isStripeConfigured`/`isPayPalConfigured`).
- `app/api/admin/env/route.ts`'s `ALLOWED_KEYS` - added the same seven Stripe/PayPal vars so they're settable through the core env-var UI/API (Vercel project env vars, admin-only per `isAdmin()`). `lib/notifications/deployment.ts` gained a `PAYMENT_KEYS` set feeding `labelForEnvKeys()` → "Payment provider keys updated" on the existing deployment-needed notification.

**Admin pages** (`/cactus-admin/m/shop/…`)

`products` (list w/ search + back-in-stock subscriber-count column linking to the filtered `back-in-stock` view, Export/Import-template buttons, an "Import CSV" button opening `ImportModal.tsx` - upload → auto-detects header mismatches via `headerMatchesFormat()` and only then shows a column-mapping step → polls job progress, recent-imports log), `products/[id]` (**tabbed editor, rebuilt v0.1.38** - see "Product editor" below), `categories` (indented tree: search box, collapsible branches, **drag-and-drop** to reorder among siblings or re-nest under any category plus ↑/↓ arrows and an inline edit panel that renames/reparents/sets the per-category display mode), `collections` (flat list + inline rename/delete, no drag-reorder UI yet), `orders` (status-tab filters incl. a `PRE_ORDER` tab), `orders/[id]` (items table, a "Refund items" button opening `RefundModal.tsx` (per-item quantity inputs pre-filled against remaining refundable qty, reason field, provider-aware copy for manual methods, one batched call to `POST .../refund`), financial summary, shipping address, "Confirm payment" for bank-transfer/cash, notes, email log, digital download tokens, and a Customer Communications section that renders only when another module - e.g. Reply Catcher - actually contributes to the `shop.order-messages` extension point), `customers`, `customers/[id]`, `discounts` (Coupons/Automatic tabs via the shared core `TabStrip`, real forms - not `prompt()` - covering type incl. fixed-amount/free-shipping, expiry window, usage/per-customer limits, minimum order value, free-shipping threshold, priority; edit + delete on both coupons and automatic discounts), `reports` (Revenue/Tax tabs via the shared core `TabStrip`), `back-in-stock` (no nav entry - reached from the products list), `tax-shipping` (`TaxShippingScreen.tsx` - tax classes CRUD (new tax class's `code` auto-slugs from `name`, read-only until unlocked via a pencil button), zones (name + postcode-prefix list, empty list = catch-all matched when no other zone's prefix matches, so one zone can cover a whole country without listing postcodes) picker+detail, per-zone tax rate per class, per-zone shipping rates (flat/weight-banded/free) picker+detail). `ShopSettingsTab` renders on core `/cactus-admin/config`, internal `TabStrip` sub-tabs (General/Checkout/Payments/Notifications/Email templates) covering the full `ShpConfig` shape: store identity+units/SEO/shop status, tax mode+checkout rules (guest checkout, min/max order value, phone requirement, per-step checkout-steps editor, back-in-stock account prompt, pre-order mixed-cart behaviour), payment methods w/ env-presence indicators, order/low-stock alert emails, and the email-templates editor.

**Product editor** (`components/admin/ProductEditor.tsx` + `components/admin/product-editor/`, rebuilt v0.1.38)

Tabbed shell with a sticky sidebar, replacing the single 700px column of stacked sections. Sidebar (collapses above the tabs under 1100px) carries status, a "View on the shop" link, cover thumbnail, at-a-glance price/stock/SKU, and **the only Save button on the page**. Own tabs: Details, Images, Pricing, Stock & delivery, Organisation, Recommendations, Search, plus Download (only when `type === 'DIGITAL'`). Files: `model.ts` (form shape, `toEditorState`/`toProductBody`, per-tab dirty compare, validation), `fields.tsx` (Field/Control/Select/Switch primitives; every field has a real `<label>`, hint and inline error wired through `aria-describedby`), `editor-css.ts` (prefix `spe-`, tokens only, injected once - real CSS so focus rings/hover/responsive work), `panels/*.tsx`, `context.tsx`.

- **Fields the old editor never exposed, all already accepted by the `PUT` and stored**: `barcode`, `weight`+`weightUnit`, `dimensionL/W/H`+`dimensionUnit` (these feed weight-priced shipping rates), and `regenerateSlug` (a "rebuild the web address from the name on save" switch; the API takes the flag, not a free-text slug). `catalogueHidden` is deliberately **not** exposed - it is the internal marker for variant child products, not a "hide from catalogue" toggle, and the page refuses to open a `catalogueHidden` product at all.
- **Numeric fields are held as strings** and converted once in `toProductBody`, so a half-typed `12.` or a cleared box stays what was typed. Validation is computed from the first keystroke but only shown after a save is attempted (`showErrors`); a failed save jumps to the offending tab via `tabForField`.
- **Position is the only cover.** `toProductBody` re-stamps `isPrimary: i === 0` from the array order. `setProductMedia` honours a supplied `isPrimary` over order and `card-template.tsx` reads `media.find(m => m.isPrimary) ?? media[0]`, so round-tripping the loaded flag unchanged would have meant drag-to-reorder moved the image but not the cover.
- **Save races.** The form stays interactive during a save. The post-save reload (needed because images may be re-filed server-side) only takes the server's copy wholesale when nothing was touched since the save started (`prev === current`); otherwise the admin's edits stand and the new baseline just marks them unsaved again. Silently binning what someone typed is the worst kind of bug.
- **`shop.product-editor-sections` is now a tab contract.** Manifest entries gained optional `label` (tab name; falls back to a prettified id) and `order` (sorted among the editor's own via `SHOP_TAB_ORDER`, default 999 = last). The page renders each contributed **server** component and passes it as a `ReactNode` into the client shell, which renders it inside `ProductEditorTabScope`. All panels stay mounted (`hidden` on the inactive ones) so a half-finished edit survives a trip to another tab and contributed tabs can report state while unopened.
- **`product-editor/context.tsx` is the public API for contributed tabs** (`shop-variations` and `product-attributes-for-shop` are the live consumers): `useProductEditorSave({dirty, save})` registers a tab's unsaved edits with the single Save button (throw an `Error` from `save` to fail it; the message is shown, prefixed with the tab name, and one failing tab does not roll the others back); `useProductEditorTabBadge(text)` puts a count on the tab label; `useProductEditorCurrency()` hands over the already-loaded currency symbol so a tab need not re-fetch shop config. All three are inert outside the editor. Registration keys off `useId()` + the scope's tab id, so a tab never names itself. Dirty tabs get an amber dot and a chip in the sidebar; errored tabs get a red one. Navigation away while dirty is guarded by core's `useUnsavedChanges` + `UnsavedChangesModal`.
- Tab selection mirrors to `?tab=<id>` via `replaceState` (deep-linkable; `tab` is read once on the server and passed as `initialTab`, so no `useSearchParams` Suspense boundary). The active tab is **derived**, not stored, so a `?tab=` naming an uninstalled module, or a tab that vanishes when a product stops being digital, falls back to the first tab instead of stranding the view.
- **Panels must be allowed to shrink (v0.1.39).** `.spe-panel>*,.spe-grid>*{min-width:0}` in `editor-css.ts` is load-bearing for any tab holding something wide. Grid children default to `min-width:auto` (their content-based minimum), and a scroll container still propagates its contents' min-content size up through block flow, so without the floor a wide panel overflows the `minmax(0,1fr)` main column and the sticky sidebar paints over it - `shop-variations`' nowrap variants table hit exactly this. A contributed tab wanting a wide surface should wrap it in its own `overflow-x:auto`, which only works because of this rule. Note `minmax(0,1fr)` on `.spe-grid-2/3/4` floors the track, not the item, hence the separate `.spe-field{min-width:0}`.

**Public pages** (`/shop/…`, via `publicBasePath: "shop"`)

`/shop` (index, resolves the `shopIndex` layout via `resolveThemeLayout`, honours `shopStatus` CLOSED), `/shop/products/[slug]` (resolves `shopProduct`, 404s if none published; `productSlug`/`productId`/`inStock` injected into `ShopProductDetail`/`ShopRelatedProducts`/`ShopUpsellProducts`/`ShopBackInStockForm` block props via `lib/inject-product-context.ts` - mirrors core's `resolveTemplateData` context-injection pattern for MenuBlock etc, since these blocks have no per-instance slug of their own in the stored template), `/shop/categories/[slug]` (resolves `shopCategory`, falls back to the original hardcoded plain grid when none published), `/shop/collections/[slug]` (resolves `shopCollection`, same fallback pattern), `/shop/cart` (resolves the `shopCart` layout via `resolveThemeLayout` and renders it with `getModuleLayoutPuckRscConfig('shopCart')`; the `<h1>Your cart</h1>` stays in the page shell; falls back to the original hardcoded client-side cart UI + coupon field + `ShopUpsellProducts` when no `shopCart` layout is published, so never blank), `/shop/checkout` (resolves `shopCheckout`), `/shop/checkout/confirmation` (resolves `shopConfirmation`), `/shop/orders/[orderNumber]` (guest lookup form), `/shop/downloads/[token]` (friendly expired/limit-reached states, real download via the API route), `/shop/account/orders`(+`[id]`)/`/shop/account/addresses` (member-session-gated, 404 when Members disabled, redirect to `{memberAreaPath}/login?redirect=` when signed out).

**Extension Points**
- `core.admin-dashboard-widgets` (id `shop-summary`) - 30-day revenue/orders/AOV, low-stock chip, pending-manual-payment chip, active-pre-order chip.
- `members.account-section` (id `shop-orders`, **first module to use this point** - it existed in core unused until now) - "Orders & addresses" card linking to the member-area pages above.
- `core.menu-entity-provider` (id `shop`, `lib/menu-entity-provider.ts` exporting `shopMenuEntityProvider`) - lets the admin menu builder's "Module content" picker link to shop pages. Four kinds: Shop home (`/shop`), Product (`/shop/products/{slug}`, `publiclyVisible` only when status `ACTIVE`), Category (`/shop/categories/{slug}`), Collection (`/shop/collections/{slug}`). Same shape as Gazette/Directory/Boards providers; URL scheme mirrors `lib/sitemap.ts`.
- `shop.order-messages` (shop is the **consumer** here, not a publisher - no manifest entry needed) - the order detail page looks up any active module's `extensionPoints` for this point name and renders its contributed component with `orderId`/`orderNumber`/`customerEmail` props, mirroring the exact mechanism `members.admin-member-detail` already uses. Reply Catcher does not currently publish to this point (Q12 - shop builds only its own side; the reply-catcher-side contribution is out of scope), so the section never renders out of the box today.
- `shop.product-detail-parts` (**published by shop, v0.1.35**; contract + resolver in `lib/detail-slot.ts`, precedent `lib/line-meta.ts`; live consumer `shop-variations`) - a **claim-and-replace** point, unlike the additive ones above. `resolveShopDetailSlot(product)` is awaited once per product page inside `ShopProductDetail.rsc.tsx` (in the existing `Promise.all`, one extra query) and asks each active provider's `claimsProduct(product)`; the first to claim supplies optional `Gallery`/`Price`/`PurchaseArea` components, which ride to the parts as `DetailPartContext.slot` via the existing `_ctx` injector (`inject-part-context.ts`, attached by reference so components survive). `ShopDetailGalleryRsc`/`ShopDetailPriceRsc`/`ShopDetailAddToCartRsc` render the slot component instead of their own markup when `slot` is set, and shop's own markup unchanged when it is null (shop-only site, or any unclaimed product) - the starter layout's block list is **not** touched, which is how a variations-aware default PDP stays free of variations-specific blocks. Shop hands the provider its own `.spd-*` class names plus its server-loaded images/price so a replaced part looks native and paints on first byte. Replace (not render-alongside) because a claimed product has no single price/stock of its own - both rendering would show two prices and two buttons. **A claimed product's `PurchaseArea` owns availability outright: shop's `outOfStock` gate is deliberately skipped**, since stock lives on the chosen combination and gating on the parent row would strand a parent that tracks no stock of its own (`ShopDetailBadges` still reads the parent's `outOfStock`, so a mis-configured parent can show an out-of-stock badge above a working buy button). Nothing in shop names variations; the point is generic and the `git grep` leak check stays clean.

- `shop.product-detail-tabs` (**published by shop, v0.1.50**; contract + resolver in `lib/detail-tabs.ts`; live consumer `product-downloads-for-shop`) - **additive**: a module contributes a tab to the product page's own tab strip, beside Description/Specification/Dimensions, rather than a block bolted underneath. Modelled on `shop.gallery-media` line for line, and additive for the same reason - a tab replaces nothing, so every provider resolves and one whose `load` throws is dropped and logged rather than taking the product page down. `resolveShopDetailTabs(productId)` is awaited once per page in `ShopProductDetail.rsc.tsx` (in the existing `Promise.all`) and rides to the parts as `DetailPartContext.detailTabs`, **not** awaited inside `ShopDetailTabsRsc` - the parts render synchronously, and `detail-parts.tsx` is dual-compiled into the client editor bundle, so it cannot import the extension-point registry (which reaches prisma) at all. Provider supplies `label`, optional `order`, `load(productId)` (server-only; payload crosses the RSC boundary so must be JSON-serialisable; **null means no tab**, which is what keeps the strip unchanged on products with nothing to add) and a `Panel` **client** component. `label`/`order` live on the provider object rather than in the manifest - unlike `shop.product-editor-sections`, whose manifest `label` is stripped by the install-time zod schema and only restored by `sync-module-manifests.mjs` on the next deploy, leaving a tab named after its own id in the meantime. Shop's own tabs are numbered in `detail-parts.tsx` (`TAB_ORDER`: desc 10, spec 20, dims 30, downloads 40); an unordered contribution lands at 50 and ties keep shop's own first (stable sort). Shop never learns what a tab holds.
- `shop.gallery-media` (**published by shop, v0.1.43**; contract + resolver in `lib/gallery-media.ts`; live consumer `product-3d-views-for-shop`) - **additive**, the counterpart to the claim-and-replace point above: a module contributes extra items to a product's gallery (a 3D model) that appear as further thumbnails and take over the stage when picked. It exists *because* `shop.product-detail-parts` is winner-takes-all - shop-variations already claims Gallery on every product with options, so a second claimant could never reach exactly the products that need it most. Being additive, nothing replaces a part of shop's, so there is no two-prices failure to design around and **every** provider is resolved, not just the first; one whose `load` throws is dropped and logged rather than taking the product page down. `resolveShopGalleryExtras(productId)` is awaited once per page in `ShopProductDetail.rsc.tsx` (in the existing `Promise.all`) and rides to the parts as `DetailPartContext.galleryExtras` - resolved by the injector, **not** awaited inside the part, because `wrapResponsiveRender` (`lib/puck/config.tsx`) calls a block's `render` as a plain function. Provider supplies `load(productId)` (server-only; the returned payload crosses the RSC boundary so must be JSON-serialisable) plus `Thumbs`/`Stage` **client** components - a function cannot cross that boundary, which is why filtering by the chosen variation is the provider's own job rather than a callback shop calls into. Shop hands over its `.spd-thumb` class names and owns the strip, the stage box and which item is picked; it never learns what the item is. Rendered by **all three** galleries - shop's `ProductGallery`, shop-variations' `VariantSlotGalleryClient` (which passes the chosen child's id as `activeProductId`, the bit shop cannot know) and shop-variations' granular `ShopVariantGallery` block (which covers shop's Gallery slot, so it is the only strip on those layouts and must resolve extras itself).

**Puck Blocks** (all 18, registered in the generated `lib/puck/module-components.ts`)

`ShopProductGrid`, `ShopProductCard`, `ShopFeaturedCollection`, `ShopCategoryBrowser`, `ShopPromoBanner` (colour prop is a semantic token name, never hex), `ShopCartSummary` (client, reads localStorage cart, untagged - header-placement widget, not part of any `layoutTypes` page), `ShopCartFull` (client, full editable cart display - `CartFullClient` localStorage island wrapped by `components/puck/ShopCartFull.tsx`; ~33 look/behaviour options: rows/cards/table layout, spacing/dividers, optional heading, product-image toggle+size+radius, unit/line-price toggles, quantity control style (stepper/number/read-only), remove button text-or-bin, stock + pre-order badges, coupon field labels, item-count/subtotal toggles + labels, checkout button label/colour/text-colour via core `SiteColourField`/full-width/radius, empty-state copy + continue-shopping link, price-accent + panel colours; tagged `shopCart` (its layout type) but ALSO present on every core page via the all-module-blocks "Modules" category, so still droppable anywhere; ONE render path shared by editor and live for parity - editor render passes `preview` to seed sample lines with inert controls and no fetch, RSC render is a server wrapper passing only plain props into the client island, same trick as `ShopCartSummary`; no new API - reuses `/api/m/shop/public/cart/validate`, `/config`, `/checkout/apply-coupon`), `ShopCheckoutContact`/`ShopCheckoutShipping`/`ShopCheckoutPayment`/`ShopCheckoutReview` (all `[ANCHOR]` - `permissions:{delete:false,duplicate:false}` - client components sharing state via a sessionStorage-backed `checkout-state.ts` store since Puck blocks don't share React state; the Payment block owns the mounted Stripe Elements instance and listens for a `cactus-shop-place-order` window CustomEvent the Review block dispatches, since only Payment has access to `stripe.confirmPayment()`), `ShopOrderConfirmation`, `ShopProductDetail` (`[ANCHOR]`, add-to-cart non-removable; RSC render also emits the schema.org Product JSON-LD script tag), `ShopBackInStockForm` (auto-hidden via an `inStock` prop the product page injects), `ShopRelatedProducts`, `ShopUpsellProducts` (client, resolves upsells for every product currently in the cart client-side by calling the per-product upsells route once per cart line and merging/deduping), `ShopCategoryHeader`/`ShopCollectionHeader` (both `[ANCHOR]`, added with the layout system integration above - breadcrumb + name + description, re-fetched server-side from an injected `categorySlug`/`collectionSlug`).

**Configuration**

`ShpConfig` (`modules/shop/lib/config.ts`, Zod-validated, stored as the single `config` JSONB column on the `shp_settings` singleton, Q2): `currency`/`currencySymbol`/`storeEmail`/`orderNumberPrefix`/`weightUnit`/`dimensionUnit`, `taxMode` (INCLUSIVE\|EXCLUSIVE), `guestCheckoutEnabled`/`postPurchaseAccountPrompt`/`minimumOrderValue`/`maximumOrderValue`/`requirePhone`/`checkoutSteps` (ordered step array), `enabledPaymentMethods` (filtered by env presence at read time via `getAvailablePaymentMethods()`), `bankTransferInstructions`/`cashInstructions`, `adminOrderAlertEmail`/`lowStockAlertEnabled`/`lowStockAlertEmail`, `shopStatus` (OPEN\|BROWSE_ONLY\|CLOSED)/`shopClosedMessage`, `shopTitle`/`shopMetaDescription` (`shopBasePath` dropped per Q3 - fixed to `"shop"` via the manifest's `publicBasePath` instead of being runtime-configurable), `backInStockAccountPrompt`, `preOrderMixedCartBehaviour` (HOLD_ALL\|PROMPT_SPLIT), `imageZoomOnHover` (default false - magnifies the point of the Product Detail gallery's main image the shopper hovers/taps; read once per page onto `DetailPartContext.zoomImages` and passed to `ProductGallery`, and through the `zoom` prop on `ShopDetailGallerySlotProps` so a `shop.product-detail-parts` provider that replaces the gallery can honour it too).

**Product photos are square everywhere; the `shape` prop is gone (shop v0.1.44, shop-variations v0.1.11)**
One ratio, 1:1, for every product photo: the Product Detail stage (`.spd-stage`) and the card image (`.shop-card-img` in `card-parts.tsx`, `.spc-img` in `product-card-css.ts`, both previously `4/3`). The per-instance `shape` select (square/portrait/landscape) is **removed** from both the `ShopDetailGallery` and `ShopCardImage` Puck blocks, from `GalleryProps`/`ImageProps`/`ProductGallery`, from `ShopDetailGallerySlotProps` (so `shop-variations`' `VariantSlotGalleryClient` stopped reading it and no longer sets `aspectRatio` inline - it inherits the ratio from shop's `.spd-stage` via `classNames`, one definition rather than two modules agreeing to keep saying `1/1`), and from every `starterLayouts.ts` block (two set `landscape`). The `.shape-*` CSS classes are gone. Its only real effect was letting one shop's photos be three shapes depending on the layout a page used. Saved `Layout` rows may still carry `props.shape`; Puck passes unknown props through and nothing reads it, so they resolve square with no data migration - correct on this fresh-install platform. **Exempt: Overlay cards** (`.shop-card-img.fill-mode`, `aspect-ratio:auto` inside a `3/4` card) - the photo being the whole card is that design, not a shape. Non-square originals crop rather than distort (`object-fit:cover` in an `overflow:hidden` box). `shop-variations` declares `requiresModules: shop >= 0.1.44`, since its gallery now leans on shop's square `.spd-stage`.

**Product Detail gallery, viewport fit (v0.1.42, reworked v0.1.44)**
The gallery column (`.spd-stage-col`, CSS in `galleryCss()`, `modules/shop/components/puck/parts/detail-parts.tsx`) is `position:sticky` so the photo stays with a shopper scrolling a taller buy column, and the stage fits the leftover viewport **by giving up width** - `aspect-ratio` takes the height with it, so it stays square and merely gets smaller. `--spd-fit` (`calc(100dvh - var(--spd-header-h) - 32px - var(--spd-thumbs-h))`) is that width budget; the stage is `flex:none;align-self:center;width:min(100%,var(--spd-fit));min-width:140px`. **v0.1.42 capped the column's height instead and let the stage flex-shrink into it, which squashed the square stage into a letterbox and cropped the photo** - the bug the square rule exists to prevent. `beside` mode overrides `--spd-fit` (the strip sits alongside, costing the stage no height) and uses `flex:1 1 auto;max-width:var(--spd-fit)`, since the strip is spending some of the row's width too.

Both numbers need measurements CSS cannot get. The site header's height: core does **not** publish it - the header is the Site Header Puck block (`lib/puck/config.tsx`), whose height is a per-site prop that may be `auto`, whose stickiness is a second prop, and which a site may omit. So `modules/shop/components/public/GalleryViewportFit.tsx` (client island, renders null) measures it and publishes `--spd-header-h` on `:root`, counting only `<header>` elements computing to `position:sticky|fixed` with `top <= 4px` (a static header scrolls away and costs the column nothing) and summing `height + top` (a header parked below an announcement bar). It also publishes `--spd-thumbs-h` - the stacked strip's height plus the column's `gap:12px`, `0` when there's no strip (no strip, no gap). Re-measures on `ResizeObserver` (headers + strip) and `resize`: late-decoding logo, wrapping nav, condense-on-scroll header, strip rewrapping rows. Fallbacks `96px`/`76px` cover pre-hydration and the editor canvas.

**The strip's width is deliberately NOT tied to `--spd-fit`.** Its height feeds that sum, so sizing it from the result would let a narrower strip wrap to more rows → taller strip → smaller budget → narrower strip: a loop the ResizeObserver would chase. It keeps its full column width (`flex:none`); only the stage moves. Rendered by `ShopDetailGalleryRsc`, **not** by `ProductGallery`, so a `shop.product-detail-parts` provider's replacement gallery gets it too - it wears `.spd-stage-col`. No `overflow` on the column: it would clip `.spd-thumb.on`'s `box-shadow: 0 0 0 1px` ring on the edge thumbnails of every page, to catch only a ~35-image outlier. Below `tabletBp` the column goes `position:static` and the stage back to `width:100%` - stacked, it has the width to itself and shouldn't shrink for a viewport it no longer shares.

**Thumbnail strip overflow affordance (`GalleryThumbStrip`, v0.1.48)**

The strip below the stage is one nowrap `overflow-x:auto` row (above), which on a product with a dozen photos simply looked like it ended at the column's edge - nothing said the row ran on. `modules/shop/components/public/GalleryThumbStrip.tsx` (client) wraps it in `.spd-thumbs-wrap` and renders, at whichever end still has scroll left in it, a `.spd-thumbs-fade` gradient and a `.spd-thumbs-arrow` button - the same affordance, geometry (2rem fade inboard of a 1.5rem arrow) and 160px step as core's admin `components/admin/TabStrip.tsx`. State is `scrollLeft` vs `scrollWidth - clientWidth` on a `scroll` + `resize` + `ResizeObserver` check; both ends start "at" so the server's markup carries no arrows and the effect earns them. Keyed on `Children.count`, **not `children`**: the gallery re-renders on every pointer move while the magnifier is tracking, and keying on the nodes would tear the listeners down and rebuild them on each one.

`beside` strips pass straight through unwrapped - left/right means nothing to a column - so that layout's markup and CSS are exactly as before. `ShopDetailGallery` (editor preview) mirrors the same wrapper for markup/class parity; its four placeholders never overflow, so no arrows are earned there.

**The new rules are scoped to `.spd-thumbs-wrap`, not to `.spd-thumbs`, and that is load-bearing.** A `shop.product-detail-parts` provider's replacement gallery (shop-variations' `VariantSlotGalleryClient` / `ShopVariantGallery`) wears the `.spd-thumbs` class it is handed via `classNames` but renders it straight into `.spd-stage-col` with no wrapper. `flex:1 1 auto` reaching it there would read as grow-to-fill on the **vertical** axis (the column's main axis) and stretch its strip down the page; hiding the scrollbar would leave it with no overflow hint at all, having no arrows to replace it with. Hence `.spd-thumbs-wrap .spd-thumbs{flex:1 1 auto;scrollbar-width:none}` and an untouched `.spd-stage-col:not(.beside) .spd-thumbs`. **Those galleries therefore still have no arrows** - giving them the treatment means shop-variations adopting `GalleryThumbStrip` in its own repo, which is a separate change there.

The hidden scrollbar slightly *raises* the photo's budget: its height was being charged to `--spd-thumbs-h`.

**Admin dialogs**
The shop admin no longer calls the browser's `confirm()`/`prompt()`/`alert()`. `modules/shop/components/admin/dialogs.tsx` exports three promise-based hooks - `useConfirm()`, `usePrompt()`, `useAlert()` - each returning `[invoke, node]`: call `await invoke(...)` and render `{node}` once in the screen. Styling matches the module's other overlays (colour tokens only, `role="dialog"`/`aria-modal`, Escape cancels, Enter confirms, delete confirms use the `btn-danger` class). Wired through CategoriesScreen, CollectionsScreen, ProductsScreen (new-item name prompts), DiscountsScreen (delete confirms + save-error alerts), TaxShippingScreen (delete confirms), ProductEditor (upload/save-error alerts).

**Money formatting**
All prices render through one helper - `modules/shop/lib/money.ts` `formatMoney(amount, symbol='£')` - which coerces the string/number a price arrives as and always emits `symbol` + 2dp (e.g. `£7.99`). Storefront pages/blocks and order emails pass `config.currencySymbol`; admin screens (client-rendered, no server config) read it via `components/admin/use-currency-symbol.ts` `useCurrencySymbol()` (fetches `/api/m/shop/public/config` once, module-cached, `£` fallback). Prices are decimal pounds end to end (`NUMERIC(10,2)`); nothing is stored or displayed in pence (the Stripe `×100` in `lib/payments/stripe.ts` is API-only). Discount "value" cells format per type: `%` for PERCENTAGE, `formatMoney` for FIXED_AMOUNT, `—` for FREE_SHIPPING.

**External Integrations**
Stripe (Payment Intents + Elements + webhooks, `stripe` npm SDK), PayPal (Orders v2 REST API directly, no SDK), core Members system (optional, guest checkout always works regardless), core Media/upload pipeline (`uploadMedia()` reused for digital files, but not `saveMediaRecord` - see core diffs above), core email (`sendEmail` via `lib/email/index.ts`, shop owns its own `shp_email_templates` table rather than reusing core's `EmailTemplate`).

**Cron Jobs**
`0 7 * * *` → `/api/m/shop/cron/low-stock-alerts` - low-stock digest email (deduped via `low_stock_alerted_at`, re-arms on any stock_count write) + `shp_import_jobs` retention (30 days) + abandoned-PENDING-order pruning (24h, Q8). `CRON_SECRET` bearer-gated.

**Scripts**
None.

**Known Limitations** (v0.1.2 - flagged here rather than silently shipped as if finished)

- Categories have an indented nested-tree admin UI with ↑/↓ sibling reorder, reparent, and per-category display-mode override; collections still have no reorder UI (the `position` column and API support it; only rename/delete are wired up in the collections screen). Neither uses drag-to-reorder (↑/↓ buttons only, like Directory).
- Reply Catcher's contribution to the `shop.order-messages` extension point is out of scope of this build (Q12) - the Communications tab section is real and will render the moment another module publishes to that point, but nothing does yet.
- The module-side rate limiter (`lib/rate-limit.ts`) is in-memory, not table-backed - resets on a cold start and doesn't share state across concurrent serverless instances. Acceptable for a secondary guard behind normal validation, but weaker than contact-form's DB-backed one.

v0.1.1 fixed five review findings from the original v0.1.0 build: Stripe/PayPal `confirmPayment` now validates charged amount/currency against the order (not just status/reference); `GET /downloads/[token]` streams the file through the endpoint instead of redirecting to the permanent storage URL; the `product`/`checkout` default page layouts now seed `ShopBackInStockForm`/`ShopUpsellProducts` (new installs only, per `ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING`); the product editor gained a real Recommendations panel, image picker, and digital-file upload; the Discounts screen, refund flow, CSV import, and page-layouts editor were all rebuilt from `prompt()`/raw-JSON placeholders into proper UI (see the Admin pages entry above for each).

### Shop Variations

- Slug: `shop-variations` (table prefix `svr_`), repo `github.com/cactus-foundation-modules/shop-variations`, manifest version 0.1.13 (registry pin v0.1.13). `requiresModules: shop >= 0.1.43` (`shop.gallery-media`; `product-editor/context` needed only 0.1.38 and `shop.product-detail-parts` only 0.1.35), `requiresCoreVersion 0.5.426`. Reuses shop's `shop.products`/`shop.reports` permissions (declares none of its own) and joins the existing **Shop** admin nav group with one entry ("Product options").
- Adds product options to the shop: fixed **variant matrices** (e.g. Size × Colour, each combination its own price/SKU/barcode/stock/weight/image) and free-form **personalisation add-ons** (text, long text, number, priced dropdown, checkbox, date, file upload). A variant is a real but `catalogue_hidden` child `shp_products` row created through shop's own `createProduct`, so basket, checkout, inventory, orders and refunds work unchanged; the storefront selector resolves the chosen combination to that child id and calls shop's `addToCart(childId, qty, {meta})`. Personalisation rides in the generic `line_meta` carrier, priced server-side by the registered resolver.

**Database**
Table prefix: `svr_` (7 tables). Full DDL in `modules/shop-variations/migrations/001_initial.sql` (idempotent). Cross-module FKs to `shp_products` are safe because shop installs first.

- `svr_options` - `id`, `product_id` FK→shp_products (cascade, the parent), `name`, `control_type` (DROPDOWN\|SWATCH\|PILL), `position`.
- `svr_option_values` - `id`, `option_id` FK (cascade), `label`, `swatch?` (hex or media id), `position`.
- `svr_variants` - `id`, `product_id` FK (parent, cascade), `child_product_id` FK→shp_products (cascade, unique - the hidden child), `enabled`, `position`.
- `svr_variant_values` - composite PK (`variant_id` FK cascade, `option_value_id` FK cascade) - which values define a variant.
- `svr_addons` - `id`, `product_id` FK (cascade), `type` (TEXT\|TEXTAREA\|NUMBER\|SELECT\|CHECKBOX\|DATE\|FILE), `label`, `required`, `position`, `config` JSONB (max length, min/max, flat/per-char price, priced choices, file limits).
- `svr_uploads` - `id`, `token` (unique), `media_ref` (public url, used as the line_meta href), `media_provider?`/`media_key?` (for orphan blob cleanup), `filename?`, `size`, `mime_type`, `order_item_id?` (unused link, retained), `ip_hash?`, `created_at`. Not FK'd to order items - orphan cleanup cross-checks `media_ref` against `shp_order_items.line_meta`.
- `svr_settings` - singleton (`id='singleton'`): `max_upload_mb` (10), `allowed_upload_types`, `upload_retention_days` (30), `max_variants` (200).

**Permissions**: none of its own - admin writes gate on `shop.products` (via shop's `requireShopUser`), the report on `shop.reports`.

**API Routes** (through `/api/m/shop-variations/…`)

- Admin (`shop.products`): `GET admin/products` (variation-enabled product list), `GET admin/products/[id]` (deep-editor payload), `POST admin/products/[id]/options`, `POST admin/products/[id]/generate-matrix`, `POST admin/products/[id]/clear-variants`, `POST admin/products/[id]/addons`, `PATCH/DELETE admin/options/[id]`, `POST admin/options/[id]/values`, `PATCH/DELETE admin/option-values/[id]`, `PATCH admin/variants/[id]` (edits the child product via shop's `updateProduct`/`setProductMedia` + `enabled`; on an image set, calls shop's `reorganiseProductMedia(childProductId, {folderProductId: parentId})` so the variant image files into the parent product's media folder), `PATCH/DELETE admin/addons/[id]`, `GET admin/export` (CSV), `POST admin/import` (CSV). `GET admin/reports` gates on `shop.reports`.
- Public: `GET public/by-slug/[slug]/variations` (storefront selector payload - options, per-variant price/stock/image, base images, add-ons; looked up by slug so no product-context injection is needed in shop), `POST public/upload` (anonymous, rate-limited, size/type-validated personalisation file upload → core media provider + `svr_uploads` row, returns a token).
- Member: `GET member/gdpr-export` (internal bearer; the member's personalisation from their orders' `line_meta`).
- Cron: `GET/POST cron/cleanup-uploads` (`Bearer $CRON_SECRET`, daily 03:00) - prunes orphaned uploads past the retention window, deleting the blob then the row.

Admin pages (`/cactus-admin/m/shop-variations/…`): `products` (cross-product list; its "Manage" links to `/m/shop/products/[id]?tab=variations-inline`), `reports` (parent-grouped variant sales), `import` (CSV import/export). A shared `VariationsTabs` sub-nav keeps the module to one Shop-group nav entry. **There is no standalone per-product editor** (`products/[productId]` was deleted in v0.1.6): the whole thing is now the **Variations tab** on shop's product editor, contributed via `shop.product-editor-sections` → `ProductVariationsSection` (server wrapper; returns `null` for a `catalogue_hidden` variant child, since a variant of a variant is not a thing) → `VariationsPanel` (client: options builder with inline rename, matrix generate/rebuild/clear, bulk variant grid, personalisation fields). Two save models on purpose: structural work (add option, generate matrix, add addon) applies immediately because it is an action, while per-variant grid edits are held locally and written by the product editor's single Save via `useProductEditorSave` (dirty rows tint, and only the rows actually written are cleared, so a row edited mid-save survives). Tab badge = variant count. A `Rebuild from options` warning appears when the option combinations no longer match the variant count.

**Extension point published: `shop-variations.variant-columns` (v0.1.12)** - another module hangs an extra column on the variants grid, one cell per variant, resolved in `ProductVariationsSection` (manifest read + permission filter + registry lookup, none of which can happen in the browser) and passed to `VariationsPanel` as `columns: VariantColumn[]`. Live consumer: `product-3d-views-for-shop`'s **3D** column, which sits beside Image and takes a dropped model file.

- It exists because the alternative broke module isolation: setting a variation's picture and its 3D model are the same errand, but the grid belongs to this module and the model to one this module has never heard of and does not depend on. So the grid learned about *columns*, not about 3D - there is **no 3D code in shop-variations**, and without that module installed there is no such column.
- Contract: a cell gets `productId`, `variantId`, `childProductId` (the knowledge only this module has - a variation IS a hidden child product) and `label`, and owns its own storage, fetching and saving.
- **A contributed cell must be a client component.** `VariationsPanel` is a client island that fetches its own variants, so cells render per row in the browser and only client references survive the crossing - same rule as `shop.gallery-media`'s `Thumbs`/`Stage`.
- Contributed cells **save themselves** and are deliberately not wired into the editor's Save button: this point exists for uploads, and holding a 40 MB file as a pending in-memory edit would be a lie that costs the admin their upload.
- `label`/`order` ride along on the manifest entry (the `shop.product-editor-sections` trick), each with a fallback for manifests written before they existed.

**Puck Blocks** (editor + RSC parity, colour tokens only): composite `ShopVariantPurchase` (layout `shopProduct` - gallery + options + personalisation + live price + variant-aware add-to-cart) and five granular parts on `shopProductDetail` mirroring shop's `ShopDetail*`: `ShopVariantOptions`, `ShopVariantPersonalisation`, `ShopVariantPrice`, `ShopVariantAddToCart`, `ShopVariantGallery`. Each is a server wrapper → a client island; editor render is a labelled skeleton (preview), RSC render is live. Parts share one selection per product keyed by slug (`lib/use-variation-selection.ts`), so they sync when placed independently. Indicative storefront pricing and the authoritative server pricing use the same pure `computeAddonPricing` (`lib/addon-pricing.ts`), so they can't disagree.

**The page opens with nothing chosen (v0.1.13).** `firstPreselect` is gone from `lib/selection-logic.ts` and neither entry path (`seededEntry`, `ensureLoaded`) seeds a selection: the opening `optionValues` is `{}`, so the price shows the parent's `basePrice`, `resolveVariant` returns null and `canAdd` is false until the shopper picks. Preselecting the first buyable variant meant a combination nobody had chosen sat in the controls looking chosen, and the buy button was live over it. Two consequences worth knowing:
- **"Out of stock" must gate on `allOptionsChosen`, not just `!inStock`** (`VariantPricePart`). `inStock` is `hasOptions ? !!(variant && enabled && inStock) : true`, and with nothing chosen there is no variant - so the unguarded check labelled *every* options product sold out on load. The purchase parts were already safe: their `reason` chain tests `!allOptionsChosen` first and says "Choose your options".
- **`ResetOptionsLink`** (exported from `VariantParts.tsx`) renders after the last option in **both** hosts - the granular `VariantOptionsPart` and the slot path's `VariantSlotPurchaseClient` - and calls `resetOptions()` → `resetOptionValues(slug)`, clearing `optionValues` only. Personalisation (`addonValues`) survives on purpose: it's typing, not a click. It renders only when `anyOptionChosen`, which is also why RSC and hydration agree - a server render never has a selection, so neither emits the link.

- **The RSC halves live in their own files (v0.1.7): `components/puck/variant-parts.rsc.tsx` and `ShopVariantPurchase.rsc.tsx`, pointed at by the manifest's `rscImport`** (same split, same reason, as shop's `ShopProductDetail.rsc.tsx`). They resolve the selector payload server-side via `lib/variation-bootstrap.ts` and pass it to the island as `initial`, so the option controls are in the page's first HTML. Before this the RSC halves were pass-throughs that rendered nothing but the editor's skeleton, and every island waited for hydration → read the slug off `window.location` → `GET public/by-slug/[slug]/variations` + `GET /api/m/shop/public/config`, which is why the options arrived a beat after the rest of the page.
- **`lib/variation-bootstrap.ts` (server-only, pulls prisma - never import from a `'use client'` file).** `getVariationBootstrap(slug)` is React-`cache`d, so all six blocks share one query per request; it returns the payload plus shop's currency symbol (killing the second fetch). Puck's `<Render>` gives a block only its own saved props and shop injects context into its own part types alone (`inject-part-context.ts`), so there is no prop carrying the slug - instead `rememberProductSlug` records it into a `cache()`-scoped, therefore per-request, slot from the detail-parts provider's `claimsProduct`, which shop calls once per product page before any block renders. `currentProductSlug()`/`bootstrapForCurrentProduct()` read it back. A null is survivable, not fatal: the island falls back to the old fetch-after-mount path (the composite block on a bare `shopProduct` layout, say).
- **The selection store must not be written during a server render.** Module state is per-tab in the browser but per-process on the server, outliving the request: an entry seeded into `store` server-side would sit there marked loaded and hand the *next* shopper of that product whatever price and stock that render happened to see, until the instance recycled. So `useVariationSelection` builds a throwaway entry from `initial` when `typeof window === 'undefined'` and touches no module state; the browser seeds the shared store as normal (first seed per slug wins, so a re-render can't discard a live selection). The currency symbol rides on the entry rather than the module-level `let` for the same reason - otherwise a server render prints the `£` default and hydrates into the real symbol.

**Extension points provided**: `shop.product-editor-sections` → `ProductVariationsSection` (component); `shop.cart-line-resolver` → `resolveVariationLineMeta` (server function; maps a variant child back to its parent, loads the parent's add-ons, re-resolves file tokens from `svr_uploads` server-authoritatively, prices via `computeAddonPricing`); and `shop.product-detail-parts` → `shopVariationsDetailParts` (`lib/detail-parts-provider.ts`, an object, id `variations-detail-parts`) - **this is what makes shop's default Product Detail layout handle options with no layout editing**. `claimsProduct` runs server-side once per product page and returns true when the product has options or add-ons and is not itself a `catalogue_hidden` variant child; shop then renders this module's `Gallery`/`Price`/`PurchaseArea` in place of its own `ShopDetailGallery`/`ShopDetailPrice`/`ShopDetailAddToCart`. Those slot components are distinct from the granular Puck blocks below: they render into shop's own `.spd-*` class names (handed down as props) and from shop's server-loaded images/price, so the swap is invisible and paints on first byte. As of v0.1.7 they are split like the Puck blocks: `components/public/DetailSlotParts.tsx` holds **async server** halves that await `getVariationBootstrap(props.slug)` (shop hands the slug down on every slot prop, so no request-scoped lookup is needed here) and pass it to the islands in `DetailSlotPartsClient.tsx` as `initial`. Awaiting is within shop's contract - it types the slots as plain components but only ever renders them from its own RSC halves (`ShopDetail*Rsc`). `OptionControl`/`AddonControl` are shared with `VariantParts.tsx` so the hand-placed blocks and the automatic slot render the identical control. Unclaimed products, and shop-only sites, are untouched.
  - **`coveredSlots(blockTypes)` - not claiming a job the layout already does by hand.** The point assumed shop's part was the only thing doing each job. Layouts written before it existed do the same job with this module's granular blocks (Deskwell's product page carries `ShopVariantPrice` and `ShopVariantOptions` beside shop's `ShopDetailPrice`/`ShopDetailAddToCart`), so taking the slot as well rendered the price and the option picker twice. Shop now passes every block type in the layout (`collectLayoutBlockTypes`, walks `content` **and** `zones` - the default Product Detail keeps its parts in a Split's zones) and this module returns the covered slots: `ShopVariantGallery`→Gallery, `ShopVariantPrice`→Price, `ShopVariantAddToCart`→PurchaseArea. Shop then renders **nothing** for those (`ctx.slot.covered`), rather than falling back to its own part - a static parent price beside a live variant price is two different figures for one product. Only applies to claimed products; an unclaimed one never consults `covered`, so shop's parts render normally.
  - **A replaced part inherits none of shop's behaviour, only its classes (v0.1.9).** Shop's `imageZoomOnHover` setting (shop settings > General) reached `VariantSlotGalleryClient` as the optional `zoom` prop from shop 0.1.40 and was simply ignored, so the shop-wide zoom silently did nothing on exactly the products this module claims - anything with options. The island now implements it: pointer-tracked `transformOrigin` + `transform: scale(2.5)` on the stage image, mouse magnifying on hover, touch on tap-drag-tap, reset when the variant image or thumbnail pick changes. Shop's behaviour is **reimplemented, not imported** - its copy lives inside `ProductGallery`, which knows nothing of variant images, and the `zoomable`/`zoomed` modifier classes behind it are shop CSS the `classNames` contract does not hand over; the two declarations they carry (cursor, and `touch-action` while magnified) go on inline instead, keeping the fix inside this module. The scale constant is duplicated deliberately and must stay level with shop's, or one setting means two things depending on the product. Generalises: any future prop shop adds to a slot is inert until a provider reads it, and nothing fails loudly when it doesn't.
  - Options and personalisation have no shop part to replace, so they can't be handled that way: they ride inside `VariantSlotPurchase`, which drops them itself when `layoutBlockTypes` (on every slot prop) shows `ShopVariantOptions`/`ShopVariantPersonalisation` already placed. Shop only ever passes block-type strings it attaches no meaning to; this module is the only side that knows what they mean. Resolution is split - `resolveShopDetailProvider(product)` (the claim, still parallel with the template fetch) then the pure `narrowShopDetailSlot(provider, blockTypes)` once the template's blocks are known.

**Cron Jobs**: `0 3 * * *` → `cron/cleanup-uploads`.

**Known Limitations**: a layout that *hand-places* a granular `ShopVariant*` block next to shop's equivalent (`ShopVariantPrice` beside `ShopDetailPrice`, etc.) now double-renders on a claimed product, because shop's own part is variant-aware via the slot as of shop 0.1.35 - the two can't see each other (the slot is per-product, the blocks are per-layout, and shop knowing about `ShopVariant*` types is exactly the coupling the point exists to avoid). Stock layouts are unaffected (they contain shop's parts only); the fix for a hand-built one is to drop the now-redundant `ShopVariant*` block. Also: variant images use a URL field (no media picker yet); `svr_settings` has no admin UI (defaults only) in v1; CSV import requires the parent product to exist by slug (creates options + child variants, not parents); deleting a parent product leaves its hidden children orphaned (retention cleanup covers uploads; child-product cleanup on parent delete / uninstall is a documented follow-up); a hidden child 404s on its own URL rather than redirecting to its parent.

### Product Attributes for Shop

- Slug: `product-attributes-for-shop` (table prefix `pat_`), repo `github.com/cactus-foundation-modules/product-attributes-for-shop`, manifest version 0.1.1, pinned in `modules.json` to v0.1.1. `requiresModules: shop >= 0.1.26`, `requiresCoreVersion 0.5.426`. Reuses shop's `shop.products` permission (declares none of its own) and joins the existing **Shop** admin nav group with one entry ("Product attributes").
- Adds shop-wide **filterable attributes** (Material, Colour, Room) with values, assignable to products *and* to individual variants, plus a storefront Puck block that filters the catalogue by them. shop-variations is an **optional** companion, not a `requiresModules` entry: every `svr_` read goes through `lib/variations-bridge.ts` as raw SQL guarded by a `to_regclass` probe (30s cache, `resetVariationsProbeCache()` test seam), because `@/modules/shop-variations/...` does not resolve on an install without it and a static import would break that build.

**Database**
Table prefix: `pat_` (4 tables). Full DDL in `modules/product-attributes-for-shop/migrations/001_initial.sql` (idempotent). Cross-module FKs to `shp_products` are safe because shop installs first.

- `pat_attributes` - `id`, `name`, `slug` (unique; the storefront filter's query key), `control_type` (CHECKBOX\|SWATCH\|DROPDOWN), `position`, `show_in_filters`, `source_option_name?` (the shop-variations option name it was imported from, so a re-import updates rather than duplicates), `created_at`.
- `pat_attribute_values` - `id`, `attribute_id` FK (cascade), `label`, `slug` (unique per attribute), `swatch?` (hex only), `position`.
- `pat_product_values` - composite PK (`product_id` FK→shp_products cascade, `value_id` FK cascade). `product_id` covers **both** parent products and shop-variations' hidden variant children - that is what makes per-variant attributes work with no second table.
- `pat_settings` - singleton (`id='singleton'`): `hide_empty_values` (true), `include_variant_values` (true).

**Permissions**: none of its own - all reads/writes gate on `shop.products` via shop's `requireShopUser` (GETs pass `allowAccess: true`).

**API Routes** (through `/api/m/product-attributes-for-shop/…`, all admin, all `shop.products`)

- `GET/POST admin/attributes`, `PATCH/DELETE admin/attributes/[id]` (rename re-slugs; case-insensitive duplicate name → 409), `POST admin/attributes/[id]/values`, `PATCH/DELETE admin/values/[id]`.
- `GET/PUT admin/products/[id]/assignments` - one round trip returning the vocabulary + this product's assignments + its variants. PUT validates every `byVariant` key against `listVariantsForProduct(id)` before writing, so a crafted id cannot rewrite another product's assignments.
- `POST admin/products/[id]/import-variations` - turns the product's `svr_options`/`svr_option_values` into attributes (matched by option **name**, so two products' "Colour" feed one shop-wide filter) and attaches values to the variant children carrying them. Idempotent: clears prior imported assignments for the touched attributes first. 409 when shop-variations is absent or the product has no options.

Admin pages (`/cactus-admin/m/product-attributes-for-shop/…`): `attributes` (define the vocabulary + values). The per-product `ProductAttributesSection` is the **Attributes tab** on shop's product editor via `shop.product-editor-sections` (server wrapper → `ProductAttributesEditor` client island: own-product ticks, collapsible per-variant grid, "Copy from variations"). It has **no save button of its own** (v0.1.2): it registers with the product editor's single Save through `useProductEditorSave`, diffing its ticks against a baseline captured at load. Tab badge = count of ticked values.

**Puck Blocks**: `ShopAttributeFilterGrid` ("Shop: Filtered Product Grid", layouts `shopIndex`/`shopCategory`/`shopCollection`, editor + RSC split via `rscImport`, colour tokens only). RSC renders every matching product up front with shop's **own** Product Card template (`resolveCardTemplate` + `buildCardContext` + `injectShopProductCardEmbed`), tagging each `.shop-card` anchor `data-pat-product`/`data-pat-values`; the `AttributeFilterShell` client island then shows/hides them in place. It deliberately mirrors shop's `renderCards` rather than calling it - the only difference is the data tag, which shop's helper has nowhere to hang. Facet semantics: OR within an attribute, AND across attributes - the rule itself is the pure `matchesSelection()` in `lib/filter-logic.ts` (7 tests in `lib/filter-logic.test.ts`), which the shell calls rather than keeping its own copy. Selection mirrors into the URL via `replaceState` (read post-mount only, so hydration cannot mismatch the server-rendered cards). Filter CSS in `components/public/filter-css.ts` (prefix `pat-`, tokens only, site breakpoints baked in like shop's grids).

**Variant rollup**: `getEffectiveValueIdsByProduct()` unions a parent's own values with those of its **enabled** variants (disabled ones excluded - not buyable, so a filter hit would be a dead end); `countProductsByValue()` counts the same way, powering the per-option counts and `hide_empty_values`.

**Known Limitations**: filtering only covers what the block rendered, and `listProducts` clamps `perPage` to 100 - so 100 products is the honest ceiling per grid (a larger catalogue wants a paginated, server-filtered grid). `pat_settings` has no admin UI (defaults only) in v1. No `settingsTabs` entry. Renaming an attribute re-slugs it, breaking any bookmarked filter URL. Imported swatches take hex only (shop-variations also allows a media id there).

### Product Downloads for Shop

- Slug: `product-downloads-for-shop` (table prefix `pdl_`), repo `github.com/cactus-foundation-modules/product-downloads-for-shop`, manifest version 0.1.1 (registry pin v0.1.1, landed in core v0.5.482 alongside the shop v0.1.50 pin that carries the tab point it hangs on).
- `requiresCoreVersion` **0.5.472**, `requiresModules` **shop >= 0.1.50** (the release adding `shop.product-detail-tabs`). Manifest v0.1.0 named 0.1.47 - the shop of the day it was written against, which shipped without the point; corrected in module v0.1.1, since a min version naming a release that lacks the feature installs cleanly and then silently renders no tab at all.
- Free downloadable literature on a product - manuals, spec sheets, care cards, drawings - each named in plain English, shown on the product page under a **Downloads** tab that anyone can take them from. Distinct from shop's `shp_digital_files`, which is the product being *sold* and is delivered post-purchase behind a token with an expiry and a download count.

**Database**
Table prefix: `pdl_`

- `pdl_files` - `id` (text PK, gen_random_uuid), `product_id` FK → `shp_products` (cascade), `name` (what the shopper reads and saves it as), `filename` (as uploaded), `url`, `media_provider?`, `media_key?`, `media_id?` (the core `Media` row, nullable), `mime_type`, `size` (int), `position` (int), `created_at`. Index: product_id.

**Extension points consumed**: `shop.product-editor-sections` (id `product-downloads-inline`, label "Downloads", order 50, permission `shop.products`) and `shop.product-detail-tabs` (id `product-downloads`, label "Downloads", order 45).

**Routes**: `GET|POST|PATCH /api/m/product-downloads-for-shop/admin/products/[id]/files` (list / upload / save order - PATCH scopes the renumber to the product in the WHERE clause, so a posted foreign id renumbers nothing), `PATCH|DELETE /api/m/product-downloads-for-shop/admin/files/[id]` (rename / drop our row + the `Media` row + the blob), `GET /api/m/product-downloads-for-shop/public/files/[id]` (the download).

**Upload path - through the server, and it has to be (4 MB)**: the direct-to-Worker path photographs and 3D models use is **closed to a document**. The Worker types an upload from its object key's extension (`contentTypeForKey`) and 415s anything that is not a raster image or a 3D model, so a signed PDF key is refused no matter what. The bytes therefore go multipart through the serverless function, where Vercel's ~4.5 MB body cap applies, so the module advertises `MAX_UPLOAD_BYTES` (4 MB) and preflights on the client rather than promising more and dying on the doorstep - the exact failure `product-3d-views-for-shop` v0.1.2 was released to fix, and the reason shop's own `digital-files` route claiming `maxSizeBytes: 200 MB` is a lie the platform overrules. Lifting it needs a core release teaching the Worker about document types **plus** every install redeploying its Worker.

**Why downloads are proxied rather than linked (`app/api/public/files/[id]`)**: core's `extensionForMimeType` derives a key's extension from the MIME **subtype**, so a `.docx` is stored under a key ending `.vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.wordprocessingml.document`, with a nanoid prefix. Link the shopper at storage and they save a file their machine cannot open; the `<a download>` attribute would rename it but is ignored cross-origin, and storage is always another origin. So the route sets `Content-Disposition` itself from `lib/download-name.ts` (owner's name + the *original* file's extension, so "Instructions.exe" cannot rename a PDF, and a typed ".pdf" does not double). Also: reads by `provider`+`key` via core's `downloadMedia` rather than fetching the stored url, so a site that later moves its Worker keeps working (shop's digital files store only a url and every link dies at that point); `Content-Length` from the bytes in hand, never the `size` column; always `attachment` + `nosniff`.

**Status gating**: the public route loads the owning product and 404s unless `status === 'ACTIVE' && !catalogueHidden` - the same line `app/public/shop/products/[slug]/page.tsx` draws. Without it an id would hand out an unlaunched product's manual or a withdrawn one's spec sheet; the uuid makes it unguessable, not access-controlled.

**Type policy** (`lib/file-kinds.ts`, single source for server and browser): pdf, zip, doc(x), xls(x), ppt(x), rtf, txt, csv, dwg, dxf, jpg/jpeg, png. **No html/svg/xml/js, deliberately** - the module serves stored bytes from the site's own origin, and a type the browser renders markup from is stored XSS rather than a download. The extension decides, not the declared MIME (a .zip arrives as `application/zip` or `application/x-zip-compressed`; a .dwg as nothing).

**Known limitations**: 4 MB per file (above). No per-variation downloads - files attach to the product only. On a DIGITAL product that also carries free literature, shop's own "Downloads" tab and this module's sit side by side, both labelled "Downloads"; rare (it means an ebook with a manual) and cosmetic, but a per-product label would need the point's contract to grow.

### Product 3D Views for Shop

- Slug: `product-3d-views-for-shop` (table prefix `p3d_`), repo `github.com/cactus-foundation-modules/product-3d-views-for-shop`, manifest version 0.1.2 (registry pin v0.1.2).
- `requiresCoreVersion` **0.5.468** (the release adding `MODEL_EXTENSION_TYPES` and the Worker's 3D write path), `requiresModules` **shop >= 0.1.43** (the release adding `shop.gallery-media`).
- A 3D model on a product or one of its variations, shown as an extra auto-rotating gallery thumbnail badged "3D"; picking it replaces the gallery's main image with an orbit/pan/zoom viewer.

**Database**
Table prefix: `p3d_`

- `p3d_models` - `id` (text PK, gen_random_uuid), `product_id` FK → `shp_products` (cascade), `url`, `media_provider?`, `media_key?`, `media_id?` (the core `Media` row, nullable - a model whose library row is deleted still renders), `filename`, `format` (check: glb | gltf | obj | fbx | 3ds), `size` (int), `position` (int), `created_at`. Index: product_id.

**Why product_id covers variations too**: a shop-variations variation IS a hidden child `shp_products` row (`svr_variants.child_product_id`), so a model on a variation is a model on that child's id. The module therefore holds **no** notion of options or variants and depends on shop alone.

**shop-variations is optional, not required**. `lib/db/models.ts` reads the `svr_` tables through raw SQL and never imports `@/modules/shop-variations/...` - that path does not exist on an install without it, and a static import would break the build there. Presence is probed with `to_regclass` (30s TTL cache), not the `Module` table, since a module row can exist before its migration has run. Same bargain and the same reasoning as `product-attributes-for-shop/lib/variations-bridge.ts`. Read-only: this module adds no column to shop-variations' schema, and its Variations-tab column is contributed through a generic point rather than built into shop-variations (below).

**Extension points consumed**: `shop.product-editor-sections` (id `product-3d-views-inline`, label "3D views", order 60, permission `shop.products`), `shop.gallery-media` (id `product-3d-views`), and `shop-variations.variant-columns` (id `product-3d-views-variant`, label "3D", order 10, permission `shop.products` - v0.1.2).

**The 3D column on the Variations tab (v0.1.2)**: `components/admin/Product3dVariantColumn.tsx`, a **client** component (only client references cross to shop-variations' client panel). Drop a model on a variant row, or click the `＋`; uploads immediately rather than via the editor's Save button, same reasoning as the 3D tab. The cells share one fetch through `lib/use-product-models.ts` (module-scoped store + `useSyncExternalStore`, keyed by the PARENT id): the route already returns the whole tree, so fifty variants must not mean fifty identical requests. The 3D tab's "Attach to" dropdown stays - it is the only way to reach the whole product rather than a variation.

**Routes**: `GET|POST /api/m/product-3d-views-for-shop/admin/products/[id]/models` (list + record/upload), `POST /api/m/product-3d-views-for-shop/admin/products/[id]/models/upload-url` (**v0.1.2**, signs a direct-to-Worker target), `DELETE /api/m/product-3d-views-for-shop/admin/models/[id]` (drops our row, the `Media` row and the blob - a 50 MB model left in the bucket is a bill). On all of them `id` is the PARENT; the target travels as `targetProductId` and is checked against the parent's tree via `isValidTarget` - without it an admin could hang a model off any product.

**Upload path - direct to the Worker (v0.1.2, was broken before it)**: the browser PUTs the model straight to the media Worker and never sends the bytes through a serverless function. It **had** to change: the old form upload advertised 50 MB while Vercel 413s any body over ~4.5 MB *before* the handler runs, and that 413's body is not JSON - so `res.json()` threw and the editor's `?? 'Upload failed'` fallback was the only thing the admin ever saw. Every model worth selling died there. Two halves, mirroring core's `/api/admin/media/upload-url` + `/record`, but module-owned because only this module knows the folder and the ownership rule: `upload-url` gates on `shop.products`, resolves the folder, `buildKey`s and `signUploadToken`s; the JSON POST to `models` verifies that same token, reads the format from the **key** (the only claim the signature covers), and writes the `Media` + `p3d_models` rows. The folder is re-resolved server-side rather than carried back through the browser - the path is already baked into the signed key. `lib/upload-model-client.ts` owns the client half for both surfaces.

- **Fallbacks are honest, not silent.** `{ available: false }` (non-S3 provider, or no Worker URL) falls back to the multipart path and says up front that a model over `MAX_UPLOAD_MB` cannot get in on this install, naming R2/B2/S3 as the fix. A **415 from the Worker** means a Worker deployed before it learned about 3D keys: the client says "Settings → Media, deploy the Worker again" rather than showing a bare refusal. The Worker only picks up new source on redeploy, so **every existing install must redeploy before 3D uploads work**.
- The multipart POST on `models` survives as that fallback; `Product3dEditor` and the variant column both go through the client helper and never touch it directly.

**Format policy** (`lib/formats.ts`, the single source for server and browser): glb, gltf, obj, fbx, 3ds. **DWG and USDZ are rejected at upload**: DWG is proprietary AutoCAD with no JS loader (needs a paid Autodesk/ODA conversion service) and USDZ renders only via Apple AR Quick Look, so neither can drive an inline viewer - accepting them would store a file nothing on the page could draw. The **extension decides**, not the declared MIME: browsers report .glb as `application/octet-stream`, .fbx as an empty string. Safe because nothing server-side parses these files. Cap is `MAX_DIRECT_UPLOAD_BYTES` (50 MB) - taken from core rather than declared here, since the Worker is the real ceiling and promising more than it accepts is how the 50 MB became a lie in the first place.

**Why models are no longer `application/octet-stream`** (`mimeForFormat`, v0.1.2): core builds an object key's extension from the MIME type, so every model used to land under a `.octet-stream` key - and the Worker reads an upload's type back out of the key's extension, that being the only claim a client cannot forge. A key naming no type is a key the Worker refuses. The type here is not a description of the bytes so much as the thing that carries the extension. Core owns the map (`MODEL_EXTENSION_TYPES`); a format core has not heard of **throws** rather than falling back to a near-enough type.

**Visibility rule**: the pure `visibleItems()` in `lib/visible-items.ts` (10 tests in `lib/visible-items.test.ts`). A model on the product itself always shows; variation models are narrowed to the chosen variation, and before a choice is made all of them show *unless* the product has its own (which then stands in). Deduplicated **by url**, so a size run pointing every variation at one file is one thumbnail, not one per variation.

**One WebGL context for all thumbnails** (`lib/three/thumb-stage.ts`): a renderer per thumbnail hits the browser's ~8-16 live-context cap, past which the oldest are silently killed - blank thumbnails on someone else's machine. Instead one off-document `WebGLRenderer` is resized per thumbnail, rendered, and `drawImage`'d into that thumbnail's plain 2D canvas; one rAF loop drives the lot, skips off-screen thumbnails, and honours `prefers-reduced-motion`. The full viewer (`Viewer3d.tsx`) gets its own context - only one is ever on screen - with OrbitControls, bounded zoom, and auto-rotate that stops for good on first touch. `three` is **dynamically imported** throughout, so a product page with no model never carries it.

**Known Limitations**: OBJ carries no materials (the `.mtl` sibling is never uploaded) so it renders plain white; a `.gltf` referencing external `.bin`/textures loads geometry only - GLB is the format to recommend and the editor says so. No settings tab. No reorder UI (models append). A model is not shown on product cards or in the cart, only on the product page.

### Twilio

Module `twilio` (repo `cactus-foundation-modules/twilio`), tablePrefix `tw_`, v0.1.9 (requiresCoreVersion 0.5.303 - needs the `admins.account-section` extension point). Twilio account integration: call forwarding for the account's incoming numbers, per-number voicemail with opening hours, per-number call/message logs with recording playback, two-leg click-to-dial, and SMS delivery of login codes (via the core `smsProviders` hook, see Scripts above). No Puck blocks, no public pages, no cron.

- Env vars (manifest `requiredEnvVars`, all `required: false` so install isn't blocked before configuration): `TWILIO_ACCOUNT_SID`, `TWILIO_AUTH_TOKEN`, `TWILIO_AUTH_TOKEN_IE1`, `TWILIO_AUTH_TOKEN_AU1`. Managed through the module's core settings tab via `/api/admin/env` (module-declared keys are allowlisted generically). `TWILIO_PHONE_NUMBER` removed in v0.1.4 - the from-number is now picked from the account's numbers and stored in `tw_site_numbers` (default SMS number), not typed as an env var. `TWILIO_REGION` existed only in v0.1.7 and is gone - see below.
- **Per-number regions / v0.1.8.** Twilio Regions (`us1`/`ie1`/`au1`) are isolated instances for data residency. Three facts shape the implementation, each learned the hard way in v0.1.7:
  1. **Numbers are a single global pool** bought through `us1`, and each number's *inbound processing Region* is set **per number** via the Routes API - there is no account-wide region. `us1` is always the control plane (`HOME_REGION`): `listIncomingNumbers`, `setNumberVoiceUrl` and the Routes API itself always go there.
  2. **A token is only valid in the Region it was created in** ("Any given Auth token or API key is only valid for the Twilio Region in which it was created"), so each Region needs its own token. Account SID is shared. `REGION_TOKEN_ENV` maps `us1`→`TWILIO_AUTH_TOKEN`, `ie1`→`TWILIO_AUTH_TOKEN_IE1`, `au1`→`TWILIO_AUTH_TOKEN_AU1`; `MissingRegionTokenError` (exported, message shown to admins verbatim) names the missing var.
  3. **FQDNs are `{product}.{edge}.{region}.twilio.com`** - the bare `{product}.{region}` form (`api.ie1.twilio.com`) was switched off 28 April 2026 and omitting the edge silently routes back to `us1`. `REGION_EDGE` = `ie1`→`dublin`, `au1`→`sydney`; `regionHost(product, region)` builds it, with `us1` staying the plain `api.twilio.com`/`routes.twilio.com`.
  Records follow the routing (a call to an `ie1`-routed number is processed and stored in `ie1` only, and querying `us1` returns an empty list rather than an error), so **every log/recording/outbound path resolves the number's Region first**: `listCallsForNumber`/`listMessagesForNumber`/`fetchRecordingAudio`/`placeCall`/`sendSms` all take a `TwilioRegion`. `lib/twilio.ts` exports `TWILIO_REGIONS`, `TWILIO_REGION_LABELS`, `HOME_REGION`, `isTwilioRegion`, `isRegionConfigured`, `getConfiguredRegions`, `regionTokenEnvVar`, `getNumberRegion`, `setNumberRegion`. Routing uses **Routes API v3** (`GET`/`POST https://routes.twilio.com/v3/PhoneNumbers/{e164}`, form params `voiceRegion`/`messagingRegion`, response `voice_region`/`messaging_region`) which is `us1`-only and covers both voice and messaging - so reading/writing routing needs **no** regional token, only the main one. This module keeps voice and messaging together (one Region per number); `getNumberRegion` reads `voice_region` and treats unset/unknown as `us1`. Twilio takes up to 5 minutes to apply a routing change. `validateTwilioSignature` now tries **every configured Region's token** (no early exit) because a webhook is signed with the token of the Region that processed the call - a number routed to `ie1` arrives signed with the `ie1` token.
- Permission: `twilio.manage` (settings tab, nav entry, admin API routes).
- Manifest surfaces: `settingsTabs` → `TwilioSettingsTab` (credentials + per-region tokens + connection status + phone-numbers picker: lists the account's incoming numbers with a Texts/No-texts capability badge, add/remove to site, per-number Country select, radio choosing the default send-texts-from number - SMS-capable numbers only); `navEntries` → `/m/twilio` admin page; `smsProviders` → `lib/sms-provider.ts` `twilioSmsProvider` (`isConfigured` = credentials set AND an SMS-capable default site number selected, `sendSms` = `sendSiteSms`); `extensionPoints` → `members.account-section` `TwilioMemberSmsSection` (member SMS 2FA enrolment card) + `admins.account-section` `TwilioAdminSmsSection` (same card for the signed-in admin on the admin account page, no permission - self-service).
- Tables: `tw_forwarding_rules` (`phone_sid` unique, `phone_number`, `forward_to`, `enabled`, `greeting_message`, `greeting_voice`, `record_calls`, `show_called_number` - added by module migration `002_show_called_number.sql`; plus the voicemail columns added by `004_voicemail.sql` and also in `001_initial.sql` for fresh installs: `voicemail_enabled` BOOLEAN DEFAULT false, `ring_timeout` INTEGER DEFAULT 20 (seconds the forwarded leg rings first, form-bounded 5-120), `voicemail_greeting` TEXT, `voicemail_voice` TEXT, `closed_voicemail_greeting` TEXT DEFAULT `''` (added by module migration `006_closed_voicemail_greeting.sql` and also in `001_initial.sql` for fresh installs - said instead of `voicemail_greeting` when the call arrives outside opening hours;
